## üõ°Ô∏è **HATA Y√ñNETƒ∞Mƒ∞ (T√ºm Kodlara Ekle)**

```python name=utils/error_handler.py
import traceback
import logging
from functools import wraps
from typing import Callable, Any

# Logger kur
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format='%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    handlers=[
        logging.FileHandler('esoteric_platform.log', encoding='utf-8'),
        logging.StreamHandler()
    ]
)

logger = logging.getLogger('EsotericPlatform')

def handle_errors(default_return=None):
    """Hata yakalama decorator"""
    def decorator(func: Callable) -> Callable:
        @wraps(func)
        def wrapper(*args, **kwargs) -> Any:
            try:
                return func(*args, **kwargs)
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Error in {func.__name__}: {str(e)}")
                logger.debug(traceback.format_exc())
                return default_return if default_return is not None else {
                    'error': True,
                    'message': str(e),
                    'function': func.__name__
                }
        return wrapper
    return decorator

# √ñrnek kullanƒ±m:
# @handle_errors(default_return={})
# def risky_function():
#     ...
```

## üöÄ **MAIN.PY (TAM ENTEGRASYON)**

```python name=main.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

"""
üîÆ Ezoterik ƒ∞limler Platformu - Kuran Merkezli
Tam entegre, √ßalƒ±≈üƒ±r halde
"""

import sys
import json
from pathlib import Path
from PyQt6.QtWidgets import QApplication, QMessageBox
from PyQt6.QtCore import Qt

# Import error handler first
try:
    from utils.error_handler import handle_errors, logger
except ImportError:
    # Fallback basit logger
    import logging
    logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    def handle_errors(default_return=None):
        def decorator(func):
            return func
        return decorator

# Core imports
try:
    from core.ebced_calculator import EbcedCalculator
    from core.cifr_engine import CifrEngine
    from core.vefk_generator import VefkGenerator
    from core.kabbalah_engine import KabbalahEngine
    from core.islamic_numerology import IslamicNumerology
    from core.remil_engine import RemilEngine
    from core.simya_engine import SimyaEngine
    from core.quran_numerics_engine import QuranNumericsEngine
    from core.theosophy_engine import TheosophyEngine
    from core.astrology_engine import AstrologyEngine
    from core.tarot_engine import TarotEngine
    from core.iching_engine import IChingEngine
    from core.hermetic_engine import HermeticEngine
    from core.data_scraper import DataScraper
except ImportError as e:
    logger.error(f"Core module import error: {e}")
    sys.exit(1)

# UI imports
try:
    from ui.main_window import EsotericMainWindow
except ImportError as e:
    logger.error(f"UI module import error: {e}")
    sys.exit(1)

class EsotericPlatform:
    """Ana platform sƒ±nƒ±fƒ±"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.config = self.load_config()
        self.engines = self.initialize_engines()
        self.app = None
        self.window = None
    
    @handle_errors(default_return={})
    def load_config(self) -> dict:
        """Konfig√ºrasyon y√ºkle"""
        config_file = Path("config.json")
        
        if config_file.exists():
            with open(config_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                config = json.load(f)
            logger.info("Config loaded successfully")
            return config
        else:
            logger.warning("Config file not found, using defaults")
            return self.create_default_config()
    
    def create_default_config(self) -> dict:
        """Varsayƒ±lan config"""
        default = {
            "api_key": "",
            "model": "gpt-4-turbo-preview",
            "language": "tr",
            "theme": "dark",
            "location": {
                "latitude": 41.0082,
                "longitude": 28.9784,
                "timezone": "Europe/Istanbul"
            }
        }
        
        # Kaydet
        with open("config.json", 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(default, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
        
        return default
    
    @handle_errors(default_return={})
    def initialize_engines(self) -> dict:
        """T√ºm motorlarƒ± ba≈ülat"""
        logger.info("Initializing engines...")
        
        engines = {}
        
        try:
            # Ebced
            engines['ebced'] = EbcedCalculator()
            logger.info("‚úì Ebced engine")
            
            # Cifr
            engines['cifr'] = CifrEngine(engines['ebced'])
            logger.info("‚úì Cifr engine")
            
            # Vefk
            engines['vefk'] = VefkGenerator(engines['ebced'])
            logger.info("‚úì Vefk engine")
            
            # Kabbalah
            engines['kabbalah'] = KabbalahEngine()
            logger.info("‚úì Kabbalah engine")
            
            # Numerology
            engines['numerology'] = IslamicNumerology(engines['ebced'])
            logger.info("‚úì Numerology engine")
            
            # Remil
            engines['remil'] = RemilEngine()
            logger.info("‚úì Remil engine")
            
            # Simya
            engines['simya'] = SimyaEngine(engines['ebced'], engines['cifr'])
            logger.info("‚úì Simya engine")
            
            # Quran Numerics
            engines['quran_numerics'] = QuranNumericsEngine(None, engines['ebced'])
            logger.info("‚úì Quran Numerics engine")
            
            # Theosophy
            engines['theosophy'] = TheosophyEngine()
            logger.info("‚úì Theosophy engine")
            
            # Astrology
            engines['astrology'] = AstrologyEngine()
            logger.info("‚úì Astrology engine")
            
            # Tarot
            engines['tarot'] = TarotEngine()
            logger.info("‚úì Tarot engine")
            
            # I-Ching
            engines['iching'] = IChingEngine()
            logger.info("‚úì I-Ching engine")
            
            # Hermetic
            engines['hermetic'] = HermeticEngine()
            logger.info("‚úì Hermetic engine")
            
            # Data Scraper
            engines['scraper'] = DataScraper()
            logger.info("‚úì Data Scraper")
            
            logger.info(f"All {len(engines)} engines initialized successfully!")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Engine initialization error: {e}")
            raise
        
        return engines
    
    def run(self):
        """Uygulamayƒ± ba≈ülat"""
        try:
            # QApplication
            self.app = QApplication(sys.argv)
            self.app.setApplicationName("Ezoterik ƒ∞limler Platformu")
            self.app.setOrganizationName("Kuran Merkezli Ara≈ütƒ±rma")
            
            # Ana pencere
            self.window = EsotericMainWindow(self.engines, self.config)
            self.window.show()
            
            logger.info("Application started successfully")
            
            # Event loop
            sys.exit(self.app.exec())
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.critical(f"Application failed to start: {e}")
            QMessageBox.critical(
                None,
                "Kritik Hata",
                f"Uygulama ba≈ülatƒ±lamadƒ±:\n{str(e)}"
            )
            sys.exit(1)

def main():
    """Ana fonksiyon"""
    try:
        platform = EsotericPlatform()
        platform.run()
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        logger.info("Application interrupted by user")
        sys.exit(0)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.critical(f"Fatal error: {e}")
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

## üé® **UI MAIN WINDOW (Basitle≈ütirilmi≈ü Ama Tam)**

```python name=ui/main_window.py
from PyQt6.QtWidgets import (QMainWindow, QWidget, QVBoxLayout, QHBoxLayout,
                             QTextEdit, QPushButton, QSplitter, QLabel)
from PyQt6.QtCore import Qt

class EsotericMainWindow(QMainWindow):
    """Ana pencere - Basit ama √ßalƒ±≈üƒ±r"""
    
    def __init__(self, engines, config):
        super().__init__()
        self.engines = engines
        self.config = config
        
        self.setWindowTitle("üîÆ Ezoterik ƒ∞limler Platformu")
        self.setGeometry(100, 100, 1400, 900)
        
        self.setup_ui()
        self.show_welcome()
    
    def setup_ui(self):
        """UI kur"""
        central = QWidget()
        self.setCentralWidget(central)
        
        main_layout = QHBoxLayout(central)
        
        # Sol: Chat
        left_widget = QWidget()
        left_layout = QVBoxLayout(left_widget)
        
        # Chat area
        self.chat_area = QTextEdit()
        self.chat_area.setReadOnly(True)
        self.chat_area.setStyleSheet("""
            QTextEdit {
                background-color: #1a1a1a;
                color: #e8e8e8;
                border: none;
                padding: 20px;
                font-size: 11pt;
            }
        """)
        
        # Input
        self.input_field = QTextEdit()
        self.input_field.setMaximumHeight(100)
        self.input_field.setPlaceholderText("Sorunuzu yazƒ±n...")
        self.input_field.setStyleSheet("""
            QTextEdit {
                background-color: #262626;
                color: #e8e8e8;
                border: 2px solid #3a3a3a;
                border-radius: 8px;
                padding: 12px;
                font-size: 11pt;
            }
        """)
        
        send_btn = QPushButton("G√∂nder")
        send_btn.setStyleSheet("""
            QPushButton {
                background-color: #3b82f6;
                color: white;
                border: none;
                padding: 12px;
                border-radius: 8px;
                font-size: 11pt;
            }
            QPushButton:hover {
                background-color: #2563eb;
            }
        """)
        send_btn.clicked.connect(self.send_message)
        
        left_layout.addWidget(self.chat_area, 1)
        left_layout.addWidget(self.input_field)
        left_layout.addWidget(send_btn)
        
        # Saƒü: Panel
        right_widget = QWidget()
        right_widget.setFixedWidth(350)
        right_layout = QVBoxLayout(right_widget)
        
        title = QLabel("üîÆ √ñzellikler")
        title.setStyleSheet("font-size: 16pt; font-weight: bold; color: white; padding: 12px;")
        right_layout.addWidget(title)
        
        # √ñzellik butonlarƒ±
        features = [
            ("Ebced", self.run_ebced),
            ("Cifr", self.run_cifr),
            ("Vefk", self.run_vefk),
            ("Kabala", self.run_kabbalah),
            ("Numeroloji", self.run_numerology),
            ("Remil", self.run_remil),
            ("Simya", self.run_simya),
            ("Kuran 19", self.run_quran19),
            ("Teosofi", self.run_theosophy),
            ("Astroloji", self.run_astrology),
            ("Tarot", self.run_tarot),
            ("I-Ching", self.run_iching),
            ("Hermetik", self.run_hermetic)
        ]
        
        for name, func in features:
            btn = QPushButton(f"‚Üí {name}")
            btn.setStyleSheet("""
                QPushButton {
                    background-color: #262626;
                    color: #e8e8e8;
                    border: none;
                    border-radius: 8px;
                    padding: 10px;
                    text-align: left;
                    font-size: 10pt;
                }
                QPushButton:hover {
                    background-color: #3b82f6;
                }
            """)
            btn.clicked.connect(func)
            right_layout.addWidget(btn)
        
        right_layout.addStretch()
        
        # Ana layout
        main_layout.addWidget(left_widget, 1)
        main_layout.addWidget(right_widget)
        
        # Stil
        self.setStyleSheet("QMainWindow { background-color: #0f0f0f; }")
    
    def show_welcome(self):
        """Ho≈ügeldin mesajƒ±"""
        self.chat_area.append("""
<h1 style='color: #3b82f6;'>üïå Kuran Merkezli Ezoterik ƒ∞limler Platformu</h1>
<p style='color: #9ca3af;'>Ho≈ü geldiniz! Saƒü panelden bir √∂zellik se√ßin veya soru sorun.</p>

<h3 style='color: #4ade80;'>‚úÖ Y√ºkl√º Mod√ºller:</h3>
<ul style='color: #e8e8e8;'>
<li>Ebced - Harf deƒüerleri</li>
<li>Cifr - Gizli anlamlar</li>
<li>Vefk - Sihirli kareler</li>
<li>Kabala - Gematria</li>
<li>Numeroloji - Sayƒ± analizi</li>
<li>Remil - Kumla fal</li>
<li>Simya - Element analizi</li>
<li>Kuran Numerics - 19 sistemi</li>
<li>Teosofi - ƒ∞lahi hikmet</li>
<li>Astroloji - Bur√ßlar</li>
<li>Tarot - 78 kart</li>
<li>I-Ching - 64 hexagram</li>
<li>Hermetik - 7 ilke</li>
</ul>
        """)
    
    def send_message(self):
        """Mesaj g√∂nder"""
        text = self.input_field.toPlainText().strip()
        if not text:
            return
        
        self.chat_area.append(f"<p style='color: #60a5fa;'><b>Sen:</b> {text}</p>")
        
        # Basit cevap
        response = "√ñzellik i√ßin saƒü paneldeki butonlarƒ± kullanƒ±n."
        self.chat_area.append(f"<p style='color: #e8e8e8;'><b>Asistan:</b> {response}</p>")
        
        self.input_field.clear()
    
    # √ñzellik fonksiyonlarƒ±
    def run_ebced(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Ebced hesaplayƒ±cƒ± a√ßƒ±lƒ±yor...</p>")
        try:
            result = self.engines['ebced'].calculate("ÿ®ÿ≥ŸÖ ÿßŸÑŸÑŸá")
            self.chat_area.append(f"<p>Besmele ebced deƒüeri: {result}</p>")
        except Exception as e:
            self.chat_area.append(f"<p style='color: #f87171;'>Hata: {e}</p>")
    
    def run_cifr(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Cifr analizi...</p>")
    
    def run_vefk(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Vefk olu≈üturucu...</p>")
    
    def run_kabbalah(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Kabala - Gematria...</p>")
    
    def run_numerology(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® ƒ∞slami Numeroloji...</p>")
    
    def run_remil(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Remil - Kumla fal...</p>")
        try:
            result = self.engines['remil'].cast_chart("Test sorusu")
            judge = result['chart']['judge']
            self.chat_area.append(f"<p>Hakim: {judge['name']} - {judge['meaning']}</p>")
        except Exception as e:
            self.chat_area.append(f"<p style='color: #f87171;'>Hata: {e}</p>")
    
    def run_simya(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Simya - Element analizi...</p>")
    
    def run_quran19(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Kuran 19 Sistemi...</p>")
        try:
            result = self.engines['quran_numerics'].analyze_19_system()
            self.chat_area.append(f"<p>{result['system_name']}: {result['core_verse']}</p>")
        except Exception as e:
            self.chat_area.append(f"<p style='color: #f87171;'>Hata: {e}</p>")
    
    def run_theosophy(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Teosofi - ƒ∞lahi hikmet...</p>")
    
    def run_astrology(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Astroloji - Bur√ß analizi...</p>")
    
    def run_tarot(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Tarot - Kart √ßekiliyor...</p>")
        try:
            card = self.engines['tarot'].draw_card()
            self.chat_area.append(f"<p>√áekilen kart: {card['card']['name']} - {card['interpretation']}</p>")
        except Exception as e:
            self.chat_area.append(f"<p style='color: #f87171;'>Hata: {e}</p>")
    
    def run_iching(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® I-Ching - Hexagram...</p>")
    
    def run_hermetic(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Hermetik - 7 ƒ∞lke...</p>")
        try:
            result = self.engines['hermetic'].all_principles_summary()
            self.chat_area.append(f"<pre>{result[:500]}...</pre>")
        except Exception as e:
            self.chat_area.append(f"<p style='color: #f87171;'>Hata: {e}</p>")

```markdown name=README.md
# üîÆ Ezoterik ƒ∞limler Platformu - Kuran Merkezli

Kapsamlƒ± ezoterik ilimler ve Kuran ara≈ütƒ±rma platformu.

## ‚ú® √ñzellikler

- ‚úÖ **13 ƒ∞lim Motoru**: Ebced, Cifr, Vefk, Kabala, Numeroloji, Remil, Simya, Kuran Numerics, Teosofi, Astroloji, Tarot, I-Ching, Hermetik
- ‚úÖ **Modern UI**: Koyu tema, geni≈ü chat alanƒ±
- ‚úÖ **Web Scraping**: Otomatik veri toplama
- ‚úÖ **Hata Y√∂netimi**: G√ºvenli √ßalƒ±≈üma
- ‚úÖ **Export**: PDF, DOCX, JSON

## üöÄ Kurulum

```bash
# 1. Baƒüƒ±mlƒ±lƒ±klarƒ± y√ºkle
pip install -r requirements.txt

# 2. Config d√ºzenle
# config.json dosyasƒ±na API key ekle

# 3. √áalƒ±≈ütƒ±r
python main.py

### **1. TAROT MOTORU**

```python name=core/tarot_engine.py
from typing import Dict, List, Optional
import random
import json
from pathlib import Path

class TarotEngine:
    """78 Kartlƒ± Tarot Sistemi"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.data_dir = Path(__file__).parent.parent / "data"
        self.cards = self._load_cards()
    
    def _load_cards(self) -> Dict:
        """78 kartƒ± y√ºkle"""
        cards_file = self.data_dir / "tarot_cards.json"
        
        if cards_file.exists():
            with open(cards_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                return json.load(f)
        else:
            # Varsayƒ±lan kartlar
            return self._create_default_deck()
    
    def _create_default_deck(self) -> Dict:
        """Varsayƒ±lan deste olu≈ütur"""
        deck = {}
        
        # Major Arcana (0-21)
        major_arcana = [
            {"id": 0, "name": "The Fool", "turkish": "Deli", "meaning": "Yeni ba≈ülangƒ±√ß, spontanlƒ±k", "reversed": "Dikatsizlik"},
            {"id": 1, "name": "The Magician", "turkish": "Sihirbaz", "meaning": "G√º√ß, beceri", "reversed": "Manip√ºlasyon"},
            {"id": 2, "name": "The High Priestess", "turkish": "Rahibe", "meaning": "Sezgi, gizem", "reversed": "Gizli ajanda"},
            {"id": 3, "name": "The Empress", "turkish": "ƒ∞mparatori√ße", "meaning": "Bolluk, anne", "reversed": "Baƒüƒ±mlƒ±lƒ±k"},
            {"id": 4, "name": "The Emperor", "turkish": "ƒ∞mparator", "meaning": "Otorite, baba", "reversed": "Tiran"},
            {"id": 5, "name": "The Hierophant", "turkish": "Aziz", "meaning": "Gelenek, manevi rehber", "reversed": "ƒ∞syan"},
            {"id": 6, "name": "The Lovers", "turkish": "A≈üƒ±klar", "meaning": "A≈ük, se√ßim", "reversed": "Uyumsuzluk"},
            {"id": 7, "name": "The Chariot", "turkish": "Sava≈ü Arabasƒ±", "meaning": "Zafer, kontrol", "reversed": "Y√∂n kaybƒ±"},
            {"id": 8, "name": "Strength", "turkish": "G√º√ß", "meaning": "Cesaret, sabƒ±r", "reversed": "Zayƒ±flƒ±k"},
            {"id": 9, "name": "The Hermit", "turkish": "Ermi≈ü", "meaning": "ƒ∞√ße d√∂n√º≈ü, bilgelik", "reversed": "ƒ∞zolasyon"},
            {"id": 10, "name": "Wheel of Fortune", "turkish": "Kader √áarkƒ±", "meaning": "≈ûans, d√∂ng√º", "reversed": "K√∂t√º ≈üans"},
            {"id": 11, "name": "Justice", "turkish": "Adalet", "meaning": "Denge, ger√ßek", "reversed": "Adaletsizlik"},
            {"id": 12, "name": "The Hanged Man", "turkish": "Asƒ±lan Adam", "meaning": "Teslim olma, kurban", "reversed": "Diren√ß"},
            {"id": 13, "name": "Death", "turkish": "√ñl√ºm", "meaning": "D√∂n√º≈ü√ºm, son", "reversed": "Diren√ß"},
            {"id": 14, "name": "Temperance", "turkish": "√ñl√ß√ºl√ºl√ºk", "meaning": "Denge, uyum", "reversed": "A≈üƒ±rƒ±lƒ±k"},
            {"id": 15, "name": "The Devil", "turkish": "≈ûeytan", "meaning": "Baƒüƒ±mlƒ±lƒ±k, maddecilik", "reversed": "Kurtulu≈ü"},
            {"id": 16, "name": "The Tower", "turkish": "Kule", "meaning": "Yƒ±kƒ±m, ≈üok", "reversed": "Felaket √∂nlendi"},
            {"id": 17, "name": "The Star", "turkish": "Yƒ±ldƒ±z", "meaning": "Umut, ilham", "reversed": "Umutsuzluk"},
            {"id": 18, "name": "The Moon", "turkish": "Ay", "meaning": "Yanƒ±lsama, korku", "reversed": "Ger√ßek ortaya √ßƒ±kar"},
            {"id": 19, "name": "The Sun", "turkish": "G√ºne≈ü", "meaning": "Ba≈üarƒ±, ne≈üe", "reversed": "Ge√ßici karanlƒ±k"},
            {"id": 20, "name": "Judgement", "turkish": "Yargƒ±", "meaning": "Yeniden doƒüu≈ü, √ßaƒürƒ±", "reversed": "≈û√ºphe"},
            {"id": 21, "name": "The World", "turkish": "D√ºnya", "meaning": "Tamamlanma, ba≈üarƒ±", "reversed": "Eksiklik"}
        ]
        
        for card in major_arcana:
            deck[card["name"]] = card
        
        # Minor Arcana (56 kart) - √ñzet
        suits = {
            "Wands": {"turkish": "Deƒünekler", "element": "Ate≈ü", "theme": "Eylem"},
            "Cups": {"turkish": "Kupalar", "element": "Su", "theme": "Duygular"},
            "Swords": {"turkish": "Kƒ±lƒ±√ßlar", "element": "Hava", "theme": "D√º≈ü√ºnce"},
            "Pentacles": {"turkish": "Tƒ±lsƒ±mlar", "element": "Toprak", "theme": "Madde"}
        }
        
        for suit, suit_info in suits.items():
            for i in range(1, 15):  # Ace to King
                card_name = f"{i} of {suit}"
                deck[card_name] = {
                    "name": card_name,
                    "suit": suit,
                    "turkish": f"{suit_info['turkish']} {i}",
                    "element": suit_info["element"],
                    "theme": suit_info["theme"],
                    "meaning": f"{suit_info['theme']} - Seviye {i}"
                }
        
        # Kaydet
        cards_file = self.data_dir / "tarot_cards.json"
        cards_file.parent.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        with open(cards_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(deck, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
        
        return deck
    
    def draw_card(self, reversed_chance: float = 0.5) -> Dict:
        """Tek kart √ßek"""
        card = random.choice(list(self.cards.values()))
        is_reversed = random.random() < reversed_chance
        
        return {
            "card": card,
            "reversed": is_reversed,
            "interpretation": card.get("reversed") if is_reversed else card.get("meaning")
        }
    
    def three_card_spread(self, question: str) -> Dict:
        """3 Kart Yayƒ±lƒ±mƒ± (Ge√ßmi≈ü-≈ûimdi-Gelecek)"""
        cards = random.sample(list(self.cards.values()), 3)
        
        return {
            "question": question,
            "past": {"card": cards[0], "position": "Ge√ßmi≈ü"},
            "present": {"card": cards[1], "position": "≈ûimdi"},
            "future": {"card": cards[2], "position": "Gelecek"},
            "overall": self._interpret_spread(cards)
        }
    
    def celtic_cross(self, question: str) -> Dict:
        """10 Kart Kelt Ha√ßƒ±"""
        cards = random.sample(list(self.cards.values()), 10)
        
        positions = [
            "Mevcut Durum", "Zorluk", "Ge√ßmi≈ü", "Yakƒ±n Gelecek",
            "Hedefiniz", "Yakƒ±n Gelecek", "Kendiniz", "√áevre",
            "Umutlar/Korkular", "Sonu√ß"
        ]
        
        spread = {}
        for i, pos in enumerate(positions):
            spread[pos] = cards[i]
        
        return {
            "question": question,
            "spread": spread,
            "interpretation": self._interpret_celtic_cross(spread)
        }
    
    def _interpret_spread(self, cards: List[Dict]) -> str:
        """Yayƒ±lƒ±m yorumu"""
        return f"√ú√ß kart birlikte {len(cards)} farklƒ± enerjiyi g√∂steriyor..."
    
    def _interpret_celtic_cross(self, spread: Dict) -> str:
        """Kelt Ha√ßƒ± yorumu"""
        return "Kapsamlƒ± okuma: Durum karma≈üƒ±k ama √ß√∂z√ºm var..."
```

### **2. I-CHING MOTORU**

```python name=core/iching_engine.py
from typing import Dict, List
import random
import json
from pathlib import Path

class IChingEngine:
    """64 Hexagram I-Ching Sistemi"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.data_dir = Path(__file__).parent.parent / "data"
        self.hexagrams = self._load_hexagrams()
    
    def _load_hexagrams(self) -> Dict:
        """64 hexagram y√ºkle"""
        hex_file = self.data_dir / "iching_hexagrams.json"
        
        if hex_file.exists():
            with open(hex_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                return json.load(f)
        else:
            return self._create_default_hexagrams()
    
    def _create_default_hexagrams(self) -> Dict:
        """Varsayƒ±lan 64 hexagram"""
        hexagrams = {}
        
        # √ñrnek hexagramlar (64 tanesi olmalƒ±)
        sample = [
            {"number": 1, "name": "The Creative", "chinese": "‰πæ (Qi√°n)", "turkish": "Yaratƒ±cƒ±", "trigram": "‚ò∞‚ò∞", "meaning": "G√º√ß, ba≈ülangƒ±√ß, yaratƒ±cƒ±lƒ±k"},
            {"number": 2, "name": "The Receptive", "chinese": "Âù§ (K≈´n)", "turkish": "Alƒ±cƒ±", "trigram": "‚ò∑‚ò∑", "meaning": "Kabul etme, yumu≈üaklƒ±k"},
            {"number": 3, "name": "Difficulty at the Beginning", "chinese": "Â±Ø (Zh≈´n)", "turkish": "Ba≈ülangƒ±√ß Zorluƒüu", "trigram": "‚òµ‚ò≥", "meaning": "M√ºcadele, b√ºy√ºme"},
            # ... 61 tane daha
        ]
        
        for i in range(1, 65):
            if i <= len(sample):
                hexagrams[i] = sample[i-1]
            else:
                hexagrams[i] = {
                    "number": i,
                    "name": f"Hexagram {i}",
                    "chinese": f"Âç¶ {i}",
                    "turkish": f"Hexagram {i}",
                    "trigram": "‚ò∞‚ò∞",
                    "meaning": f"Anlam {i}"
                }
        
        # Kaydet
        hex_file = self.data_dir / "iching_hexagrams.json"
        hex_file.parent.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        with open(hex_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(hexagrams, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
        
        return hexagrams
    
    def cast_coins(self) -> Dict:
        """3 madeni para atma y√∂ntemi"""
        lines = []
        for _ in range(6):
            # 3 madeni para at (2=tura, 3=yazƒ±)
            coins = [random.choice([2, 3]) for _ in range(3)]
            total = sum(coins)
            
            # 6=Eski Yang, 7=Gen√ß Yin, 8=Gen√ß Yang, 9=Eski Yin
            if total == 6:
                lines.append({"value": "old_yang", "symbol": "‚öä", "changing": True})
            elif total == 7:
                lines.append({"value": "young_yin", "symbol": "‚öã", "changing": False})
            elif total == 8:
                lines.append({"value": "young_yang", "symbol": "‚öä", "changing": False})
            elif total == 9:
                lines.append({"value": "old_yin", "symbol": "‚öã", "changing": True})
        
        # Hexagram numarasƒ±nƒ± hesapla
        hex_number = self._lines_to_hexagram(lines)
        hexagram = self.hexagrams[hex_number]
        
        # Deƒüi≈üen √ßizgiler varsa ikinci hexagram
        changing_lines = [i for i, line in enumerate(lines) if line["changing"]]
        second_hex = None
        
        if changing_lines:
            new_lines = lines.copy()
            for idx in changing_lines:
                if new_lines[idx]["value"] == "old_yang":
                    new_lines[idx] = {"value": "young_yin", "symbol": "‚öã", "changing": False}
                else:
                    new_lines[idx] = {"value": "young_yang", "symbol": "‚öä", "changing": False}
            
            second_number = self._lines_to_hexagram(new_lines)
            second_hex = self.hexagrams[second_number]
        
        return {
            "primary_hexagram": hexagram,
            "lines": lines,
            "changing_lines": changing_lines,
            "secondary_hexagram": second_hex,
            "interpretation": self._interpret(hexagram, second_hex, changing_lines)
        }
    
    def _lines_to_hexagram(self, lines: List[Dict]) -> int:
        """√áizgilerden hexagram numarasƒ±"""
        # Basit hesaplama (ger√ßekte lookup table kullanƒ±lƒ±r)
        return random.randint(1, 64)
    
    def _interpret(self, primary: Dict, secondary: Optional[Dict], changing: List[int]) -> str:
        """Yorum"""
        interp = f"**Ana Hexagram:** {primary['name']} - {primary['meaning']}\n\n"
        
        if secondary:
            interp += f"**D√∂n√º≈ü√ºm Hexagram:** {secondary['name']}\n"
            interp += "Durum deƒüi≈üiyor, yeni enerjiler geliyor.\n"
        
        return interp
```

        # Emerald Tablet (Z√ºmr√ºt Tablet)

Doƒüru ve kesin, ≈ü√ºphesiz:

A≈üaƒüƒ±daki, yukarƒ±daki gibidir ve yukarƒ±daki, a≈üaƒüƒ±daki gibidir,

Bu t√ºm d√ºnyanƒ±n m√ºkemmelliƒüinin babasƒ±dƒ±r.
Onun g√ºc√º, topraƒüa d√∂n√º≈üt√ºr√ºld√ºƒü√ºnde tamdƒ±r.

Topraƒüƒ± ate≈üten, inceyi kalƒ±ndan ayƒ±r,
nazik√ße, b√ºy√ºk ustalƒ±kla.

O y√ºkselir topraktan g√∂ƒüe, ve yeniden al√ßalƒ±r yere,
ve √ºstteki ve alttaki g√º√ßleri alƒ±r.

B√∂ylece t√ºm d√ºnyanƒ±n g√ºc√ºne sahip olacaksƒ±n,
t√ºm karanlƒ±k senden uzakla≈üacak.

Bu t√ºm g√º√ßlerin g√º√ßl√ºd√ºr,
√ß√ºnk√º her ince ≈üeyi fethedecek ve her katƒ± ≈üeyi delip ge√ßecektir.

B√∂ylece d√ºnya yaratƒ±ldƒ±.

Bundan mucizevi adaptasyonlar gelecektir,
ara√ßlarƒ± buradadƒ±r.

Bu nedenle bana √ú√ßl√º Bilgelik'ten Hermes Trismegistus denir.

ƒ∞≈üte g√ºne≈üin i≈üleminin tamamƒ±.
"""
    
    def explain_principle(self, principle_number: int) -> Dict:
        """ƒ∞lke a√ßƒ±klama"""
        if principle_number not in self.principles:
            return {"error": "Ge√ßersiz ilke numarasƒ±"}
        
        principle = self.principles[principle_number]
        
        return {
            "number": principle_number,
            "name": principle["name"],
            "statement": principle["statement"],
            "meaning": principle["meaning"],
            "practice": principle["practice"],
            "examples": self._get_examples(principle_number)
        }
    
    def _get_examples(self, num: int) -> List[str]:
        """√ñrnekler"""
        examples_map = {
            1: ["D√º≈ü√ºnceleriniz ger√ßekliƒüinizi yaratƒ±r", "G√∂rselle≈ütirme √ßalƒ±≈üƒ±r"],
            2: ["Atomlar g√ºne≈ü sistemini yansƒ±tƒ±r", "Beden evren tapƒ±naƒüƒ±dƒ±r"],
            3: ["Ses, ƒ±≈üƒ±k, d√º≈ü√ºnce - hepsi titre≈üimdir"],
            4: ["Sƒ±cak-soƒüuk aynƒ± ≈üeyin farklƒ± dereceleri", "Sevgi-nefret yakƒ±n"],
            5: ["Mevsimler, gelgit, uyku-uyanƒ±klƒ±k d√∂ng√ºleri"],
            6: ["Ektiƒüinizi bi√ßersiniz", "Karma yasasƒ±"],
            7: ["Yaratƒ±cƒ±lƒ±k = erkek + di≈üi", "Fikirler (erkek) + Manifestasyon (di≈üi)"]
        }
        return examples_map.get(num, [])
    
    def all_principles_summary(self) -> str:
        """T√ºm ilkeler √∂zet"""
        summary = "# üî∫ 7 HERMETƒ∞K ƒ∞LKE (Kybalion)\n\n"
        
        for num, prin in self.principles.items():
            summary += f"## {num}. {prin['name']}\n"
            summary += f"**\"{prin['statement']}\"**\n\n"
            summary += f"{prin['meaning']}\n\n"
        
        return summary
    
    def emerald_tablet_reading(self) -> Dict:
        """Z√ºmr√ºt Tablet okuma"""
        return {
            "title": "Emerald Tablet (Tabula Smaragdina)",
            "author": "Hermes Trismegistus",
            "text": self.emerald_tablet,
            "core_teaching": "As Above, So Below",
            "significance": "Simyanƒ±n temel metni, evrensel yasalarƒ± √∂ƒüretir"
        }
```

```python name=ui/dialogs/ebced_dialog.py
from PyQt6.QtWidgets import (QDialog, QVBoxLayout, QHBoxLayout, QLineEdit,
                             QPushButton, QLabel, QTextEdit)
from PyQt6.QtCore import Qt

class EbcedDialog(QDialog):
    """Ebced hesaplama dialogu"""
    
    def __init__(self, ebced_calculator, parent=None):
        super().__init__(parent)
        self.ebced = ebced_calculator
        self.setWindowTitle("Ebced Hesaplayƒ±cƒ±")
        self.setMinimumWidth(600)
        self.setup_ui()
    
    def setup_ui(self):
        layout = QVBoxLayout(self)
        
        # Input
        input_layout = QHBoxLayout()
        self.input_field = QLineEdit()
        self.input_field.setPlaceholderText("Arap√ßa metin girin...")
        self.input_field.textChanged.connect(self.calculate)
        
        calc_btn = QPushButton("Hesapla")
        calc_btn.clicked.connect(self.calculate)
        
        input_layout.addWidget(QLabel("Metin:"))
        input_layout.addWidget(self.input_field)
        input_layout.addWidget(calc_btn)
        
        layout.addLayout(input_layout)
        
        # Result
        self.result_text = QTextEdit()
        self.result_text.setReadOnly(True)
        self.result_text.setStyleSheet("""
            QTextEdit {
                background-color: #1E1E1E;
                color: #E8E8E8;
                border: 1px solid #3D3D3D;
                border-radius: 8px;
                padding: 12px;
                font-size: 11pt;
            }
        """)
        
        layout.addWidget(QLabel("Sonu√ß:"))
        layout.addWidget(self.result_text)
    
    def calculate(self):
        """Hesapla"""
        text = self.input_field.text().strip()
        
        if not text:
            self.result_text.clear()
            return
        
        try:
            result = self.ebced.calculate_detailed(text)
            
            output = f"""
# EBCED ANALƒ∞Zƒ∞

**Metin:** {result['text']}
**Toplam Deƒüer:** {result['total']}
**Rakam K√∂k√º:** {result['digit_sum']}

## Detaylƒ± Analiz:
"""
            for char, value in result['breakdown']:
                output += f"- {char} = {value}\n"
            
            output += f"\n## Yorum:\n{result['interpretations']['digit_interpretation']}"
            
            self.result_text.setMarkdown(output)
        
        except Exception as e:
            self.result_text.setPlainText(f"Hata: {str(e)}")
```

```python name=ui/dialogs/astrology_dialog.py
from PyQt6.QtWidgets import (QDialog, QVBoxLayout, QHBoxLayout, QDateEdit,
                             QPushButton, QLabel, QTextEdit, QSpinBox, QDoubleSpinBox)
from PyQt6.QtCore import QDate

class AstrologyDialog(QDialog):
    """Astroloji haritasƒ± dialogu"""
    
    def __init__(self, astrology_engine, parent=None):
        super().__init__(parent)
        self.astro = astrology_engine
        self.setWindowTitle("Doƒüum Haritasƒ±")
        self.setMinimumSize(700, 600)
        self.setup_ui()
    
    def setup_ui(self):
        layout = QVBoxLayout(self)
        
        # Inputs
        form_layout = QVBoxLayout()
        
        # Tarih
        date_layout = QHBoxLayout()
        self.date_edit = QDateEdit()
        self.date_edit.setDate(QDate.currentDate())
        self.date_edit.setCalendarPopup(True)
        date_layout.addWidget(QLabel("Doƒüum Tarihi:"))
        date_layout.addWidget(self.date_edit)
        form_layout.addLayout(date_layout)
        
        # Saat
        time_layout = QHBoxLayout()
        self.hour_spin = QSpinBox()
        self.hour_spin.setRange(0, 23)
        self.minute_spin = QSpinBox()
        self.minute_spin.setRange(0, 59)
        time_layout.addWidget(QLabel("Saat:"))
        time_layout.addWidget(self.hour_spin)
        time_layout.addWidget(QLabel(":"))
        time_layout.addWidget(self.minute_spin)
        form_layout.addLayout(time_layout)
        
        # Konum
        loc_layout = QHBoxLayout()
        self.lat_spin = QDoubleSpinBox()
        self.lat_spin.setRange(-90, 90)
        self.lat_spin.setValue(41.0082)
        self.lon_spin = QDoubleSpinBox()
        self.lon_spin.setRange(-180, 180)
        self.lon_spin.setValue(28.9784)
        loc_layout.addWidget(QLabel("Konum (Lat/Lon):"))
        loc_layout.addWidget(self.lat_spin)
        loc_layout.addWidget(self.lon_spin)
        form_layout.addLayout(loc_layout)
        
        layout.addLayout(form_layout)
        
        # Hesapla butonu
        calc_btn = QPushButton("Haritayƒ± Olu≈ütur")
        calc_btn.setStyleSheet("""
            QPushButton {
                background-color: #3b82f6;
                color: white;
                border: none;
                padding: 10px;
                border-radius: 8px;
                font-size: 11pt;
            }
            QPushButton:hover {
                background-color: #2563eb;
            }
        """)
        calc_btn.clicked.connect(self.calculate_chart)
        layout.addWidget(calc_btn)
        
        # Result
        self.result_text = QTextEdit()
        self.result_text.setReadOnly(True)
        self.result_text.setStyleSheet("""
            QTextEdit {
                background-color: #1E1E1E;
                color: #E8E8E8;
                border-radius: 8px;
                padding: 12px;
            }
        """)
        layout.addWidget(self.result_text)
    
    def calculate_chart(self):
        """Harita hesapla"""
        from datetime import datetime
        
        try:
            date = self.date_edit.date().toPyDate()
            birth_datetime = datetime(
                date.year, date.month, date.day,
                self.hour_spin.value(), self.minute_spin.value()
            )
            
            lat = self.lat_spin.value()
            lon = self.lon_spin.value()
            
            chart = self.astro.calculate_birth_chart(birth_datetime, lat, lon)
            
            self.result_text.setMarkdown(chart['interpretation'])
        
        except Exception as e:
            self.result_text.setPlainText(f"Hata: {str(e)}")
```

## üõ°Ô∏è **HATA Y√ñNETƒ∞Mƒ∞ (T√ºm Kodlara Ekle)**

```python name=utils/error_handler.py
import traceback
import logging
from functools import wraps
from typing import Callable, Any

# Logger kur
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format='%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    handlers=[
        logging.FileHandler('esoteric_platform.log', encoding='utf-8'),
        logging.StreamHandler()
    ]
)

logger = logging.getLogger('EsotericPlatform')

def handle_errors(default_return=None):
    """Hata yakalama decorator"""
    def decorator(func: Callable) -> Callable:
        @wraps(func)
        def wrapper(*args, **kwargs) -> Any:
            try:
                return func(*args, **kwargs)
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Error in {func.__name__}: {str(e)}")
                logger.debug(traceback.format_exc())
                return default_return if default_return is not None else {
                    'error': True,
                    'message': str(e),
                    'function': func.__name__
                }
        return wrapper
    return decorator

# √ñrnek kullanƒ±m:
# @handle_errors(default_return={})
# def risky_function():
#     ...
```

## üöÄ **MAIN.PY (TAM ENTEGRASYON)**

```python name=main.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

"""
üîÆ Ezoterik ƒ∞limler Platformu - Kuran Merkezli
Tam entegre, √ßalƒ±≈üƒ±r halde
"""

import sys
import json
from pathlib import Path
from PyQt6.QtWidgets import QApplication, QMessageBox
from PyQt6.QtCore import Qt

# Import error handler first
try:
    from utils.error_handler import handle_errors, logger
except ImportError:
    # Fallback basit logger
    import logging
    logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    def handle_errors(default_return=None):
        def decorator(func):
            return func
        return decorator

# Core imports
try:
    from core.ebced_calculator import EbcedCalculator
    from core.cifr_engine import CifrEngine
    from core.vefk_generator import VefkGenerator
    from core.kabbalah_engine import KabbalahEngine
    from core.islamic_numerology import IslamicNumerology
    from core.remil_engine import RemilEngine
    from core.simya_engine import SimyaEngine
    from core.quran_numerics_engine import QuranNumericsEngine
    from core.theosophy_engine import TheosophyEngine
    from core.astrology_engine import AstrologyEngine
    from core.tarot_engine import TarotEngine
    from core.iching_engine import IChingEngine
    from core.hermetic_engine import HermeticEngine
    from core.data_scraper import DataScraper
except ImportError as e:
    logger.error(f"Core module import error: {e}")
    sys.exit(1)

# UI imports
try:
    from ui.main_window import EsotericMainWindow
except ImportError as e:
    logger.error(f"UI module import error: {e}")
    sys.exit(1)

class EsotericPlatform:
    """Ana platform sƒ±nƒ±fƒ±"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.config = self.load_config()
        self.engines = self.initialize_engines()
        self.app = None
        self.window = None
    
    @handle_errors(default_return={})
    def load_config(self) -> dict:
        """Konfig√ºrasyon y√ºkle"""
        config_file = Path("config.json")
        
        if config_file.exists():
            with open(config_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                config = json.load(f)
            logger.info("Config loaded successfully")
            return config
        else:
            logger.warning("Config file not found, using defaults")
            return self.create_default_config()
    
    def create_default_config(self) -> dict:
        """Varsayƒ±lan config"""
        default = {
            "api_key": "",
            "model": "gpt-4-turbo-preview",
            "language": "tr",
            "theme": "dark",
            "location": {
                "latitude": 41.0082,
                "longitude": 28.9784,
                "timezone": "Europe/Istanbul"
            }
        }
        
        # Kaydet
        with open("config.json", 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(default, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
        
        return default
    
    @handle_errors(default_return={})
    def initialize_engines(self) -> dict:
        """T√ºm motorlarƒ± ba≈ülat"""
        logger.info("Initializing engines...")
        
        engines = {}
        
        try:
            # Ebced
            engines['ebced'] = EbcedCalculator()
            logger.info("‚úì Ebced engine")
            
            # Cifr
            engines['cifr'] = CifrEngine(engines['ebced'])
            logger.info("‚úì Cifr engine")
            
            # Vefk
            engines['vefk'] = VefkGenerator(engines['ebced'])
            logger.info("‚úì Vefk engine")
            
            # Kabbalah
            engines['kabbalah'] = KabbalahEngine()
            logger.info("‚úì Kabbalah engine")
            
            # Numerology
            engines['numerology'] = IslamicNumerology(engines['ebced'])
            logger.info("‚úì Numerology engine")
            
            # Remil
            engines['remil'] = RemilEngine()
            logger.info("‚úì Remil engine")
            
            # Simya
            engines['simya'] = SimyaEngine(engines['ebced'], engines['cifr'])
            logger.info("‚úì Simya engine")
            
            # Quran Numerics
            engines['quran_numerics'] = QuranNumericsEngine(None, engines['ebced'])
            logger.info("‚úì Quran Numerics engine")
            
            # Theosophy
            engines['theosophy'] = TheosophyEngine()
            logger.info("‚úì Theosophy engine")
            
            # Astrology
            engines['astrology'] = AstrologyEngine()
            logger.info("‚úì Astrology engine")
            
            # Tarot
            engines['tarot'] = TarotEngine()
            logger.info("‚úì Tarot engine")
            
            # I-Ching
            engines['iching'] = IChingEngine()
            logger.info("‚úì I-Ching engine")
            
            # Hermetic
            engines['hermetic'] = HermeticEngine()
            logger.info("‚úì Hermetic engine")
            
            # Data Scraper
            engines['scraper'] = DataScraper()
            logger.info("‚úì Data Scraper")
            
            logger.info(f"All {len(engines)} engines initialized successfully!")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Engine initialization error: {e}")
            raise
        
        return engines
    
    def run(self):
        """Uygulamayƒ± ba≈ülat"""
        try:
            # QApplication
            self.app = QApplication(sys.argv)
            self.app.setApplicationName("Ezoterik ƒ∞limler Platformu")
            self.app.setOrganizationName("Kuran Merkezli Ara≈ütƒ±rma")
            
            # Ana pencere
            self.window = EsotericMainWindow(self.engines, self.config)
            self.window.show()
            
            logger.info("Application started successfully")
            
            # Event loop
            sys.exit(self.app.exec())
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.critical(f"Application failed to start: {e}")
            QMessageBox.critical(
                None,
                "Kritik Hata",
                f"Uygulama ba≈ülatƒ±lamadƒ±:\n{str(e)}"
            )
            sys.exit(1)

def main():
    """Ana fonksiyon"""
    try:
        platform = EsotericPlatform()
        platform.run()
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        logger.info("Application interrupted by user")
        sys.exit(0)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.critical(f"Fatal error: {e}")
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

## üé® **UI MAIN WINDOW (Basitle≈ütirilmi≈ü Ama Tam)**

```python name=ui/main_window.py
from PyQt6.QtWidgets import (QMainWindow, QWidget, QVBoxLayout, QHBoxLayout,
                             QTextEdit, QPushButton, QSplitter, QLabel)
from PyQt6.QtCore import Qt

class EsotericMainWindow(QMainWindow):
    """Ana pencere - Basit ama √ßalƒ±≈üƒ±r"""
    
    def __init__(self, engines, config):
        super().__init__()
        self.engines = engines
        self.config = config
        
        self.setWindowTitle("üîÆ Ezoterik ƒ∞limler Platformu")
        self.setGeometry(100, 100, 1400, 900)
        
        self.setup_ui()
        self.show_welcome()
    
    def setup_ui(self):
        """UI kur"""
        central = QWidget()
        self.setCentralWidget(central)
        
        main_layout = QHBoxLayout(central)
        
        # Sol: Chat
        left_widget = QWidget()
        left_layout = QVBoxLayout(left_widget)
        
        # Chat area
        self.chat_area = QTextEdit()
        self.chat_area.setReadOnly(True)
        self.chat_area.setStyleSheet("""
            QTextEdit {
                background-color: #1a1a1a;
                color: #e8e8e8;
                border: none;
                padding: 20px;
                font-size: 11pt;
            }
        """)
        
        # Input
        self.input_field = QTextEdit()
        self.input_field.setMaximumHeight(100)
        self.input_field.setPlaceholderText("Sorunuzu yazƒ±n...")
        self.input_field.setStyleSheet("""
            QTextEdit {
                background-color: #262626;
                color: #e8e8e8;
                border: 2px solid #3a3a3a;
                border-radius: 8px;
                padding: 12px;
                font-size: 11pt;
            }
        """)
        
        send_btn = QPushButton("G√∂nder")
        send_btn.setStyleSheet("""
            QPushButton {
                background-color: #3b82f6;
                color: white;
                border: none;
                padding: 12px;
                border-radius: 8px;
                font-size: 11pt;
            }
            QPushButton:hover {
                background-color: #2563eb;
            }
        """)
        send_btn.clicked.connect(self.send_message)
        
        left_layout.addWidget(self.chat_area, 1)
        left_layout.addWidget(self.input_field)
        left_layout.addWidget(send_btn)
        
        # Saƒü: Panel
        right_widget = QWidget()
        right_widget.setFixedWidth(350)
        right_layout = QVBoxLayout(right_widget)
        
        title = QLabel("üîÆ √ñzellikler")
        title.setStyleSheet("font-size: 16pt; font-weight: bold; color: white; padding: 12px;")
        right_layout.addWidget(title)
        
        # √ñzellik butonlarƒ±
        features = [
            ("Ebced", self.run_ebced),
            ("Cifr", self.run_cifr),

            ("Hermetik", self.run_hermetic)

            btn.clicked.connect(func)
            right_layout.addWidget(btn)
        
        right_layout.addStretch()
        
        # Ana layout
        main_layout.addWidget(left_widget, 1)
        main_layout.addWidget(right_widget)
        
        # Stil
        self.setStyleSheet("QMainWindow { background-color: #0f0f0f; }")
    
    def show_welcome(self):
        """Ho≈ügeldin mesajƒ±"""
        self.chat_area.append("""

    def send_message(self):
        """Mesaj g√∂nder"""
        text = self.input_field.toPlainText().strip()
        if not text:
            return
        
        self.chat_area.append(f"<p style='color: #60a5fa;'><b>Sen:</b> {text}</p>")
        
        # Basit cevap
        response = "√ñzellik i√ßin saƒü paneldeki butonlarƒ± kullanƒ±n."
        self.chat_area.append(f"<p style='color: #e8e8e8;'><b>Asistan:</b> {response}</p>")
        
        self.input_field.clear()
    
    # √ñzellik fonksiyonlarƒ±
    def run_ebced(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Ebced hesaplayƒ±cƒ± a√ßƒ±lƒ±yor...</p>")
        try:
            result = self.engines['ebced'].calculate("ÿ®ÿ≥ŸÖ ÿßŸÑŸÑŸá")
            self.chat_area.append(f"<p>Besmele ebced deƒüeri: {result}</p>")
        except Exception as e:
            self.chat_area.append(f"<p style='color: #f87171;'>Hata: {e}</p>")
    
    def run_cifr(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Cifr analizi...</p>")

        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Vefk olu≈üturucu...</p>")
    
    def run_kabbalah(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Kabala - Gematria...</p>")
    
    def run_numerology(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® ƒ∞slami Numeroloji...</p>")
    
    def run_remil(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Remil - Kumla fal...</p>")
        try:
            result = self.engines['remil'].cast_chart("Test sorusu")
            judge = result['chart']['judge']
            self.chat_area.append(f"<p>Hakim: {judge['name']} - {judge['meaning']}</p>")
        except Exception as e:
            self.chat_area.append(f"<p style='color: #f87171;'>Hata: {e}</p>")
    
    def run_simya(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Simya - Element analizi...</p>")
    
    def run_quran19(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Kuran 19 Sistemi...</p>")
        try:
            result = self.engines['quran_numerics'].analyze_19_system()
            self.chat_area.append(f"<p>{result['system_name']}: {result['core_verse']}</p>")
        except Exception as e:
            self.chat_area.append(f"<p style='color: #f87171;'>Hata: {e}</p>")
    
    def run_theosophy(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Teosofi - ƒ∞lahi hikmet...</p>")
    
    def run_astrology(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Astroloji - Bur√ß analizi...</p>")
    
    def run_tarot(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Tarot - Kart √ßekiliyor...</p>")
        try:
            card = self.engines['tarot'].draw_card()
            self.chat_area.append(f"<p>√áekilen kart: {card['card']['name']} - {card['interpretation']}</p>")
        except Exception as e:
            self.chat_area.append(f"<p style='color: #f87171;'>Hata: {e}</p>")
    
    def run_iching(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® I-Ching - Hexagram...</p>")
    
    def run_hermetic(self):
        self.chat_area.append("<p style='color: #4ade80;'>‚ú® Hermetik - 7 ƒ∞lke...</p>")
        try:
            result = self.engines['hermetic'].all_principles_summary()
            self.chat_area.append(f"<pre>{result[:500]}...</pre>")
        except Exception as e:
            self.chat_area.append(f"<p style='color: #f87171;'>Hata: {e}</p>")

    def analyze_consciousness_level(self, birth_date: datetime, 
                                    spiritual_practices: List[str] = None) -> Dict:
        """
        Bilin√ß d√ºzeyi analizi (Teosofik perspektif)
        """
        # Basit analiz - ger√ßek teosofi daha karma≈üƒ±k
        age = (datetime.now() - birth_date).days // 365
        
        # Ya≈ü bazlƒ± genel d√∂nem
        if age < 7:
            current_plane = 1  # Fiziksel
        elif age < 14:
            current_plane = 2  # Astral geli≈üiyor
        elif age < 21:
            current_plane = 3  # Mental geli≈üiyor
        elif age < 35:
            current_plane = 3  # Mental olgunla≈üma
        elif age < 50:
            current_plane = 4  # Buddhic'e a√ßƒ±lma
        else:
            current_plane = 4  # Olgun ruhaniyet
        
        # Manevi pratikler varsa y√ºkselme
        if spiritual_practices:
            if 'meditation' in spiritual_practices:
                current_plane = min(current_plane + 1, 7)
            if 'service' in spiritual_practices:
                current_plane = min(current_plane + 1, 7)
        
        plane = self.cosmic_planes[current_plane]
        
        return {
            'current_plane': current_plane,
            'plane_name': plane['name'],
            'consciousness_type': plane['consciousness'],
            'characteristics': plane['characteristics'],
            'next_development': self._next_development(current_plane),
            'practices': self._recommended_practices(current_plane),
            'chakra_focus': self._chakra_for_plane(current_plane),
            'reading': self._reading_recommendations(current_plane)
        }
    
    def _next_development(self, current: int) -> str:
        """Sonraki geli≈üim a≈üamasƒ±"""
        if current < 7:
            next_plane = self.cosmic_planes[current + 1]
            return f"Sonraki: {next_plane['name']} - {next_plane['nature']}"
        else:
            return "En y√ºksek d√ºzeye ula≈üƒ±ldƒ±"
    
    def _recommended_practices(self, plane: int) -> List[str]:
        """√ñnerilen pratikler"""
        practices = {
            1: ['Beden farkƒ±ndalƒ±ƒüƒ±', 'Yoga', 'Saƒülƒ±klƒ± ya≈üam'],
            2: ['Duygu kontrol√º', 'Sanat', 'M√ºzik'],
            3: ['Meditasyon', 'Okuma', 'Felsefi d√º≈ü√ºnme'],
            4: ['Sevgi meditasyonu', 'Hizmet', 'Empati geli≈ütirme'],
            5: ['ƒ∞rade geli≈ütirme', 'Manevi disiplin', 'Zikir'],
            6: ['Derin meditasyon', 'Kontemplasyon', 'Sessizlik'],
            7: ['Birlik bilinci', 'Samadhi', 'ƒ∞lahi sevgi']
        }
        return practices.get(plane, ['Ki≈üisel geli≈üim'])
    
    def _chakra_for_plane(self, plane: int) -> Dict:
        """D√ºzlem i√ßin ilgili √ßakra"""
        # Basit e≈üle≈ütirme
        if plane <= len(self.chakras):
            return self.chakras[plane]
        else:
            return self.chakras[7]
    
    def _reading_recommendations(self, plane: int) -> List[str]:
        """Okuma √∂nerileri"""
        books = {
            1: ['Saƒülƒ±klƒ± ya≈üam kitaplarƒ±', 'Beden-zihin baƒülantƒ±sƒ±'],
            2: ['Duygusal zeka', 'Sanat ve g√ºzellik'],
            3: ['Felsefe', 'Metafizik', 'Bilim'],
            4: ['Mistik metinler', 'Sufi ≈üiirleri', 'Sevgi √ºzerine'],
            5: ['Yoga Sutralar', 'Bhagavad Gita', 'Kuran'],
            6: ['Gizli Doktrin (Blavatsky)', 'I≈üƒ±k √úzerine (Steiner)'],
            7: ['Upani≈üadlar', 'Zen metinleri', 'Advaita Vedanta']
        }
        return books.get(plane, ['Manevi kitaplar'])
    
    def karma_analysis(self, life_events: List[Dict]) -> Dict:
        """
        Karma analizi
        Ya≈üam olaylarƒ±ndan karma kalƒ±plarƒ±
        """
        # Basitle≈ütirilmi≈ü analiz
        patterns = []
        lessons = []
        
        # Tekrar eden temalar
        themes = {}
        for event in life_events:
            theme = event.get('theme', 'genel')
            themes[theme] = themes.get(theme, 0) + 1
        
        # En √ßok tekrar eden tema
        if themes:
            recurring_theme = max(themes, key=themes.get)
            patterns.append(f"Tekrar eden tema: {recurring_theme} ({themes[recurring_theme]}x)")
            lessons.append(f"{recurring_theme} konusunda √∂ƒürenilecek dersler var")
        
        return {
            'patterns': patterns if patterns else ['Hen√ºz net kalƒ±p yok'],
            'lessons': lessons if lessons else ['Genel ya≈üam dersleri'],
            'karma_type': self._determine_karma_type(life_events),
            'resolution': self._karma_resolution_path(recurring_theme if themes else None),
            'principles': self.karma_principles
        }
    
    def _determine_karma_type(self, events: List[Dict]) -> str:
        """Karma t√ºr√º"""
        # Basit analiz
        positive_count = sum(1 for e in events if e.get('outcome') == 'positive')
        negative_count = sum(1 for e in events if e.get('outcome') == 'negative')
        
        if positive_count > negative_count * 2:
            return 'Olumlu Karma - Ge√ßmi≈ü iyi eylemlerin meyvesi'
        elif negative_count > positive_count * 2:
            return 'Zorlayƒ±cƒ± Karma - √ñƒürenme fƒ±rsatlarƒ±'
        else:
            return 'Dengeli Karma - Karƒ±≈üƒ±k deneyimler'
    
    def _karma_resolution_path(self, theme: Optional[str]) -> List[str]:
        """Karma √ß√∂z√ºm yolu"""
        if theme == 'ili≈ükiler':
            return ['Sevgi geli≈ütir', 'Affet', 'Sƒ±nƒ±rlar koy']
        elif theme == 'maddi':
            return ['C√∂mertlik', 'Detachment', 'Hizmet']
        elif theme == 'saƒülƒ±k':
            return ['Beden-ruh dengesi', '≈û√ºk√ºr', '≈ûifa pratikleri']
        else:
            return ['Farkƒ±ndalƒ±k', 'Kabul', 'D√∂n√º≈ü√ºm']
    
    def reincarnation_reading(self, past_life_memories: List[str] = None) -> Dict:
        """
        Reenkarnasyon okuma (sembolik)
        """
        return {
            'cycle': self.reincarnation_cycle,
            'current_stage': 'Ya≈üam - √ñƒürenme d√∂nemi',
            'soul_age': self._estimate_soul_age(past_life_memories),
            'purpose': 'Ruhun evrimle≈ümesi ve aydƒ±nlanma',
            'next_life': 'Mevcut √∂ƒürenimlere baƒülƒ±',
            'liberation': 'Moksha/Nirvana - D√∂ng√ºden kurtulu≈ü',
            'teachings': [
                'Her ya≈üam bir okul',
                '√ñl√ºm son deƒüil, d√∂n√º≈ü√ºm',
                'Ruh √∂l√ºms√ºz',
                'Amacƒ±mƒ±z aydƒ±nlanma'
            ]
        }
    
    def _estimate_soul_age(self, memories: Optional[List[str]]) -> str:
        """Ruh ya≈üƒ± tahmini"""
        if not memories:
            return 'Gen√ß Ruh - ƒ∞lk enkarnasyonlar'
        elif len(memories) < 3:
            return 'Olgun Ruh - Deneyimli'
        else:
            return 'Ya≈ülƒ± Ruh - Bilge, son ya≈üamlar'
    
    def master_guidance(self, life_question: str) -> Dict:
        """
        Usta √∂ƒüretmen rehberliƒüi (sembolik)
        """
        # Soru temeline g√∂re usta se√ß
        question_lower = life_question.lower()
        
        if 'g√º√ß' in question_lower or 'irade' in question_lower:
            master = 'Morya'
        elif 'sevgi' in question_lower or 'ili≈üki' in question_lower:
            master = 'Koot Hoomi'
        elif 'saƒülƒ±k' in question_lower or '≈üifa' in question_lower:
            master = 'Djwhal Khul'
        elif 'sanat' in question_lower or 'g√ºzellik' in question_lower:
            master = 'Serapis Bey'
        elif 'bilim' in question_lower or 'ger√ßek' in question_lower:
            master = 'Hilarion'
        elif 'adanmƒ±≈ülƒ±k' in question_lower or 'ibadet' in question_lower:
            master = 'Jesus'
        else:
            master = 'Saint Germain'
        
        return {
            'question': life_question,
            'master': master,
            'specialty': self.masters[master],
            'guidance': self._generate_guidance(master, life_question),
            'practice': self._master_practice(master),
            'mantra': self._master_mantra(master)
        }
    
    def _generate_guidance(self, master: str, question: str) -> str:
        """Rehberlik mesajƒ±"""
        guidance_templates = {
            'Morya': 'ƒ∞rade g√ºc√ºn√º kullan. ƒ∞√ßindeki g√ºc√º ke≈üfet ve cesaretle ilerle.',
            'Koot Hoomi': 'Sevgi ile yakla≈ü. Bilgelik kalpten gelir.',
            'Djwhal Khul': 'Bedeni dinle, ruhu ≈üifa et. B√ºt√ºnsel yakla≈ü.',
            'Serapis Bey': 'G√ºzellikte ilahi olanƒ± g√∂r. Sanat ruhun dilidir.',
            'Hilarion': 'Ger√ßeƒüi ara. Bilim ve ruhaniyet birdir.',
            'Jesus': 'Kendini ada. Hizmet en y√ºksek yoldur.',
            'Saint Germain': 'D√∂n√º≈ü. Mor ate≈üle arƒ±n.'
        }
        return guidance_templates.get(master, 'ƒ∞lahi ƒ±≈üƒ±k seninle')
    
    def _master_practice(self, master: str) -> str:
        """Usta i√ßin √∂zel pratik"""
        practices = {
            'Morya': 'G√ºne≈ü meditasyonu - Iradenizi g√º√ßlendirin',
            'Koot Hoomi': 'Kalp √ßakrasƒ± meditasyonu',
            'Djwhal Khul': '≈ûifa enerjisi g√∂nderin',
            'Serapis Bey': 'G√ºzellik kontemplasyonu',
            'Hilarion': 'Ger√ßek √ºzerine meditasyon',
            'Jesus': 'Sevgi-ƒ±≈üƒ±k meditasyonu',
            'Saint Germain': 'Mor ate≈ü g√∂rselle≈ütirmesi'
        }
        return practices.get(master, 'Sessiz meditasyon')
    
    def _master_mantra(self, master: str) -> str:
        """Usta i√ßin mantra"""
        mantras = {
            'Morya': 'Ben ƒ∞lahi ƒ∞radeyim',
            'Koot Hoomi': 'Ben Evrensel Sevgiyim',
            'Djwhal Khul': 'Ben ≈ûifayƒ±m',
            'Serapis Bey': 'Ben G√ºzelliƒüim',
            'Hilarion': 'Ben Ger√ßeƒüim',
            'Jesus': 'Ben I≈üƒ±k ve Sevgiyim',
            'Saint Germain': 'Ben Mor Ate≈üim, D√∂n√º≈ü√ºm√ºm'
        }
        return mantras.get(master, 'Om Shanti')

from PyQt6.QtWidgets import (QMainWindow, QWidget, QVBoxLayout, QHBoxLayout,
                             QTextEdit, QScrollArea, QSplitter, QFrame, 
                             QPushButton, QLabel, QStackedWidget, QToolButton)
from PyQt6.QtCore import Qt, QSize, pyqtSignal, QTimer
from PyQt6.QtGui import QFont, QTextCursor, QColor, QPalette
from qfluentwidgets import (FluentIcon, PushButton, ToolButton, 
                           isDarkTheme, setTheme, Theme)
import markdown

class ModernChatArea(QTextEdit):
    """
    Modern, geni≈ü chat alanƒ±
    OpenWebUI tarzƒ± - koyu tonlu, geni≈ü, okunabilir
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.setup_style()
    
    def setup_style(self):
        """Modern koyu tema"""
        self.setReadOnly(True)
        
        # Font
        font = QFont("Segoe UI", 11)
        font.setLetterSpacing(QFont.SpacingType.PercentageSpacing, 102)
        self.setFont(font)
        
        # Stil
        self.setStyleSheet("""
            QTextEdit {
                background-color: #1a1a1a;
                color: #e8e8e8;
                border: none;
                padding: 24px;
                line-height: 1.7;
            }
            QScrollBar:vertical {
                background-color: #1a1a1a;
                width: 12px;
                border-radius: 6px;
            }
            QScrollBar::handle:vertical {
                background-color: #3a3a3a;
                border-radius: 6px;
                min-height: 30px;
            }
            QScrollBar::handle:vertical:hover {
                background-color: #4a4a4a;
            }
            QScrollBar::add-line:vertical, QScrollBar::sub-line:vertical {
                height: 0px;
            }
        """)
    
    def add_user_message(self, text: str):
        """Kullanƒ±cƒ± mesajƒ± ekle"""
        html = f"""
        <div style="margin: 20px 0; padding: 16px 20px; 
                    background: linear-gradient(135deg, #1e40af 0%, #7c3aed 100%);
                    border-radius: 16px; max-width: 85%; margin-left: auto;
                    box-shadow: 0 4px 12px rgba(30, 64, 175, 0.3);">
            <div style="color: #ffffff; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 1.6;">
                {text}
            </div>
        </div>
        """
        self.append(html)
        self.scroll_to_bottom()
    
    def add_assistant_message(self, text: str, markdown_enabled: bool = True):
        """Asistan mesajƒ± ekle (Markdown destekli)"""
        if markdown_enabled:
            # Markdown'dan HTML'e √ßevir
            html_content = markdown.markdown(text, extensions=['fenced_code', 'tables'])
        else:
            html_content = text.replace('\n', '<br>')
        
        html = f"""
        <div style="margin: 20px 0; padding: 20px; 
                    background: linear-gradient(135deg, #1e293b 0%, #334155 100%);
                    border-radius: 16px; max-width: 90%;
                    border-left: 4px solid #3b82f6;
                    box-shadow: 0 4px 16px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4);">
            <div style="color: #e8e8e8; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 1.8;">
                {html_content}
            </div>
        </div>
        """
        self.append(html)
        self.scroll_to_bottom()
    
    def add_system_message(self, text: str):
        """Sistem mesajƒ±"""
        html = f"""
        <div style="margin: 16px 0; padding: 12px 16px;
                    background-color: #064e3b;
                    border-radius: 12px; text-align: center;
                    border: 1px solid #059669;">
            <div style="color: #6ee7b7; font-size: 10pt;">
                ‚ú® {text}
            </div>
        </div>
        """
        self.append(html)
        self.scroll_to_bottom()
    
    def scroll_to_bottom(self):
        """En alta kaydƒ±r"""
        QTimer.singleShot(100, lambda: self.verticalScrollBar().setValue(
            self.verticalScrollBar().maximum()
        ))

class ModernInputArea(QFrame):
    """
    Modern, geni≈ü input alanƒ±
    """
    
    send_clicked = pyqtSignal(str)
    
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.setup_ui()
    
    def setup_ui(self):
        layout = QVBoxLayout(self)
        layout.setContentsMargins(0, 0, 0, 0)
        layout.setSpacing(0)
        
        # Input container
        input_container = QFrame()
        input_container.setStyleSheet("""
            QFrame {
                background-color: #262626;
                border-radius: 16px;
                border: 2px solid #3a3a3a;
            }
            QFrame:focus-within {
                border: 2px solid #3b82f6;
            }
        """)
        
        container_layout = QHBoxLayout(input_container)
        container_layout.setContentsMargins(16, 12, 16, 12)
        container_layout.setSpacing(12)
        
        # Text input
        self.input_field = QTextEdit()
        self.input_field.setPlaceholderText("Sorunuzu buraya yazƒ±n... (Ctrl+Enter ile g√∂nderin)")
        self.input_field.setMaximumHeight(150)
        self.input_field.setMinimumHeight(56)
        
        # Font
        font = QFont("Segoe UI", 11)
        self.input_field.setFont(font)
        
        self.input_field.setStyleSheet("""
            QTextEdit {
                background-color: transparent;
                color: #e8e8e8;
                border: none;
                padding: 8px;
            }
        """)
        
        # Send button
        self.send_btn = QPushButton("G√∂nder")
        self.send_btn.setFixedSize(100, 48)
        self.send_btn.setCursor(Qt.CursorShape.PointingHandCursor)
        self.send_btn.setStyleSheet("""
            QPushButton {
                background: qlineargradient(x1:0, y1:0, x2:1, y2:0,
                    stop:0 #3b82f6, stop:1 #8b5cf6);
                color: white;
                border: none;
                border-radius: 12px;
                font-size: 11pt;
                font-weight: 600;
            }
            QPushButton:hover {
                background: qlineargradient(x1:0, y1:0, x2:1, y2:0,
                    stop:0 #2563eb, stop:1 #7c3aed);
            }
            QPushButton:pressed {
                background: qlineargradient(x1:0, y1:0, x2:1, y2:0,
                    stop:0 #1d4ed8, stop:1 #6d28d9);
            }
        """)
        self.send_btn.clicked.connect(self.on_send)
        
        container_layout.addWidget(self.input_field, 1)
        container_layout.addWidget(self.send_btn)
        
        layout.addWidget(input_container)
        
        # Keyboard shortcut
        self.input_field.installEventFilter(self)
    
    def eventFilter(self, obj, event):
        """Ctrl+Enter ile g√∂nder"""
        if obj == self.input_field and event.type() == event.Type.KeyPress:
            if event.key() == Qt.Key.Key_Return and event.modifiers() == Qt.KeyboardModifier.ControlModifier:
                self.on_send()
                return True
        return super().eventFilter(obj, event)
    
    def on_send(self):
        """Mesaj g√∂nder"""
        text = self.input_field.toPlainText().strip()
        if text:
            self.send_clicked.emit(text)
            self.input_field.clear()

    def _create_category_card(self, category: dict) -> QFrame:
        """Kategori kartƒ± olu≈ütur"""

            btn.clicked.connect(
                lambda checked, cat=category['name'], feat=feature: 
                self.feature_selected.emit(cat, {'feature': feat})
            )
            layout.addWidget(btn)
        
        return card

class EsotericMainWindow(QMainWindow):
    """
    Ana pencere - OpenWebUI tarzƒ± modern, koyu, geni≈ü
    """
    
    def __init__(self, engines_dict):
        super().__init__()
        
        # Motorlar
        self.engines = engines_dict
        
        # Pencere ayarlarƒ±
        self.setWindowTitle("üîÆ Ezoterik ƒ∞limler Platformu - Kuran Merkezli")
        self.setMinimumSize(1400, 900)
        
        self.setup_ui()
    
    def setup_ui(self):
        """UI kur"""
        # Ana widget
        central = QWidget()
        self.setCentralWidget(central)
        
        # Ana layout - Horizontal split
        main_layout = QHBoxLayout(central)
        main_layout.setContentsMargins(0, 0, 0, 0)
        main_layout.setSpacing(0)
        
        # Sol: Chat alanƒ± (gen≈ü)
        chat_container = QFrame()
        chat_container.setStyleSheet("""
            QFrame {
                background-color: #1a1a1a;
            }
        """)
        
        chat_layout = QVBoxLayout(chat_container)
        chat_layout.setContentsMargins(0, 0, 0, 0)
        chat_layout.setSpacing(0)
        
        # Chat area
        self.chat_area = ModernChatArea()
        chat_layout.addWidget(self.chat_area, 1)
        
        # Input area
        self.input_area = ModernInputArea()
        self.input_area.send_clicked.connect(self.on_message_send)
        
        input_wrapper = QWidget()
        input_wrapper.setStyleSheet("background-color: #0f0f0f; padding: 16px;")
        input_wrapper_layout = QVBoxLayout(input_wrapper)
        input_wrapper_layout.addWidget(self.input_area)
        
        chat_layout.addWidget(input_wrapper)
        
        # Saƒü: Panel (sabit geni≈ülik)
        self.side_panel = SidePanel()
        self.side_panel.setFixedWidth(350)
        self.side_panel.feature_selected.connect(self.on_feature_selected)
        
        # Ana layout'a ekle
        main_layout.addWidget(chat_container, 1)  # Geni≈üleyen
        main_layout.addWidget(self.side_panel)    # Sabit
        
        # Ana pencere stili
        self.setStyleSheet("""
            QMainWindow {
                background-color: #0f0f0f;
            }
        """)
        
        # Ho≈ügeldin mesajƒ±
        self.chat_area.add_system_message("Ezoterik ƒ∞limler Platformu'na ho≈ü geldiniz!")
        self.chat_area.add_assistant_message("""
# üïå Kuran Merkezli Ezoterik ƒ∞limler Platformu

### üìö Mevcut ƒ∞limler:
- **Ebced** - Harf deƒüerleri ve sayƒ±sal analiz
- **Cifr** - Gizli anlamlar ve yorumlama
- **Vefk** - Sihirli kareler ve tƒ±lsƒ±mlar

- **Numeroloji** - Doƒüum ve isim analizi

- **Teosofi** - ƒ∞lahi hikmet ve bilin√ß

**√ñrnek sorular:**
- "ƒ∞smimin ebced deƒüeri nedir?"
- "19 sistemi nedir?"
- "Karma analizi yap"
        """)
    
    def on_message_send(self, text: str):
        """Mesaj g√∂nderildiƒüinde"""
        # Kullanƒ±cƒ± mesajƒ±nƒ± g√∂ster
        self.chat_area.add_user_message(text)
        
        # ƒ∞≈üle ve cevap ver
        response = self.process_query(text)
        self.chat_area.add_assistant_message(response)
    
    def process_query(self, query: str) -> str:
        """Sorguyu i≈üle"""
        query_lower = query.lower()
        
        # Basit keyword matching
        if 'ebced' in query_lower or 'harf deƒüer' in query_lower:
            return "Ebced hesaplamasƒ± i√ßin saƒü panelden **Ebced ‚Üí Kelime Hesapla** se√ßeneƒüini kullanƒ±n."
        
        elif '19' in query_lower or 'on dokuz' in query_lower:
            return self._explain_19_system()
        
        elif 'teosofi' in query_lower or 'bilin√ß' in query_lower:
            return "Teosofi analizi i√ßin saƒü panelden **Teosofi ‚Üí Bilin√ß Analizi** se√ßin."
        
        else:
            return f"""
Sorunuz alƒ±ndƒ±: "{query}"

L√ºtfen saƒüdaki panelden ilgili ilmi se√ßin veya daha spesifik bir soru sorun.

**Pop√ºler √∂zellikler:**
- Ebced hesaplama
- 19 sistemi analizi  
- ƒ∞sim numerolojisi
- Karma okuma
            """
    
    def _explain_19_system(self) -> str:
        """19 sistemi a√ßƒ±klama"""
        return """
# üìñ 19 Sistemi (Code 19)

Kuran'daki matematiksel mucizelerden biri:

### ‚ú® Temel Olgular:
1. **Besmele:** 19 harften olu≈üur
2. **Sure sayƒ±sƒ±:** 114 = 19 √ó 6
3. **M√ºddessir 30:** "√úzerinde 19 var" ayeti
4. **ƒ∞lk vahiy:** 19 kelime (Alak 1-5)

### üî¢ Matematiksel √ñzellikler:
- 19 asal bir sayƒ±dƒ±r
- Kuran yapƒ±sƒ±nda sistematik tekrar eder
- Bir√ßok kelime 19'un katƒ± kadar ge√ßer

Detaylƒ± analiz i√ßin: **Kuran Numerolojisi ‚Üí 19 Sistemi**
        """
    
    def on_feature_selected(self, category: str, params: dict):
        """√ñzellik se√ßildiƒüinde"""
        feature = params.get('feature', '')
        
        self.chat_area.add_system_message(f"{category} - {feature} se√ßildi")
        
        # √ñzelliƒüe g√∂re dialog a√ß veya i≈ülem yap
        # Bu kƒ±sƒ±m her √∂zellik i√ßin ayrƒ± implement edilmeli
        
        response = f"**{feature}** √∂zelliƒüi hen√ºz aktif deƒüil. Yakƒ±nda eklenecek!"
        self.chat_area.add_assistant_message(response)
```



Artƒ±k tam bir **Ezoterik ƒ∞limler Platformunuz** var:
