## üíé **√ñNCELƒ∞KLƒ∞ MOD√úLLER (Detaylƒ± Kod)**

### 1Ô∏è‚É£ **EBCED HESAPLAYICISI**

```python name=core/ebced_calculator.py
from typing import Dict, List, Tuple
import json
from pathlib import Path

class EbcedCalculator:
    """
    Ebced (Abjad) hesaplama sistemi
    Arap√ßa harflerin sayƒ±sal deƒüerlerini hesaplar
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        # Ebced tablosu
        self.ebced_table = {
            # Birler (1-9)
            'ÿß': 1, 'ÿ£': 1, 'ÿ•': 1, 'ÿ¢': 1,  # Elif
            'ÿ®': 2,   # Be
            'ÿ¨': 3,   # Cim
            'ÿØ': 4,   # Dal
            'Ÿá': 5,   # He
            'Ÿà': 6,   # Vav
            'ÿ≤': 7,   # Ze
            'ÿ≠': 8,   # Ha
            'ÿ∑': 9,   # Tƒ±
            
            # Onlar (10-90)
            'Ÿä': 10, '€å': 10,  # Ye
            'ŸÉ': 20, '⁄©': 20,  # Kef
            'ŸÑ': 30,  # Lam
            'ŸÖ': 40,  # Mim
            'ŸÜ': 50,  # Nun
            'ÿ≥': 60,  # Sin
            'ÿπ': 70,  # Ayn
            'ŸÅ': 80,  # Fe
            'ÿµ': 90,  # Sad
            
            # Y√ºzler (100-900)
            'ŸÇ': 100,  # Kaf
            'ÿ±': 200,  # Re
            'ÿ¥': 300,  # ≈ûƒ±n
            'ÿ™': 400,  # Te
            'ÿ´': 500,  # Se
            'ÿÆ': 600,  # Hƒ±
            'ÿ∞': 700,  # Zel
            'ÿ∂': 800,  # Dad
            'ÿ∏': 900,  # Zƒ±
            'ÿ∫': 1000, # ƒûayn
            
            # Diƒüer karakterler
            ' ': 0,
            '.': 0,
            ',': 0,
        }
        
        # Ters √ßevrilmi≈ü tablo (sayƒ±dan harfe)
        self.reverse_table = {v: k for k, v in self.ebced_table.items() if v > 0}
        
        # Allah'ƒ±n 99 ismi ve ebced deƒüerleri
        self.esma_ul_husna = self._load_esma()
    
    def _load_esma(self) -> Dict:
        """Allah'ƒ±n 99 ismini y√ºkle"""
        esma = {
            'ÿßŸÑÿ±ÿ≠ŸÖŸÜ': {'latin': 'Er-Rahman', 'meaning': 'Rahmeti sonsuz olan'},
            'ÿßŸÑÿ±ÿ≠ŸäŸÖ': {'latin': 'Er-Rahim', 'meaning': 'Merhametli olan'},
            'ÿßŸÑŸÖŸÑŸÉ': {'latin': 'El-Melik', 'meaning': 'Malik olan'},
            # ... t√ºm 99 isim
        }
        
        # Her ismin ebced deƒüerini hesapla
        for arabic_name in esma:
            esma[arabic_name]['ebced'] = self.calculate(arabic_name)
        
        return esma
    
    def calculate(self, text: str) -> int:
        """
        Metinin ebced deƒüerini hesapla
        
        Args:
            text: Arap√ßa metin
        
        Returns:
            Toplam ebced deƒüeri
        """
        total = 0
        
        for char in text:
            value = self.ebced_table.get(char, 0)
            total += value
        
        return total
    
    def calculate_detailed(self, text: str) -> Dict:
        """
        Detaylƒ± ebced analizi
        
        Returns:
            {
                'text': 'ÿ®ÿ≥ŸÖ ÿßŸÑŸÑŸá',
                'total': 102,
                'breakdown': [('ÿ®', 2), ('ÿ≥', 60), ...],
                'digit_sum': 3,  # 102 -> 1+0+2 = 3
                'properties': {...}
            }
        """
        breakdown = []
        total = 0
        
        for char in text:
            value = self.ebced_table.get(char, 0)
            if value > 0:
                breakdown.append((char, value))
                total += value
        
        # Rakam toplamƒ± (digit root)
        digit_sum = self._calculate_digit_root(total)
        
        # Sayƒ±sal √∂zellikler
        properties = self._analyze_number(total)
        
        return {
            'text': text,
            'total': total,
            'breakdown': breakdown,
            'digit_sum': digit_sum,
            'properties': properties,
            'interpretations': self._get_interpretations(total, digit_sum)
        }
    
    def _calculate_digit_root(self, number: int) -> int:
        """Rakam k√∂k√º hesapla (1-9 arasƒ±)"""
        while number > 9:
            number = sum(int(digit) for digit in str(number))
        return number
    
    def _analyze_number(self, number: int) -> Dict:
        """Sayƒ±nƒ±n √∂zelliklerini analiz et"""
        return {
            'is_prime': self._is_prime(number),
            'is_perfect': self._is_perfect(number),
            'divisors': self._get_divisors(number),
            'prime_factors': self._prime_factorization(number)
        }
    
    def _is_prime(self, n: int) -> bool:
        """Asal sayƒ± kontrol√º"""
        if n < 2:
            return False
        for i in range(2, int(n ** 0.5) + 1):
            if n % i == 0:
                return False
        return True
    
    def _is_perfect(self, n: int) -> bool:
        """M√ºkemmel sayƒ± kontrol√º (b√∂lenler toplamƒ± = sayƒ±)"""
        if n < 2:
            return False
        divisors = [i for i in range(1, n) if n % i == 0]
        return sum(divisors) == n
    
    def _get_divisors(self, n: int) -> List[int]:
        """B√∂lenleri bul"""
        divisors = []
        for i in range(1, n + 1):
            if n % i == 0:
                divisors.append(i)
        return divisors
    
    def _prime_factorization(self, n: int) -> List[int]:
        """Asal √ßarpanlar"""
        factors = []
        d = 2
        while d * d <= n:
            while n % d == 0:
                factors.append(d)
                n //= d
            d += 1
        if n > 1:
            factors.append(n)
        return factors
    
    def _get_interpretations(self, total: int, digit_sum: int) -> Dict:
        """
        Sayƒ±larƒ±n ezoterik yorumlarƒ±
        """
        interpretations = {
            1: 'Birlik, Tevhid, Ba≈ülangƒ±√ß',
            2: 'ƒ∞kili, Denge, Zƒ±tlƒ±k',
            3: '√ú√ßl√º, M√ºkemmellik, Tamamlƒ±k',
            4: 'D√∂rt y√∂n, ƒ∞stikrar, D√ºnya',
            5: 'Be≈ü duygu, ƒ∞nsan, Merkez',
            6: 'Yaratƒ±lƒ±≈ü, Altƒ± g√ºn',
            7: 'Kutsal sayƒ±, Yedi g√∂k, Yedi yer',
            8: 'Sonsuzluk, Cennet kapƒ±larƒ±',
            9: 'Son, Tamamlanma, Olgunluk'
        }
        
        return {
            'digit_interpretation': interpretations.get(digit_sum, '√ñzel anlam'),
            'total_interpretation': self._interpret_large_number(total),
            'quranic_connection': self._find_quran_connection(total)
        }
    
    def _interpret_large_number(self, n: int) -> str:
        """B√ºy√ºk sayƒ±larƒ±n yorumu"""
        special_numbers = {
            19: 'Kuran\'ƒ±n mucize sayƒ±sƒ±',
            99: 'Esma-√ºl H√ºsna (Allah\'ƒ±n 99 ismi)',
            114: 'Kuran\'daki sure sayƒ±sƒ±',
            6236: 'Kuran\'daki ayet sayƒ±sƒ±',
            786: 'Besmele\'nin ebced deƒüeri',
            66: 'Allah lafzƒ±nƒ±n ebced deƒüeri'
        }
        
        return special_numbers.get(n, f'{n} sayƒ±sƒ±nƒ±n √∂zel anlamƒ± ara≈ütƒ±rƒ±lmalƒ±')
    
    def _find_quran_connection(self, number: int) -> str:
        """Sayƒ±nƒ±n Kuran'la ili≈ükisi"""
        # Sure veya ayet numarasƒ± olabilir mi?
        if 1 <= number <= 114:
            return f'Bu sayƒ± bir sure numarasƒ± olabilir: {number}. sure'
        elif number <= 286:  # En uzun sure (Bakara)
            return f'Bu sayƒ± bir ayet numarasƒ± olabilir'
        else:
            return 'Kuran\'da bu sayƒ±ya kar≈üƒ±lƒ±k gelen √∂zel bir yer ara≈ütƒ±rƒ±lmalƒ±dƒ±r'
    
    def find_words_by_value(self, target_value: int, word_list: List[str]) -> List[str]:
        """
        Belirli ebced deƒüerine sahip kelimeleri bul
        """
        matching_words = []
        
        for word in word_list:
            if self.calculate(word) == target_value:
                matching_words.append(word)
        
        return matching_words
    
    def compare_texts(self, text1: str, text2: str) -> Dict:
        """
        ƒ∞ki metnin ebced deƒüerlerini kar≈üƒ±la≈ütƒ±r
        """
        value1 = self.calculate(text1)
        value2 = self.calculate(text2)
        
        return {
            'text1': {'text': text1, 'value': value1},
            'text2': {'text': text2, 'value': value2},
            'difference': abs(value1 - value2),
            'ratio': value1 / value2 if value2 != 0 else None,
            'are_equal': value1 == value2,
            'interpretation': self._interpret_comparison(value1, value2)
        }
    
    def _interpret_comparison(self, v1: int, v2: int) -> str:
        """ƒ∞ki deƒüerin kar≈üƒ±la≈ütƒ±rmasƒ±"""
        if v1 == v2:
            return 'ƒ∞ki metin aynƒ± ebced deƒüerine sahip - derin bir baƒülantƒ± var'
        elif abs(v1 - v2) <= 10:
            return 'Deƒüerler √ßok yakƒ±n - benzer titre≈üim'
        else:
            return 'Farklƒ± deƒüerler - farklƒ± anlamlar'
    
    def calculate_name_compatibility(self, name1: str, name2: str) -> Dict:
        """
        ƒ∞ki ismin uyumunu hesapla (Numeroloji)
        """
        v1 = self.calculate(name1)
        v2 = self.calculate(name2)
        
        # Rakam k√∂kleri
        root1 = self._calculate_digit_root(v1)
        root2 = self._calculate_digit_root(v2)
        
        # Uyum skoru (1-10)
        compatibility_score = 10 - abs(root1 - root2)
        
        return {
            'name1': name1,
            'name2': name2,
            'value1': v1,
            'value2': v2,
            'root1': root1,
            'root2': root2,
            'compatibility_score': compatibility_score,
            'interpretation': self._interpret_compatibility(compatibility_score)
        }
    
    def _interpret_compatibility(self, score: int) -> str:
        """Uyum yorumu"""
        if score >= 9:
            return 'M√ºkemmel uyum - √ßok uyumlu'
        elif score >= 7:
            return 'ƒ∞yi uyum - uyumlu'
        elif score >= 5:
            return 'Orta uyum - dengeli'
        else:
            return 'Zayƒ±f uyum - tamamlayƒ±cƒ± olabilir'
```

# üîÆ EZOTERƒ∞K ƒ∞Lƒ∞MLER PLATFORMU (Devam)

## 2Ô∏è‚É£ **Cƒ∞FR ƒ∞LMƒ∞ MOTORU**

```python name=core/cifr_engine.py
from typing import Dict, List, Tuple, Optional
from datetime import datetime
import json
from pathlib import Path

class CifrEngine:
    """
    ƒ∞lm-i Cifr (Cifr ƒ∞lmi) Motoru
    Harflerin gizli anlamlarƒ± ve gelecek yorumlarƒ±
    """
    
    def __init__(self, ebced_calculator):
        self.ebced = ebced_calculator
        
        # Cifr t√ºrleri
        self.cifr_types = {
            'kebir': 'Cifr-i Kebir (B√ºy√ºk Cifr)',
            'sagir': 'Cifr-i Sagir (K√º√ß√ºk Cifr)',
            'cami': 'Cifr-i Cami (Kapsamlƒ± Cifr)',
            'mufassal': 'Cifr-i Mufassal (Detaylƒ± Cifr)'
        }
        
        # Huruf kategorileri
        self.huruf_categories = self._initialize_huruf_categories()
        
        # Bur√ßlar ve harf ili≈ükileri
        self.zodiac_letters = self._initialize_zodiac_mapping()
        
        # Elementler (4 element)
        self.elements = self._initialize_elements()
        
        # Vakitler ve harfler
        self.time_letters = self._initialize_time_mapping()
    
    def _initialize_huruf_categories(self) -> Dict:
        """Harflerin kategorileri"""
        return {
            'nurlu': {
                'letters': ['ÿß', 'Ÿá', 'ÿ∑', 'ŸÖ', 'ŸÅ', 'ÿ¥', 'ÿ∞'],
                'meaning': 'Nurlu/I≈üƒ±klƒ± harfler - Hayƒ±r, bereket',
                'properties': 'Pozitif enerji, aydƒ±nlƒ±k'
            },
            'karanlƒ±k': {
                'letters': ['ÿ®', 'Ÿà', '€å', 'ŸÜ', 'ÿµ', 'ÿ™', 'ÿ∂'],
                'meaning': 'Zulmet/Karanlƒ±k harfler - Gizem, sƒ±r',
                'properties': 'Gizli g√º√ß, derin bilgi'
            },
            'm√º≈üterek': {
                'letters': ['ÿ¨', 'ÿ≤', '⁄©', 'ÿ≥', 'ŸÇ', 'ÿ´', 'ÿ∏'],
                'meaning': 'Ortak harfler - Denge',
                'properties': 'Hem aydƒ±nlƒ±k hem karanlƒ±k'
            },
            'm√ºtevassƒ±t': {
                'letters': ['ÿØ', 'ÿ≠', 'ŸÑ', 'ÿπ', 'ÿ±', 'ÿÆ', 'ÿ∫'],
                'meaning': 'Orta harfler - Ge√ßi≈ü',
                'properties': 'D√∂n√º≈ü√ºm, deƒüi≈üim'
            }
        }
    
    def _initialize_zodiac_mapping(self) -> Dict:
        """Bur√ßlar ve harf ili≈ükileri"""
        return {
            'Ko√ß': {'letters': ['ÿß', 'Ÿá'], 'element': 'Ate≈ü', 'planet': 'Mars'},
            'Boƒüa': {'letters': ['ÿ®', 'Ÿà'], 'element': 'Toprak', 'planet': 'Ven√ºs'},
            'ƒ∞kizler': {'letters': ['ÿ¨', 'ÿ≤'], 'element': 'Hava', 'planet': 'Merk√ºr'},
            'Yenge√ß': {'letters': ['ÿØ', 'ÿ≠'], 'element': 'Su', 'planet': 'Ay'},
            'Aslan': {'letters': ['Ÿá', 'ÿ∑'], 'element': 'Ate≈ü', 'planet': 'G√ºne≈ü'},
            'Ba≈üak': {'letters': ['€å', '⁄©'], 'element': 'Toprak', 'planet': 'Merk√ºr'},
            'Terazi': {'letters': ['ŸÑ', 'ŸÖ'], 'element': 'Hava', 'planet': 'Ven√ºs'},
            'Akrep': {'letters': ['ŸÜ', 'ÿ≥'], 'element': 'Su', 'planet': 'Pl√ºton'},
            'Yay': {'letters': ['ÿπ', 'ŸÅ'], 'element': 'Ate≈ü', 'planet': 'J√ºpiter'},
            'Oƒülak': {'letters': ['ÿµ', 'ŸÇ'], 'element': 'Toprak', 'planet': 'Sat√ºrn'},
            'Kova': {'letters': ['ÿ±', 'ÿ¥'], 'element': 'Hava', 'planet': 'Uran√ºs'},
            'Balƒ±k': {'letters': ['ÿ™', 'ÿ´'], 'element': 'Su', 'planet': 'Nept√ºn'}
        }
    
    def _initialize_elements(self) -> Dict:
        """4 Element ve harfler"""
        return {
            'Ate≈ü': {
                'letters': ['ÿß', 'Ÿá', 'ÿ∑', 'ŸÖ', 'ŸÅ', 'ÿ¥', 'ÿ∞'],
                'properties': 'G√º√ß, cesaret, liderlik, hƒ±z',
                'color': 'Kƒ±rmƒ±zƒ±',
                'season': 'Yaz',
                'temperament': 'Safra (Kolerik)'
            },
            'Su': {
                'letters': ['ÿ®', 'Ÿà', '€å', 'ŸÜ', 'ÿµ', 'ÿ™', 'ÿ∂'],
                'properties': 'Duygu, sezgi, akƒ±≈ü, uyum',
                'color': 'Mavi',
                'season': 'Kƒ±≈ü',
                'temperament': 'Balgam (Flegmatik)'
            },
            'Hava': {
                'letters': ['ÿ¨', 'ÿ≤', '⁄©', 'ÿ≥', 'ŸÇ', 'ÿ´', 'ÿ∏'],
                'properties': 'Akƒ±l, ileti≈üim, √∂zg√ºrl√ºk',
                'color': 'Sarƒ±',
                'season': 'ƒ∞lkbahar',
                'temperament': 'Kan (Sanguine)'
            },
            'Toprak': {
                'letters': ['ÿØ', 'ÿ≠', 'ŸÑ', 'ÿπ', 'ÿ±', 'ÿÆ', 'ÿ∫'],
                'properties': 'ƒ∞stikrar, pratiklik, madde',
                'color': 'Ye≈üil/Kahverengi',
                'season': 'Sonbahar',
                'temperament': 'Sevda (Melankolik)'
            }
        }
    
    def _initialize_time_mapping(self) -> Dict:
        """Vakit ve harf ili≈ükileri"""
        return {
            'Fecir': ['ÿß', 'ÿ®', 'ÿ¨', 'ÿØ'],
            'G√ºn': ['Ÿá', 'Ÿà', 'ÿ≤', 'ÿ≠'],
            '√ñƒüle': ['ÿ∑', '€å', '⁄©', 'ŸÑ'],
            'ƒ∞kindi': ['ŸÖ', 'ŸÜ', 'ÿ≥', 'ÿπ'],
            'Ak≈üam': ['ŸÅ', 'ÿµ', 'ŸÇ', 'ÿ±'],
            'Gece': ['ÿ¥', 'ÿ™', 'ÿ´', 'ÿÆ'],
            'Gece Yarƒ±sƒ±': ['ÿ∞', 'ÿ∂', 'ÿ∏', 'ÿ∫']
        }
    
    def analyze_text(self, text: str, cifr_type: str = 'kebir') -> Dict:
        """
        Metni Cifr ilmi ile analiz et
        
        Args:
            text: Arap√ßa metin (isim, ayet, kelime)
            cifr_type: 'kebir', 'sagir', 'cami', 'mufassal'
        """
        # Ebced hesapla
        ebced_result = self.ebced.calculate_detailed(text)
        
        # Harf analizi
        letter_analysis = self._analyze_letters(text)
        
        # Element analizi
        element_analysis = self._analyze_elements(text)
        
        # Bur√ß ili≈ükisi
        zodiac_analysis = self._analyze_zodiac(text)
        
        # Numerolojik analiz
        numerology = self._numerology_analysis(ebced_result['total'])
        
        # Zaman analizi
        time_analysis = self._analyze_time_correlation(text)
        
        # Yorumlama
        interpretation = self._generate_cifr_interpretation(
            text, ebced_result, letter_analysis, element_analysis
        )
        
        return {
            'text': text,
            'cifr_type': self.cifr_types[cifr_type],
            'ebced': ebced_result,
            'letter_analysis': letter_analysis,
            'element_analysis': element_analysis,
            'zodiac_analysis': zodiac_analysis,
            'numerology': numerology,
            'time_analysis': time_analysis,
            'interpretation': interpretation,
            'predictions': self._generate_predictions(ebced_result['total'])
        }
    
    def _analyze_letters(self, text: str) -> Dict:
        """Harflerin kategori analizi"""
        categories = {
            'nurlu': 0,
            'karanlƒ±k': 0,
            'm√º≈üterek': 0,
            'm√ºtevassƒ±t': 0
        }
        
        letter_details = []
        
        for char in text:
            if char in [' ', '.', ',']:
                continue
                
            for category, data in self.huruf_categories.items():
                if char in data['letters']:
                    categories[category] += 1
                    letter_details.append({
                        'letter': char,
                        'category': category,
                        'meaning': data['meaning']
                    })
                    break
        
        # Dominant kategori
        dominant = max(categories, key=categories.get)
        
        return {
            'categories': categories,
            'letter_details': letter_details,
            'dominant_category': dominant,
            'dominant_meaning': self.huruf_categories[dominant]['meaning'],
            'balance': self._calculate_balance(categories)
        }
    
    def _calculate_balance(self, categories: Dict) -> str:
        """Harf dengesi"""
        total = sum(categories.values())
        if total == 0:
            return 'Analiz edilemedi'
        
        nurlu_ratio = categories['nurlu'] / total
        
        if nurlu_ratio > 0.6:
            return 'G√º√ßl√º pozitif enerji - Hayƒ±rlƒ±'
        elif nurlu_ratio > 0.4:
            return 'Dengeli enerji - Uyumlu'
        else:
            return 'Derin sƒ±rlar - Gizli g√º√ß'
    
    def _analyze_elements(self, text: str) -> Dict:
        """Element analizi"""
        element_count = {
            'Ate≈ü': 0,
            'Su': 0,
            'Hava': 0,
            'Toprak': 0
        }
        
        for char in text:
            for element, data in self.elements.items():
                if char in data['letters']:
                    element_count[element] += 1
                    break
        
        dominant_element = max(element_count, key=element_count.get)
        
        return {
            'element_distribution': element_count,
            'dominant_element': dominant_element,
            'element_properties': self.elements[dominant_element]['properties'],
            'temperament': self.elements[dominant_element]['temperament'],
            'season': self.elements[dominant_element]['season'],
            'interpretation': self._interpret_element(dominant_element, element_count)
        }
    
    def _interpret_element(self, dominant: str, distribution: Dict) -> str:
        """Element yorumu"""
        total = sum(distribution.values())
        dominant_ratio = distribution[dominant] / total if total > 0 else 0
        
        if dominant_ratio > 0.5:
            return f'{dominant} elementi baskƒ±n - {self.elements[dominant]["properties"]}'
        else:
            return 'Elementler dengeli - √ßok y√∂nl√º yapƒ±'
    
    def _analyze_zodiac(self, text: str) -> Dict:
        """Bur√ß analizi"""
        zodiac_count = {sign: 0 for sign in self.zodiac_letters.keys()}
        
        for char in text:
            for sign, data in self.zodiac_letters.items():
                if char in data['letters']:
                    zodiac_count[sign] += 1
        
        # En g√º√ßl√º bur√ß
        strongest_sign = max(zodiac_count, key=zodiac_count.get)
        
        return {
            'zodiac_distribution': zodiac_count,
            'strongest_sign': strongest_sign,
            'ruling_planet': self.zodiac_letters[strongest_sign]['planet'],
            'element': self.zodiac_letters[strongest_sign]['element'],
            'interpretation': f'{strongest_sign} burcu etkisi g√º√ßl√º'
        }
    
    def _numerology_analysis(self, number: int) -> Dict:
        """Numerolojik analiz"""
        # Master sayƒ±lar
        master_numbers = [11, 22, 33, 44, 55, 66, 77, 88, 99]
        
        # Rakam k√∂k√º
        digit_root = self.ebced._calculate_digit_root(number)
        
        # √ñzel sayƒ±lar
        special_meanings = {
            1: 'Liderlik, ba≈ülangƒ±√ß, baƒüƒ±msƒ±zlƒ±k',
            2: 'ƒ∞≈übirliƒüi, denge, hassasiyet',
            3: 'Yaratƒ±cƒ±lƒ±k, ileti≈üim, ne≈üe',
            4: 'ƒ∞stikrar, d√ºzen, pratiklik',
            5: '√ñzg√ºrl√ºk, deƒüi≈üim, macera',
            6: 'A≈ük, sorumluluk, uyum',
            7: 'Bilgelik, ruhaniyet, i√ßg√∂r√º',
            8: 'G√º√ß, ba≈üarƒ±, bolluk',
            9: 'Evrensellik, tamamlanma, fedakarlƒ±k'
        }
        
        is_master = number in master_numbers
        
        return {
            'number': number,
            'digit_root': digit_root,
            'is_master_number': is_master,
            'meaning': special_meanings.get(digit_root, '√ñzel anlam'),
            'master_interpretation': self._master_number_meaning(number) if is_master else None,
            'life_path_insights': self._life_path_interpretation(digit_root)
        }
    
    def _master_number_meaning(self, number: int) -> str:
        """Master sayƒ± anlamlarƒ±"""
        master_meanings = {
            11: 'Ruhani Aydƒ±nlanma - Sezgi ve i√ßg√∂r√º',
            22: 'Usta ƒ∞n≈üaat√ßƒ± - B√ºy√ºk i≈üler ba≈üarma',
            33: 'Usta √ñƒüretmen - ƒ∞nsanlƒ±ƒüa hizmet',
            44: 'Usta Healcƒ± - ≈ûifa ve d√∂n√º≈ü√ºm',
            99: 'Evrensel A≈ük - ƒ∞nsanlƒ±k sevgisi'
        }
        return master_meanings.get(number, 'G√º√ßl√º master enerji')
    
    def _life_path_interpretation(self, root: int) -> str:
        """Hayat yolu yorumu"""
        interpretations = {
            1: '√ñnc√º ruh - Liderlik ve baƒüƒ±msƒ±zlƒ±k pe≈üinde',
            2: 'Barƒ±≈ü el√ßisi - Denge ve uyum arayan',
            3: 'ƒ∞fade sanat√ßƒ±sƒ± - Yaratƒ±cƒ± ve sosyal',
            4: 'Yapƒ±cƒ± - ƒ∞stikrar ve g√ºven in≈üa eden',
            5: '√ñzg√ºr ruh - Deƒüi≈üim ve macera seven',
            6: '≈ûefkatli kalp - Sorumluluk ve sevgi dolu',
            7: 'Ger√ßek arayan - Bilgelik ve ruhaniyet yolunda',
            8: 'G√º√ß odaƒüƒ± - Ba≈üarƒ± ve bolluk √ßeken',
            9: 'ƒ∞nsancƒ±l - Evrensel sevgi ve hizmet'
        }
        return interpretations.get(root, '√ñzel yol')
    
    def _analyze_time_correlation(self, text: str) -> Dict:
        """Zaman ili≈ükisi analizi"""
        time_score = {time_period: 0 for time_period in self.time_letters.keys()}
        
        for char in text:
            for period, letters in self.time_letters.items():
                if char in letters:
                    time_score[period] += 1
        
        best_time = max(time_score, key=time_score.get)
        
        return {
            'time_distribution': time_score,
            'most_auspicious_time': best_time,
            'recommendation': f'{best_time} vakti bu kelime/isim i√ßin en uygundur'
        }
    
    def _generate_cifr_interpretation(self, text: str, ebced: Dict, 
                                     letters: Dict, elements: Dict) -> str:
        """Kapsamlƒ± Cifr yorumu olu≈ütur"""
        interpretation = f"""
üîÆ **Cƒ∞FR ƒ∞LMƒ∞ YORUMU: {text}**

üìä **Ebced Deƒüeri:** {ebced['total']}
üî¢ **Rakam K√∂k√º:** {ebced['digit_sum']}

üåü **Harf Analizi:**
- Dominant Kategori: {letters['dominant_category']}
- {letters['dominant_meaning']}
- Enerji Dengesi: {letters['balance']}

üî• **Element Analizi:**
- Baskƒ±n Element: {elements['dominant_element']}
- √ñzellikler: {elements['element_properties']}
- Miza√ß: {elements['temperament']}

üí´ **Genel Yorum:**
Bu isim/kelime {letters['dominant_category']} harflere sahip olup, 
{elements['dominant_element']} elementinin etkisi altƒ±ndadƒ±r. 
Ebced deƒüeri {ebced['total']} olan bu yapƒ±, {ebced['interpretations']['digit_interpretation']} 
√∂zelliƒüi ta≈üƒ±r.

{elements['interpretation']}
"""
        return interpretation
    
    def _generate_predictions(self, ebced_value: int) -> List[str]:
        """
        Basit tahminler/yorumlar
        (Ger√ßek Cifr tahminleri √ßok daha karma≈üƒ±ktƒ±r)
        """
        predictions = []
        
        # Sayƒ± analizi bazlƒ±
        if ebced_value % 7 == 0:
            predictions.append('üåô Bu sayƒ± 7\'nin katƒ± - manevi g√º√ß g√∂stergesi')
        
        if ebced_value % 19 == 0:
            predictions.append('‚ú® 19 sistemi uyumu - Kurani baƒülantƒ±')
        
        if self.ebced._is_prime(ebced_value):
            predictions.append('‚≠ê Asal sayƒ± - benzersiz ve g√º√ßl√º enerji')
        
        # Genel yorumlar
        if ebced_value < 100:
            predictions.append('üìâ D√º≈ü√ºk deƒüer - ba≈ülangƒ±√ß enerjisi, sadelik')
        elif ebced_value < 500:
            predictions.append('‚û°Ô∏è Orta deƒüer - dengeli, uyumlu yapƒ±')
        else:
            predictions.append('üìà Y√ºksek deƒüer - g√º√ßl√º, etkili enerji')
        
        return predictions
    
    def date_analysis(self, date: datetime) -> Dict:
        """
        Tarih analizi (Cifr ile tarih yorumlama)
        """
        # Tarihi sayƒ±lara √ßevir
        day = date.day
        month = date.month
        year = date.year
        
        # Toplam
        total = day + month + year
        
        # Rakam k√∂k√º
        digit_root = self.ebced._calculate_digit_root(total)
        
        # Hicri tarih ile ili≈üki (yakla≈üƒ±k)
        hijri_year = year - 579  # Basit yakla≈üƒ±m
        
        return {
            'gregorian_date': date.strftime('%d.%m.%Y'),
            'day': day,
            'month': month,
            'year': year,
            'total': total,
            'digit_root': digit_root,
            'hijri_year_approx': hijri_year,
            'interpretation': self._interpret_date(digit_root),
            'auspicious_activities': self._suggest_activities(digit_root)
        }
    
    def _interpret_date(self, root: int) -> str:
        """Tarih yorumu"""
        date_meanings = {
            1: 'Yeni ba≈ülangƒ±√ßlar i√ßin ideal',
            2: 'ƒ∞≈übirliƒüi ve diplomasi g√ºn√º',
            3: 'Yaratƒ±cƒ±lƒ±k ve ileti≈üim g√ºn√º',
            4: 'Pratik i≈üler i√ßin uygun',
            5: 'Deƒüi≈üim ve √∂zg√ºrl√ºk g√ºn√º',
            6: 'Aile ve sorumluluk g√ºn√º',
            7: 'Ruhani √ßalƒ±≈ümalar i√ßin ideal',
            8: 'ƒ∞≈ü ve ba≈üarƒ± g√ºn√º',
            9: 'Tamamlama ve baƒüƒ±≈ü g√ºn√º'
        }
        return date_meanings.get(root, '√ñzel g√ºn')
    
    def _suggest_activities(self, root: int) -> List[str]:
        """G√ºn√ºn uygun aktiviteleri"""
        activities = {
            1: ['Yeni projelere ba≈ülama', 'Liderlik alma', 'Baƒüƒ±msƒ±z √ßalƒ±≈üma'],
            2: ['ƒ∞≈übirliƒüi', 'Diplomasi', 'ƒ∞li≈üki geli≈ütirme'],
            3: ['Yaratƒ±cƒ± √ßalƒ±≈ümalar', 'ƒ∞leti≈üim', 'Sosyal aktiviteler'],
            4: ['Organizasyon', 'ƒ∞n≈üa etme', 'Pratik i≈üler'],
            5: ['Seyahat', 'Deƒüi≈üim', 'Yeni deneyimler'],
            6: ['Aile zamanƒ±', 'Sorumluluk alma', 'Yardƒ±m etme'],
            7: ['Meditasyon', '√ñƒürenme', 'Ruhani pratikler'],
            8: ['ƒ∞≈ü geli≈ütirme', 'Finans', 'Hedef belirleme'],
            9: ['Tamamlama', 'Baƒüƒ±≈ü', 'Affetme']
        }
        return activities.get(root, ['Genel aktiviteler'])
    
    def predict_future_event(self, text: str, target_year: int) -> Dict:
        """
        Gelecek tahmini (Cifr y√∂ntemi ile - sembolik)
        ‚ö†Ô∏è Bu sadece geleneksel y√∂ntem g√∂sterimidir
        """
        # Metni analiz et
        analysis = self.analyze_text(text)
        ebced_value = analysis['ebced']['total']
        
        # Hedef yƒ±l ile ili≈ükilendir
        year_cycle = target_year % 12  # 12 yƒ±l d√∂ng√ºs√º
        combined_value = ebced_value + target_year
        
        # Tahmin kategorileri
        prediction_categories = {
            1: 'Yeni ba≈ülangƒ±√ßlar',
            2: 'ƒ∞≈übirlikleri',
            3: 'ƒ∞leti≈üim artƒ±≈üƒ±',
            4: 'ƒ∞stikrar d√∂nemi',
            5: 'Deƒüi≈üimler',
            6: 'Sorumluluklar',
            7: 'Ruhani geli≈üim',
            8: 'Maddi geli≈üim',
            9: 'Tamamlanma',
            10: 'D√∂n√º≈ü√ºm',
            11: 'Aydƒ±nlanma',
            12: 'D√∂ng√º sonu'
        }
        
        prediction_type = prediction_categories.get(year_cycle, '√ñzel d√∂nem')
        
        return {
            'text': text,
            'target_year': target_year,
            'ebced_value': ebced_value,
            'year_cycle': year_cycle,
            'combined_value': combined_value,
            'prediction_type': prediction_type,
            'interpretation': self._generate_future_interpretation(
                text, target_year, year_cycle, ebced_value
            ),
            'advice': self._generate_advice(year_cycle),
            'disclaimer': '‚ö†Ô∏è Bu tahminler geleneksel Cifr y√∂ntemlerine dayanƒ±r ve semboliktir.'
        }
    
    def _generate_future_interpretation(self, text: str, year: int, 
                                       cycle: int, ebced: int) -> str:
        """Gelecek yorumu"""
        return f"""
üìÖ {year} yƒ±lƒ± i√ßin {text} analizi:

üîÆ Yƒ±l D√∂ng√ºs√º: {cycle}/12
üìä Ebced Deƒüeri: {ebced}

{self._get_cycle_meaning(cycle)}

Bu d√∂nemde {text} ile ilgili konular √∂ne √ßƒ±kabilir.
"""
    
    def _get_cycle_meaning(self, cycle: int) -> str:
        """D√∂ng√º anlamƒ±"""
        meanings = {
            1: 'Yeni ba≈ülangƒ±√ßlar d√∂nemi - √ñnc√º olmak',
            2: 'ƒ∞≈übirliƒüi ve ortaklƒ±klar d√∂nemi',
            3: 'ƒ∞leti≈üim ve yaratƒ±cƒ±lƒ±k d√∂nemi',
            4: 'Temel atma ve istikrar d√∂nemi',
            5: '√ñzg√ºrl√ºk ve deƒüi≈üim d√∂nemi',
            6: 'Sorumluluk ve hizmet d√∂nemi',
            7: 'ƒ∞√ße d√∂n√ºk ve ruhani d√∂nem',
            8: 'Ba≈üarƒ± ve maddi kazan√ß d√∂nemi',
            9: 'Tamamlama ve bƒ±rakma d√∂nemi',
            10: 'D√∂n√º≈ü√ºm ve yenilenme',
            11: 'Ruhani aydƒ±nlanma',
            12: 'D√∂ng√º sonu ve hazƒ±rlƒ±k'
        }
        return meanings.get(cycle, '√ñzel d√∂nem')
    
    def _generate_advice(self, cycle: int) -> List[str]:
        """Tavsiyeler"""
        advice_map = {
            1: ['Cesur olun', 'ƒ∞nisiyatif alƒ±n', 'Yeni projeler ba≈ülatƒ±n'],
            2: ['ƒ∞≈übirliƒüi yapƒ±n', 'Sabƒ±rlƒ± olun', 'Dinleyin'],
            3: ['ƒ∞leti≈üim kurun', 'Yaratƒ±cƒ± olun', 'Payla≈üƒ±n'],
            4: ['Planlƒ± √ßalƒ±≈üƒ±n', 'Sabƒ±rlƒ± olun', 'Temel atƒ±n'],
            5: ['Esnek olun', 'Deƒüi≈üime a√ßƒ±k olun', 'Macera edin'],
            6: ['Sorumluluk alƒ±n', 'Yardƒ±m edin', 'Dengeli olun'],
            7: ['ƒ∞√ße d√∂n√ºn', '√ñƒürenin', 'Meditasyon yapƒ±n'],
            8: ['Odaklanƒ±n', 'Organize olun', 'Hedeflerinizi takip edin'],
            9: ['Bƒ±rakƒ±n', 'Affedƒ±n', 'Tamamlayƒ±n']
        }
        return advice_map.get(cycle, ['Sezgilerinizi takip edin'])
```

## 3Ô∏è‚É£ **VEFK (TALISMATIK KARE) OLU≈ûTURUCU**

```python name=core/vefk_generator.py
import numpy as np
from typing import List, Dict, Tuple
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
from matplotlib.patches import Rectangle
import io
from PIL import Image

class VefkGenerator:
    """
    Vefk (Tƒ±lsƒ±mlƒ± Kare) Olu≈üturucu
    Sayƒ±sal kareler ve kutsal isimler ile vefk yapma
    """
    
    def __init__(self, ebced_calculator):
        self.ebced = ebced_calculator
        
        # Vefk t√ºrleri
        self.vefk_types = {
            'adadi': 'Sayƒ±sal Vefk (Sihirli Kareler)',
            'harfi': 'Harfli Vefk (Kutsal ƒ∞simler)',
            'muhtelif': 'Karma Vefk'
        }
        
        # Esma-√ºl H√ºsna i√ßin vefk ≈üablonlarƒ±
        self.esma_vefk_templates = self._load_esma_templates()
    
    def _load_esma_templates(self) -> Dict:
        """Esma-√ºl H√ºsna vefk ≈üablonlarƒ±"""
        return {
            'Allah': {
                'ebced': 66,
                'size': 3,
                'purpose': 'Genel bereket ve koruma'
            },
            'Er-Rahman': {
                'ebced': 298,
                'size': 4,
                'purpose': 'Merhamet √ßekme'
            },
            'El-Aziz': {
                'ebced': 94,
                'size': 3,
                'purpose': 'G√º√ß ve izzet'
            }
            # ... daha fazla isim
        }
    
    def create_magic_square(self, n: int) -> np.ndarray:
        """
        Sihirli kare olu≈ütur (n x n)
        
        Magic Square: Her satƒ±r, s√ºtun ve √ßapraz toplamƒ± e≈üit
        
        Args:
            n: Karenin boyutu (3, 4, 5, ...)
        """
        if n % 2 == 1:  # Tek sayƒ±lar i√ßin
            return self._odd_magic_square(n)
        elif n % 4 == 0:  # 4'√ºn katlarƒ± i√ßin
            return self._doubly_even_magic_square(n)
        else:  # Diƒüerleri i√ßin (4k+2)
            return self._singly_even_magic_square(n)
    
    def _odd_magic_square(self, n: int) -> np.ndarray:
        """Tek boyutlu sihirli kare (Siamese y√∂ntemi)"""
        square = np.zeros((n, n), dtype=int)
        
        # Ba≈ülangƒ±√ß pozisyonu: √ºst orta
        i, j = 0, n // 2
        
        for num in range(1, n * n + 1):
            square[i][j] = num
            
            # Sonraki pozisyon: yukarƒ± ve saƒüa
            new_i = (i - 1) % n
            new_j = (j + 1) % n
            
            # Eƒüer dolu ise, bir a≈üaƒüƒ± git
            if square[new_i][new_j] != 0:
                new_i = (i + 1) % n
                new_j = j
            
            i, j = new_i, new_j
        
        return square
    
    def _doubly_even_magic_square(self, n: int) -> np.ndarray:
        """4'√ºn katƒ± boyutlu sihirli kare"""
        square = np.arange(1, n * n + 1).reshape(n, n)
        
        # √áaprazlarƒ± tersine √ßevir
        for i in range(n):
            for j in range(n):
                if (i % 4 == j % 4) or ((i % 4) + (j % 4) == 3):
                    square[i][j] = n * n + 1 - square[i][j]
        
        return square
    
    def _singly_even_magic_square(self, n: int) -> np.ndarray:
        """4k+2 boyutlu sihirli kare (karma≈üƒ±k algoritma)"""
        # Basit versiyon - tam algoritma √ßok karma≈üƒ±k
        k = n // 2
        odd_square = self._odd_magic_square(k)
        
        # 4 kadrana b√∂l ve doldur
        square = np.zeros((n, n), dtype=int)
        
        # √úst sol
        square[0:k, 0:k] = odd_square
        # √úst saƒü
        square[0:k, k:n] = odd_square + k * k
        # Alt sol
        square[k:n, 0:k] = odd_square + 2 * k * k
        # Alt saƒü
        square[k:n, k:n] = odd_square + 3 * k * k
        
        return square
    
    def create_ebced_vefk(self, name: str, size: int = None) -> Dict:
        """
        ƒ∞sim/kelime i√ßin ebced bazlƒ± vefk olu≈ütur
        
        Args:
            name: Arap√ßa isim/kelime
            size: Karenin boyutu (None ise otomatik)
        """
        # Ebced deƒüerini hesapla
        ebced_value = self.ebced.calculate(name)
        
        # Boyut belirle
        if size is None:
            size = self._determine_vefk_size(ebced_value)
        
        # Sihirli kare olu≈ütur
        magic_square = self.create_magic_square(size)
        
        # Sihirli sabit
        magic_constant = size * (size * size + 1) // 2
        
        # Ebced ile sihirli kareyi √∂l√ßeklendir
        scaled_square = self._scale_square_to_ebced(magic_square, ebced_value)
        
        return {
            'name': name,
            'ebced_value': ebced_value,
            'size': size,
            'magic_constant': magic_constant,
            'original_square': magic_square.tolist(),
            'scaled_square': scaled_square.tolist(),
            'properties': self._analyze_vefk(scaled_square),
            'visualization': self._visualize_vefk(scaled_square, name)
        }
    
    def _determine_vefk_size(self, ebced: int) -> int:
        """Ebced deƒüerine g√∂re vefk boyutu belirle"""
        if ebced < 50:
            return 3
        elif ebced < 150:
            return 4
        elif ebced < 300:
            return 5
        elif ebced < 500:
            return 6
        else:
            return 7
    
    def _scale_square_to_ebced(self, square: np.ndarray, ebced: int) -> np.ndarray:
        """
        Sihirli kareyi ebced deƒüerine g√∂re √∂l√ßeklendir
        """
        n = square.shape[0]
        magic_constant = n * (n * n + 1) // 2
        
        # √ñl√ßek fakt√∂r√º
        scale_factor = ebced / magic_constant
        
        # √ñl√ßeklendir ve yuvarla
        scaled = np.round(square * scale_factor).astype(int)
        
        return scaled
    
    def _analyze_vefk(self, square: np.ndarray) -> Dict:
        """Vefk √∂zelliklerini analiz et"""
        n = square.shape[0]
        
        # Satƒ±r toplamlarƒ±
        row_sums = square.sum(axis=1).tolist()
        
        # S√ºtun toplamlarƒ±
        col_sums = square.sum(axis=0).tolist()
        
        # √áapraz toplamlar
        diag1_sum = np.trace(square)
        diag2_sum = np.trace(np.fliplr(square))
        
        # T√ºm toplamlar e≈üit mi?
        all_sums = row_sums + col_sums + [diag1_sum, diag2_sum]
        is_magic = len(set(all_sums)) == 1
        
        # Merkez deƒüer (tek boyutlar i√ßin)
        center_value = None
        if n % 2 == 1:
            center_value = int(square[n//2, n//2])
        
        return {
            'size': n,
            'row_sums': row_sums,
            'col_sums': col_sums,
            'diagonal_sums': [int(diag1_sum), int(diag2_sum)],
            'is_magic_square': is_magic,
            'magic_constant': int(all_sums[0]) if is_magic else None,
            'center_value': center_value,
            'total_sum': int(square.sum())
        }
    
    def _visualize_vefk(self, square: np.ndarray, title: str) -> str:
        """
        Vefk'i g√∂rselle≈ütir
        
        Returns:
            Base64 encoded image string
        """
        n = square.shape[0]
        
        fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(8, 8))
        ax.set_xlim(0, n)
        ax.set_ylim(0, n)
        ax.set_aspect('equal')
        
        # Ba≈ülƒ±k
        ax.set_title(f'Vefk: {title}', fontsize=16, fontweight='bold', pad=20)
        
        # Kareleri √ßiz
        for i in range(n):
            for j in range(n):
                # Kare
                rect = Rectangle((j, n-1-i), 1, 1, 
                                linewidth=2, edgecolor='black', facecolor='lightyellow')
                ax.add_patch(rect)
                
                # Sayƒ±
                ax.text(j + 0.5, n-1-i + 0.5, str(square[i, j]),
                       ha='center', va='center', fontsize=20, fontweight='bold')
        
        # Eksenleri kaldƒ±r
        ax.set_xticks([])
        ax.set_yticks([])
        ax.spines['top'].set_visible(False)
        ax.spines['right'].set_visible(False)
        ax.spines['bottom'].set_visible(False)
        ax.spines['left'].set_visible(False)
        
        # G√∂rselibytearray olarak kaydet
        buf = io.BytesIO()
        plt.savefig(buf, format='png', dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')
        buf.seek(0)
        plt.close()
        
        # PIL Image'e √ßevir
        img = Image.open(buf)
        
        # Base64'e √ßevir (isteƒüe baƒülƒ±)
        import base64
        buf.seek(0)
        img_base64 = base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode()
        
        return img_base64
    
    def create_esma_vefk(self, esma_name: str) -> Dict:
        """
        Esma-√ºl H√ºsna i√ßin √∂zel vefk
        """
        if esma_name not in self.esma_vefk_templates:
            return {'error': f'{esma_name} i√ßin ≈üablon bulunamadƒ±'}
        
        template = self.esma_vefk_templates[esma_name]
        
        # Vefk olu≈ütur
        vefk = self.create_ebced_vefk(esma_name, template['size'])
        
        # Ek bilgiler ekle
        vefk['purpose'] = template['purpose']
        vefk['esma_meaning'] = f'Allah\'ƒ±n "{esma_name}" ismi'
        vefk['usage'] = self._get_esma_usage(esma_name)
        
        return vefk
    
    def _get_esma_usage(self, esma_name: str) -> str:
        """Esma kullanƒ±m tavsiyeleri"""
        usage_guide = {
            'Allah': 'Genel dua ve zikirlerde, koruma i√ßin',
            'Er-Rahman': 'Merhamet dilemek, ≈üefkat √ßekmek i√ßin',
            'El-Aziz': 'G√º√ß ve izzet kazanmak i√ßin'
        }
        return usage_guide.get(esma_name, '√ñzel ama√ßlar i√ßin')
    
    def create_planetary_vefk(self, planet: str) -> Dict:
        """
        Gezegen vefkleri (klasik yƒ±ldƒ±z falƒ± vefkleri)
        """
        planetary_data = {
            'Sat√ºrn': {'size': 3, 'magic_constant': 15, 'day': 'Cumartesi'},
            'J√ºpiter': {'size': 4, 'magic_constant': 34, 'day': 'Per≈üembe'},
            'Mars': {'size': 5, 'magic_constant': 65, 'day': 'Salƒ±'},
            'G√ºne≈ü': {'size': 6, 'magic_constant': 111, 'day': 'Pazar'},
            'Ven√ºs': {'size': 7, 'magic_constant': 175, 'day': 'Cuma'},
            'Merk√ºr': {'size': 8, 'magic_constant': 260, 'day': '√áar≈üamba'},
            'Ay': {'size': 9, 'magic_constant': 369, 'day': 'Pazartesi'}
        }
        
        if planet not in planetary_data:
            return {'error': 'Ge√ßersiz gezegen'}
        
        data = planetary_data[planet]
        size = data['size']
        
        # Sihirli kare olu≈ütur
        square = self.create_magic_square(size)
        
        return {
            'planet': planet,
            'size': size,
            'magic_constant': data['magic_constant'],
            'auspicious_day': data['day'],
            'square': square.tolist(),
            'properties': self._analyze_vefk(square),
            'visualization': self._visualize_vefk(square, f'{planet} Vefki'),
            'interpretation': self._interpret_planetary_vefk(planet)
        }
    
    def _interpret_planetary_vefk(self, planet: str) -> str:
        """Gezegen vefki yorumu"""
        interpretations = {
            'Sat√ºrn': 'Disiplin, yapƒ±, sorumluluk i√ßin',
            'J√ºpiter': 'Bolluk, geni≈üleme, ≈üans i√ßin',
            'Mars': 'G√º√ß, cesaret, enerji i√ßin',
            'G√ºne≈ü': 'Liderlik, ba≈üarƒ±, tanƒ±nma i√ßin',
            'Ven√ºs': 'A≈ük, g√ºzellik, uyum i√ßin',
            'Merk√ºr': 'ƒ∞leti≈üim, zeka, ticaret i√ßin',
            'Ay': 'Duygular, sezgi, kadƒ±nlƒ±k i√ßin'
        }
        return interpretations.get(planet, '√ñzel ama√ßlar i√ßin')
```

# üîÆ EZOTERƒ∞K ƒ∞Lƒ∞MLER PLATFORMU (Devam - 4)

            },
            9: {

    def _initialize_72_names(self) -> Dict:
        """72 Kutsal ƒ∞sim (Exodus 14:19-21'den t√ºretilmi≈ü)"""
        # Basitle≈ütirilmi≈ü versiyon - ger√ßek liste √ßok uzun

            # ... 72 tanesi var
        }
    
    def _load_sacred_words(self) -> Dict:
        """Kutsal kelimeler ve Gematria deƒüerleri"""
        return {
            '◊ê◊î◊ë◊î': {'value': 13, 'meaning': 'A≈ük (Ahavah)'},
            '◊ê◊ó◊ì': {'value': 13, 'meaning': 'Bir/Tek (Echad)'},
            '◊ô◊î◊ï◊î': {'value': 26, 'meaning': 'Tanrƒ±\'nƒ±n ismi (YHVH/Tetragrammaton)'},
            '◊ê◊ú◊î◊ô◊ù': {'value': 86, 'meaning': 'Tanrƒ± (Elohim)'},
            '◊û◊©◊ô◊ó': {'value': 358, 'meaning': 'Mesih (Mashiach)'},
            '◊©◊ò◊ü': {'value': 364, 'meaning': '≈ûeytan (Satan)'},
        }
    
    def calculate_gematria(self, hebrew_text: str, method: str = 'standard') -> Dict:
        """
        Gematria hesaplama
        
        Args:
            hebrew_text: ƒ∞branice metin
            method: 'standard', 'mispar_gadol', 'mispar_katan', 'atbash', vb.
        """
        if method == 'standard':
            value = self._standard_gematria(hebrew_text)
        elif method == 'mispar_gadol':
            value = self._mispar_gadol(hebrew_text)
        elif method == 'mispar_katan':
            value = self._mispar_katan(hebrew_text)
        elif method == 'atbash':
            return self._atbash_cipher(hebrew_text)
        elif method == 'albam':
            return self._albam_cipher(hebrew_text)
        elif method == 'avgad':
            return self._avgad_cipher(hebrew_text)
        else:
            value = self._standard_gematria(hebrew_text)
        
        # Detaylƒ± analiz
        return {
            'text': hebrew_text,
            'method': self.gematria_methods[method],
            'value': value,
            'reduced_value': self._reduce_to_single(value),
            'interpretation': self._interpret_gematria(value),
            'matching_words': self._find_matching_gematria(value),
            'sefiroth_connection': self._connect_to_sefiroth(value),
            'sacred_connections': self._check_sacred_connections(value)
        }
    
    def _standard_gematria(self, text: str) -> int:
        """Standart Gematria hesaplama"""
        total = 0
        for char in text:
            if char in self.hebrew_gematria:
                total += self.hebrew_gematria[char]
        return total
    
    def _mispar_gadol(self, text: str) -> int:
        """
        Mispar Gadol (B√ºy√ºk Gematria)
        Son harfler i√ßin √∂zel deƒüerler: ◊ö=500, ◊ù=600, ◊ü=700, ◊£=800, ◊•=900
        """
        extended_values = {
            '◊ö': 500,
            '◊ù': 600,
            '◊ü': 700,
            '◊£': 800,
            '◊•': 900
        }
        
        total = 0
        for char in text:
            if char in extended_values:
                total += extended_values[char]
            elif char in self.hebrew_gematria:
                total += self.hebrew_gematria[char]
        
        return total
    
    def _mispar_katan(self, text: str) -> int:
        """
        Mispar Katan (K√º√ß√ºk Gematria)
        Her sayƒ±yƒ± tek haneye indirge
        """
        standard_value = self._standard_gematria(text)
        return self._reduce_to_single(standard_value)
    
    def _reduce_to_single(self, number: int) -> int:
        """Sayƒ±yƒ± tek haneye indirge"""
        while number > 9:
            number = sum(int(digit) for digit in str(number))
        return number
    
    def _atbash_cipher(self, text: str) -> Dict:
        """
        Atba≈ü ≈ûifresi (Ters alfabe)
        ◊ê‚Üî◊™, ◊ë‚Üî◊©, ◊í‚Üî◊®, vb.
        """
        # ƒ∞branice alfabeyi olu≈ütur
        hebrew_alphabet = list(self.hebrew_gematria.keys())
        
        # Atba≈ü e≈üle≈ütirmesi
        atbash_map = {}
        n = len(hebrew_alphabet)
        for i, char in enumerate(hebrew_alphabet):
            atbash_map[char] = hebrew_alphabet[n - 1 - i]
        
        # Metni d√∂n√º≈üt√ºr
        transformed = ''.join(atbash_map.get(char, char) for char in text)
        
        return {
            'original': text,
            'transformed': transformed,
            'original_value': self._standard_gematria(text),
            'transformed_value': self._standard_gematria(transformed),
            'cipher_type': 'Atba≈ü'
        }
    
    def _albam_cipher(self, text: str) -> Dict:
        """
        Albam ≈ûifresi
        Alfabeyi ikiye b√∂l ve kar≈üƒ±lƒ±klƒ± e≈üle≈ütir
        """
        hebrew_alphabet = list(self.hebrew_gematria.keys())
        mid = len(hebrew_alphabet) // 2
        
        albam_map = {}
        for i in range(mid):
            albam_map[hebrew_alphabet[i]] = hebrew_alphabet[i + mid]
            albam_map[hebrew_alphabet[i + mid]] = hebrew_alphabet[i]
        
        transformed = ''.join(albam_map.get(char, char) for char in text)
        
        return {
            'original': text,
            'transformed': transformed,
            'original_value': self._standard_gematria(text),
            'transformed_value': self._standard_gematria(transformed),
            'cipher_type': 'Albam'
        }
    
    def _avgad_cipher(self, text: str) -> Dict:
        """
        Avgad ≈ûifresi (+1 kaydƒ±rma)
        ◊ê‚Üí◊ë, ◊ë‚Üí◊í, vb.
        """
        hebrew_alphabet = list(self.hebrew_gematria.keys())
        n = len(hebrew_alphabet)
        
        avgad_map = {}
        for i, char in enumerate(hebrew_alphabet):
            avgad_map[char] = hebrew_alphabet[(i + 1) % n]
        
        transformed = ''.join(avgad_map.get(char, char) for char in text)
        
        return {
            'original': text,
            'transformed': transformed,
            'original_value': self._standard_gematria(text),
            'transformed_value': self._standard_gematria(transformed),
            'cipher_type': 'Avgad'
        }
    
    def _interpret_gematria(self, value: int) -> str:
        """Gematria deƒüerini yorumla"""
        special_values = {
            13: 'A≈ük ve Birlik sayƒ±sƒ± (Ahavah ve Echad)',
            26: 'Tanrƒ±\'nƒ±n kutsal ismi (YHVH)',
            72: '72 Kutsal ƒ∞sim',
            86: 'Elohim (Tanrƒ±)',
            358: 'Mesih (Mashiach)',
            613: '613 Mitzvah (emir)',
            1000: 'M√ºkemmellik'
        }
        
        if value in special_values:
            return special_values[value]
        else:
            return f'{value} deƒüerinin √∂zel anlamƒ± ara≈ütƒ±rƒ±lmalƒ±'
    
    def _find_matching_gematria(self, value: int) -> List[Dict]:
        """Aynƒ± Gematria deƒüerine sahip kelimeleri bul"""
        matches = []
        
        for word, data in self.sacred_words.items():
            if data['value'] == value:
                matches.append({
                    'word': word,
                    'meaning': data['meaning'],
                    'value': value
                })
        
        return matches
    
    def _connect_to_sefiroth(self, value: int) -> Optional[Dict]:
        """Deƒüeri Sefiroth ile ili≈ükilendir"""
        # Basit e≈üle≈ütirme: deƒüer modulo 10
        sefira_number = (value % 10) if (value % 10) != 0 else 10
        
        sefira = self.sefiroth.get(sefira_number)
        
        if sefira:
            return {
                'sefira_number': sefira_number,
                'sefira_name': sefira['name'],
                'hebrew': sefira['hebrew'],
                'meaning': sefira['meaning'],
                'attribute': sefira['attribute'],
                'planet': sefira['planet'],
                'color': sefira['color']
            }
        
        return None
    
    def _check_sacred_connections(self, value: int) -> List[str]:
        """Kutsal sayƒ±larla baƒülantƒ±larƒ± kontrol et"""
        connections = []
        
        # 3, 7, 10, 12, 22, 40, 72 gibi kutsal sayƒ±lar
        sacred_numbers = {
            3: '√ú√ßl√º - Tanrƒ±\'nƒ±n √º√ß y√∂n√º',
            7: 'M√ºkemmellik - Yaratƒ±lƒ±≈ü',
            10: 'Sefiroth sayƒ±sƒ±',
            12: 'ƒ∞srail kabileleri',
            22: 'ƒ∞branice alfabenin harf sayƒ±sƒ±',
            40: 'Arƒ±nma d√∂nemi',
            72: 'Kutsal isimler'
        }
        
        for sacred_num, meaning in sacred_numbers.items():
            if value == sacred_num:
                connections.append(f'{value} = {meaning}')
            elif value % sacred_num == 0:
                connections.append(f'{value}, {sacred_num}\'nin katƒ± - {meaning}')
        
        return connections if connections else ['√ñzel kutsal baƒülantƒ± tespit edilemedi']
    
    def tree_of_life_reading(self, question: str = None) -> Dict:
        """
        Ya≈üam Aƒüacƒ± (Tree of Life) okuma
        10 Sefiroth √ºzerinden manevi analiz
        """
        import random
        
        # Rastgele bir Sefira se√ß (veya soru bazlƒ±)
        if question:
            # Sorunun Gematria deƒüerine g√∂re
            question_value = len(question) % 10
            selected_sefira = question_value if question_value != 0 else 10
        else:
            selected_sefira = random.randint(1, 10)
        
        sefira = self.sefiroth[selected_sefira]
        
        # Yol analizi (hangi sefiralar arasƒ±)
        paths = self._analyze_tree_paths(selected_sefira)
        
        return {
            'question': question if question else 'Genel okuma',
            'selected_sefira': sefira,
            'number': selected_sefira,
            'guidance': self._generate_sefira_guidance(sefira),
            'paths': paths,
            'meditation': self._sefira_meditation(sefira),
            'affirmation': self._sefira_affirmation(sefira)
        }
    
    def _analyze_tree_paths(self, sefira_num: int) -> Dict:
        """Ya≈üam Aƒüacƒ± yollarƒ±"""
        # 22 yol var (harflerle ili≈ükili)
        connections = {
            1: [2, 3, 6],  # Kether -> Chokmah, Binah, Tiphereth
            2: [1, 3, 4, 6],
            3: [1, 2, 5, 6],
            4: [2, 5, 6, 7],
            5: [3, 4, 6, 8],
            6: [1, 4, 5, 7, 8, 9],
            7: [4, 6, 8, 9, 10],
            8: [5, 6, 7, 9, 10],
            9: [6, 7, 8, 10],
            10: [7, 8, 9]
        }
        
        connected_sefirot = connections.get(sefira_num, [])
        
        return {
            'connected_sefirot': [
                self.sefiroth[num]['name'] for num in connected_sefirot
            ],
            'interpretation': f'Bu Sefira, {len(connected_sefirot)} diƒüer Sefira ile baƒülantƒ±lƒ±dƒ±r'
        }
    
    def _generate_sefira_guidance(self, sefira: Dict) -> str:
        """Sefira rehberliƒüi"""
        guidance_map = {
            'Kether': 'En y√ºksek bilin√ßle baƒülantƒ± kurun. ƒ∞lahi irade ile uyum saƒülayƒ±n.',
            'Chokmah': 'Bilgeliƒüinizi kullanƒ±n. Yaratƒ±cƒ± enerjinizi ortaya √ßƒ±karƒ±n.',
            'Binah': 'Derin anlayƒ±≈ü geli≈ütirin. Yapƒ± ve form verin fikirlerinize.',
            'Chesed': 'C√∂mert olun. Sevgi ve ≈üefkat g√∂sterin.',
            'Geburah': 'Disiplinli olun. Gerektiƒüinde sƒ±nƒ±rlar koyun.',
            'Tiphereth': 'Dengeyi bulun. ƒ∞√ß g√ºzelliƒüinizi ortaya √ßƒ±karƒ±n.',
            'Netzach': 'Dayanƒ±klƒ± olun. Duygusal zekanƒ±zƒ± kullanƒ±n.',
            'Hod': 'Mantƒ±ƒüƒ±nƒ±zƒ± kullanƒ±n. Net ileti≈üim kurun.',
            'Yesod': 'Temellerinizi g√º√ßlendirin. Bilin√ßaltƒ±nƒ±zla √ßalƒ±≈üƒ±n.',
            'Malkuth': 'Fiziksel d√ºnyada tezah√ºr ettirin. Topraklƒ± olun.'
        }
        
        return guidance_map.get(sefira['name'], 'Manevi geli≈üiminize odaklanƒ±n')
    
    def _sefira_meditation(self, sefira: Dict) -> str:
        """Sefira meditasyon √∂nerisi"""
        return f"{sefira['color']} rengini g√∂rselle≈ütirin. {sefira['attribute']} √ºzerine meditasyon yapƒ±n."
    
    def _sefira_affirmation(self, sefira: Dict) -> str:
        """Sefira olumlamasƒ±"""
        affirmations = {
            'Kether': 'Ben ilahi iradenin bir par√ßasƒ±yƒ±m',
            'Chokmah': 'Ben saf bilgeliƒüim',
            'Binah': 'Ben derin anlayƒ±≈üƒ±m',
            'Chesed': 'Ben sƒ±nƒ±rsƒ±z sevgiyim',
            'Geburah': 'Ben disiplinli g√ºc√ºm',
            'Tiphereth': 'Ben dengeli g√ºzelliƒüim',
            'Netzach': 'Ben dayanƒ±klƒ± zaferim',
            'Hod': 'Ben parlak ihti≈üamƒ±m',
            'Yesod': 'Ben saƒülam temelem',
            'Malkuth': 'Ben tezah√ºr eden krallƒ±ƒüƒ±m'
        }
        
        return affirmations.get(sefira['name'], 'Ben ƒ±≈üƒ±ƒüƒ±m')
    
    def compare_with_quran(self, hebrew_text: str, arabic_text: str) -> Dict:
        """
        Kabala (ƒ∞branice) ve Kuran (Arap√ßa) kar≈üƒ±la≈ütƒ±rmasƒ±
        """
        # Gematria hesapla
        hebrew_value = self._standard_gematria(hebrew_text)
        
        # Ebced hesapla (Arap√ßa i√ßin - dƒ±≈üarƒ±dan ebced_calculator gerekli)
        # Bu fonksiyon ana uygulamada ebced calculator ile birle≈ütirilmeli
        
        return {
            'hebrew_text': hebrew_text,
            'hebrew_gematria': hebrew_value,
            'arabic_text': arabic_text,
            'comparison': 'Her iki gelenekte de sayƒ±sal mistisizm √∂nemli rol oynar',
            'similarities': [
                'Her iki sistem de harflere sayƒ±sal deƒüerler atar',
                'Kutsal metinlerde gizli anlamlar aranƒ±r',
                'Sayƒ±larƒ±n manevi √∂nemi vurgulanƒ±r'
            ],
            'differences': [
                'ƒ∞branice 22 harf, Arap√ßa 28 harf',
                'Farklƒ± deƒüer sistemleri',
                'Farklƒ± kutsal sayƒ±lar (Kabala: 10,22,72 | ƒ∞slam: 7,19,99)'
            ]
        }
```

## 5Ô∏è‚É£ **ƒ∞SLAMƒ∞ NUMEROLOJƒ∞ MOTORU**

        }
        
        # ƒ∞slamƒ± a√ßƒ±dan √∂zel sayƒ±lar
        self.islamic_sacred_numbers = {
            7: 'Yedi g√∂k, yedi yer',
            19: 'Kuran mucizesi',
            99: 'Esma-√ºl H√ºsna',
            313: 'Bedir Gazvesi m√ºcahit sayƒ±sƒ±',
            1000: 'Kadir Gecesi deƒüeri',
            786: 'Besmele ebced deƒüeri'

    def birth_chart_analysis(self, birth_date: datetime, name: str) -> Dict:
        """
        Doƒüum tarihi ve isim bazlƒ± tam numeroloji analizi
        
        Args:
            birth_date: Doƒüum tarihi
            name: Arap√ßa isim
        """
        # Tarih analizi
        day = birth_date.day
        month = birth_date.month
        year = birth_date.year
        
        # Ana sayƒ±lar
        life_path = self._calculate_life_path(birth_date)
        destiny = self._calculate_destiny(name)
        soul_urge = self._calculate_soul_urge(name)
        personality = self._calculate_personality(name)
        maturity = self._calculate_maturity(life_path, destiny)
        
        # Doƒüum g√ºn√º sayƒ±sƒ±
        birth_day_number = self._reduce_number(day)
        
        # Yƒ±l d√∂ng√ºs√º
        personal_year = self._calculate_personal_year(birth_date, datetime.now().year)
        
        return {
            'birth_date': birth_date.strftime('%d.%m.%Y'),
            'name': name,
            'life_path_number': life_path,
            'destiny_number': destiny,
            'soul_urge_number': soul_urge,
            'personality_number': personality,
            'maturity_number': maturity,
            'birth_day_number': birth_day_number,
            'personal_year': personal_year,
            'interpretations': {
                'life_path': self._interpret_number(life_path['final']),
                'destiny': self._interpret_number(destiny['final']),
                'soul_urge': self._interpret_number(soul_urge['final']),
                'personality': self._interpret_number(personality['final'])
            },
            'compatibility': self._calculate_compatibility_factors(life_path['final'], destiny['final']),
            'strengths': self._identify_strengths(life_path['final'], destiny['final']),
            'challenges': self._identify_challenges(life_path['final'], destiny['final']),
            'islamic_perspective': self._islamic_interpretation(life_path['final'])
        }
    
    def _calculate_life_path(self, birth_date: datetime) -> Dict:
        """
        Hayat Yolu Sayƒ±sƒ± (Life Path Number)
        En √∂nemli sayƒ± - ki≈üinin hayattaki amacƒ±
        """
        day = birth_date.day
        month = birth_date.month
        year = birth_date.year
        
        # Her birimi ayrƒ± ayrƒ± indirge
        day_reduced = self._reduce_number(day)
        month_reduced = self._reduce_number(month)
        year_reduced = self._reduce_number(year)
        
        # Topla ve tekrar indirge
        total = day_reduced + month_reduced + year_reduced
        final = self._reduce_number(total)
        
        return {
            'day': day,
            'month': month,
            'year': year,
            'day_reduced': day_reduced,
            'month_reduced': month_reduced,
            'year_reduced': year_reduced,
            'total': total,
            'final': final,
            'calculation': f'{day} -> {day_reduced} + {month} -> {month_reduced} + {year} -> {year_reduced} = {final}'
        }
    
    def _calculate_destiny(self, name: str) -> Dict:
        """
        Kader Sayƒ±sƒ± (Destiny Number)
        ƒ∞smin ebced deƒüerinden
        """
        ebced_value = self.ebced.calculate(name)
        reduced = self._reduce_number(ebced_value)
        
        return {
            'name': name,
            'ebced_value': ebced_value,
            'final': reduced,
            'calculation': f'{name} = {ebced_value} -> {reduced}'
        }
    
    def _calculate_soul_urge(self, name: str) -> Dict:
        """
        Ruh Arzusu Sayƒ±sƒ± (Soul Urge Number)
        Sadece sesli harfler (basitle≈ütirilmi≈ü)
        """
        # Arap√ßa'da sesli harfler: ÿß Ÿà €å
        vowels = ['ÿß', 'Ÿà', '€å']
        
        vowel_value = 0
        vowel_letters = []
        
        for char in name:
            if char in vowels:
                vowel_letters.append(char)
                vowel_value += self.ebced.ebced_table.get(char, 0)
        
        reduced = self._reduce_number(vowel_value)
        
        return {
            'vowels': ''.join(vowel_letters),
            'vowel_value': vowel_value,
            'final': reduced,
            'meaning': 'ƒ∞√ß motivasyon ve arzular'
        }
    
    def _calculate_personality(self, name: str) -> Dict:
        """
        Ki≈üilik Sayƒ±sƒ± (Personality Number)
        Sadece sessiz harfler
        """
        vowels = ['ÿß', 'Ÿà', '€å']
        
        consonant_value = 0
        consonant_letters = []
        
        for char in name:
            if char not in vowels and char in self.ebced.ebced_table:
                consonant_letters.append(char)
                consonant_value += self.ebced.ebced_table[char]
        
        reduced = self._reduce_number(consonant_value)
        
        return {
            'consonants': ''.join(consonant_letters),
            'consonant_value': consonant_value,
            'final': reduced,
            'meaning': 'Dƒ±≈ü ki≈üilik ve imaj'
        }
    
    def _calculate_maturity(self, life_path: Dict, destiny: Dict) -> Dict:
        """
        Olgunluk Sayƒ±sƒ± (Maturity Number)
        Hayat yolu + Kader sayƒ±sƒ±
        """
        total = life_path['final'] + destiny['final']
        final = self._reduce_number(total)
        
        return {
            'life_path': life_path['final'],
            'destiny': destiny['final'],
            'total': total,
            'final': final,
            'meaning': 'Ya≈üamƒ±n ikinci yarƒ±sƒ±nda ortaya √ßƒ±kan √∂zellikler'
        }
    
    def _calculate_personal_year(self, birth_date: datetime, current_year: int) -> Dict:
        """
        Ki≈üisel Yƒ±l Sayƒ±sƒ± (Personal Year)
        Bu yƒ±lƒ±n enerjisi
        """
        day = birth_date.day
        month = birth_date.month
        
        # G√ºn + Ay + Mevcut Yƒ±l
        total = self._reduce_number(day) + self._reduce_number(month) + self._reduce_number(current_year)
        final = self._reduce_number(total)
        
        return {
            'current_year': current_year,
            'calculation': f'{day} + {month} + {current_year}',
            'final': final,
            'interpretation': self._interpret_personal_year(final)
        }
    
    def _reduce_number(self, number: int) -> int:
        """
        Sayƒ±yƒ± tek haneye indirge (Master sayƒ±lar hari√ß)
        """
        # Master sayƒ±lar: 11, 22, 33
        if number in [11, 22, 33]:
            return number
        
        while number > 9:
            number = sum(int(digit) for digit in str(number))
        
        return number
    
    def _interpret_number(self, number: int) -> Dict:
        """Sayƒ± yorumu"""
        if number in self.number_meanings:
            return self.number_meanings[number]
        elif number in self.master_numbers:
            return {
                'meaning': self.master_numbers[number],
                'attributes': ['Y√ºksek potansiyel', 'Manevi misyon'],
                'characteristics': 'G√º√ßl√º ruhani enerji'
            }
        else:
            return {'meaning': 'Bilinmeyen sayƒ±'}
    
    def _interpret_personal_year(self, number: int) -> str:
        """Ki≈üisel yƒ±l yorumu"""
        year_meanings = {
            1: 'Yeni ba≈ülangƒ±√ßlar yƒ±lƒ± - Projelere ba≈ülama zamanƒ±',
            2: 'ƒ∞≈übirliƒüi yƒ±lƒ± - ƒ∞li≈ükiler √∂nemli',
            3: 'Yaratƒ±cƒ±lƒ±k yƒ±lƒ± - Kendini ifade et',
            4: 'ƒ∞stikrar yƒ±lƒ± - Temel atma zamanƒ±',
            5: 'Deƒüi≈üim yƒ±lƒ± - √ñzg√ºrl√ºk ve macera',
            6: 'Sorumluluk yƒ±lƒ± - Aile ve ev √∂nemli',
            7: 'ƒ∞√ße d√∂n√º≈ü yƒ±lƒ± - Ruhani geli≈üim',
            8: 'Ba≈üarƒ± yƒ±lƒ± - Maddi kazan√ß',
            9: 'Tamamlama yƒ±lƒ± - Bƒ±rakma ve yeniden ba≈ülama'
        }
        
        return year_meanings.get(number, '√ñzel yƒ±l')
    
    def _calculate_compatibility_factors(self, life_path: int, destiny: int) -> Dict:
        """ƒ∞√ß uyum fakt√∂rleri"""
        harmony = 10 - abs(life_path - destiny)
        
        return {
            'harmony_score': harmony,
            'interpretation': self._interpret_harmony(harmony)
        }
    
    def _interpret_harmony(self, score: int) -> str:
        """Uyum yorumu"""
        if score >= 8:
            return 'M√ºkemmel i√ß uyum - Hayat yolu ve kader uyumlu'
        elif score >= 6:
            return 'ƒ∞yi uyum - Dengeli yapƒ±'
        elif score >= 4:
            return 'Orta uyum - Bazƒ± √ßatƒ±≈ümalar olabilir'
        else:
            return 'D√º≈ü√ºk uyum - ƒ∞√ß √ßatƒ±≈üma potansiyeli'
    
    def _identify_strengths(self, life_path: int, destiny: int) -> List[str]:
        """G√º√ßl√º y√∂nler"""
        strengths = []
        
        if life_path in self.number_meanings:
            strengths.extend(self.number_meanings[life_path]['attributes'])
        
        if destiny in self.number_meanings:
            strengths.extend(self.number_meanings[destiny]['attributes'])
        
        return list(set(strengths))  # Tekrarlarƒ± kaldƒ±r
    
    def _identify_challenges(self, life_path: int, destiny: int) -> List[str]:
        """Zorluklar/Dersler"""
        challenges = {
            1: ['Ego kontrol√º', 'Baƒüƒ±msƒ±zlƒ±k ile i≈übirliƒüi dengesi'],
            2: ['Kararsƒ±zlƒ±k', 'A≈üƒ±rƒ± hassasiyet'],
            3: ['Daƒüƒ±nƒ±klƒ±k', 'Y√ºzeysellik'],
            4: ['Katƒ±lƒ±k', 'Deƒüi≈üime diren√ß'],
            5: ['Sorumsuzluk', 'ƒ∞stikrarsƒ±zlƒ±k'],
            6: ['A≈üƒ±rƒ± sorumluluk', 'Kendini ihmal'],
            7: ['ƒ∞zolasyon', 'A≈üƒ±rƒ± analiz'],
            8: ['Materya lizmobsesyonu', 'G√º√ß hƒ±rsƒ±'],
            9: ['Kendini kaybetme', 'A≈üƒ±rƒ± fedakarlƒ±k']
        }
        
        life_challenges = challenges.get(life_path, [])
        destiny_challenges = challenges.get(destiny, [])
        
        return list(set(life_challenges + destiny_challenges))
    
    def _islamic_interpretation(self, number: int) -> str:
        """ƒ∞slami perspektif"""
        islamic_views = {
            1: 'Tevhid - Allah\'ƒ±n birliƒüi. Liderlik ve √∂nc√ºl√ºk.',
            2: 'Denge ve adalet. ƒ∞ki d√ºnya (d√ºnya-ahiret).',
            3: 'M√ºkemmellik √º√ßl√ºs√º (ƒ∞man, ƒ∞slam, ƒ∞hsan).',
            4: 'D√∂rt melek, d√∂rt kitap, d√∂rt halife.',
            5: 'Be≈ü vakit namaz. Be≈ü duygu.',
            6: 'Altƒ± g√ºn yaratƒ±lƒ±≈ü. ƒ∞manƒ±n altƒ± ≈üartƒ±.',
            7: 'Yedi g√∂k, yedi yer. Kutsal sayƒ±.',
            8: 'Cennetin sekiz kapƒ±sƒ±. Ar≈ü\'ƒ±n ta≈üƒ±yƒ±cƒ±larƒ±.',
            9: 'Tamamlanma. Son peygamber Hz. Muhammed (SAV).'
        }
        
        return islamic_views.get(number, 'Her sayƒ± Allah\'ƒ±n yaratƒ±≈üƒ±nda hikmet ta≈üƒ±r')
    
    def name_compatibility(self, name1: str, name2: str) -> Dict:
        """
        ƒ∞ki ismin uyumu
        """
        # Her iki ismin ebced ve numeroloji deƒüerleri
        destiny1 = self._calculate_destiny(name1)
        destiny2 = self._calculate_destiny(name2)
        
        # Uyum skoru
        difference = abs(destiny1['final'] - destiny2['final'])
        compatibility_score = 10 - difference
        
        return {
            'name1': name1,
            'name2': name2,
            'destiny1': destiny1['final'],
            'destiny2': destiny2['final'],
            'difference': difference,
            'compatibility_score': compatibility_score,
            'interpretation': self._interpret_name_compatibility(compatibility_score),
            'advice': self._compatibility_advice(compatibility_score)
        }
    
    def _interpret_name_compatibility(self, score: int) -> str:
        """Uyum yorumu"""
        if score >= 9:
            return 'M√ºkemmel uyum - √áok uyumlu isimler'
        elif score >= 7:
            return '√áok iyi uyum - Uyumlu'
        elif score >= 5:
            return 'ƒ∞yi uyum - Dengeli'
        elif score >= 3:
            return 'Orta uyum - Tamamlayƒ±cƒ±'
        else:
            return 'Zayƒ±f uyum - Farklƒ± enerjiler'
    
    def _compatibility_advice(self, score: int) -> str:
        """Uyum tavsiyesi"""
        if score >= 7:
            return 'Bu isimler doƒüal olarak uyumludur. ƒ∞li≈üki akƒ±cƒ± olacaktƒ±r.'
        elif score >= 5:
            return 'Dengeli bir ili≈üki. Kar≈üƒ±lƒ±klƒ± anlayƒ±≈ü √∂nemli.'
        else:
            return 'Farklƒ± enerjiler olsa da, tamamlayƒ±cƒ± olabilirsiniz. Sabƒ±r gerekli.'
```

            },
            'Amissio': {

            'Conjunctio': {
                'dots': [2, 1, 1, 1],
                'arabic': 'ÿßŸÑÿßÿ¨ÿ™ŸÖÿßÿπ',
                'meaning': 'Birle≈üim',

            'Carcer': {

                'arabic': 'ÿßŸÑÿ≥ÿ¨ŸÜ',
