## üíé Level 2 Kod ƒ∞mplementasyonu

### 1Ô∏è‚É£ `core/session_manager.py` - √áoklu Konu≈üma Oturumlarƒ±

```python name=core/session_manager.py
import json
import uuid
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime
from typing import List, Dict, Optional

class Session:
    """Tek bir konu≈üma oturumu"""
    
    def __init__(self, session_id: str = None, title: str = "Yeni Konu≈üma"):
        self.id = session_id or str(uuid.uuid4())
        self.title = title
        self.created_at = datetime.now().isoformat()
        self.updated_at = self.created_at
        self.messages: List[Dict] = []
        self.metadata: Dict = {
            'total_tokens': 0,
            'total_cost': 0.0,
            'model_used': [],
            'tags': []
        }
    
    def add_message(self, role: str, content: str, metadata: Dict = None):
        """Mesaj ekle"""
        message = {
            'role': role,
            'content': content,
            'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(),
            'metadata': metadata or {}
        }
        self.messages.append(message)
        self.updated_at = datetime.now().isoformat()
    
    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:
        """Dictionary'ye √ßevir"""
        return {
            'id': self.id,
            'title': self.title,
            'created_at': self.created_at,
            'updated_at': self.updated_at,
            'messages': self.messages,
            'metadata': self.metadata
        }
    
    @classmethod
    def from_dict(cls, data: Dict) -> 'Session':
        """Dictionary'den olu≈ütur"""
        session = cls(data['id'], data['title'])
        session.created_at = data['created_at']
        session.updated_at = data['updated_at']
        session.messages = data['messages']
        session.metadata = data['metadata']
        return session

class SessionManager:
    """Konu≈üma oturumlarƒ±nƒ± y√∂netir"""
    
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.sessions_dir = Path.home() / ".rag_chatbot" / "sessions"
        self.sessions_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        
        self.sessions: Dict[str, Session] = {}
        self.current_session: Optional[Session] = None
        
        self.load_sessions()
    
    def load_sessions(self):
        """T√ºm oturumlarƒ± y√ºkle"""
        for file_path in self.sessions_dir.glob("*.json"):
            try:
                with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                    data = json.load(f)
                    session = Session.from_dict(data)
                    self.sessions[session.id] = session
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"Session y√ºklenemedi {file_path.name}: {e}")
        
        # Eƒüer hi√ß session yoksa yeni olu≈ütur
        if not self.sessions:
            self.create_new_session()
        else:
            # En son g√ºncellenen session'ƒ± aktif yap
            latest = max(self.sessions.values(), key=lambda s: s.updated_at)
            self.current_session = latest
    
    def save_session(self, session: Session):
        """Oturumu kaydet"""
        file_path = self.sessions_dir / f"{session.id}.json"
        with open(file_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(session.to_dict(), f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
    
    def create_new_session(self, title: str = None) -> Session:
        """Yeni oturum olu≈ütur"""
        if title is None:
            title = f"Konu≈üma {len(self.sessions) + 1}"
        
        session = Session(title=title)
        self.sessions[session.id] = session
        self.current_session = session
        self.save_session(session)
        return session
    
    def get_session(self, session_id: str) -> Optional[Session]:
        """ID'ye g√∂re oturum al"""
        return self.sessions.get(session_id)
    
    def set_current_session(self, session_id: str):
        """Aktif oturumu deƒüi≈ütir"""
        session = self.get_session(session_id)
        if session:
            self.current_session = session
    
    def delete_session(self, session_id: str):
        """Oturumu sil"""
        if session_id in self.sessions:
            file_path = self.sessions_dir / f"{session_id}.json"
            if file_path.exists():
                file_path.unlink()
            
            del self.sessions[session_id]
            
            # Eƒüer aktif session silindiyse yeni olu≈ütur
            if self.current_session and self.current_session.id == session_id:
                if self.sessions:
                    self.current_session = list(self.sessions.values())[0]
                else:
                    self.create_new_session()
    
    def rename_session(self, session_id: str, new_title: str):
        """Oturumu yeniden adlandƒ±r"""
        session = self.get_session(session_id)
        if session:
            session.title = new_title
            session.updated_at = datetime.now().isoformat()
            self.save_session(session)
    
    def get_all_sessions(self) -> List[Session]:
        """T√ºm oturumlarƒ± listele (en yeniden eskiye)"""
        return sorted(
            self.sessions.values(),
            key=lambda s: s.updated_at,
            reverse=True
        )
    
    def search_sessions(self, query: str) -> List[Session]:
        """Oturumlarda arama yap"""
        results = []
        query_lower = query.lower()
        
        for session in self.sessions.values():
            # Ba≈ülƒ±kta ara
            if query_lower in session.title.lower():
                results.append(session)
                continue
            
            # Mesajlarda ara
            for message in session.messages:
                if query_lower in message['content'].lower():
                    results.append(session)
                    break
        
        return sorted(results, key=lambda s: s.updated_at, reverse=True)
    
    def export_session(self, session_id: str, format: str = 'json') -> str:
        """Oturumu dƒ±≈üa aktar"""
        session = self.get_session(session_id)
        if not session:
            raise ValueError("Session bulunamadƒ±")
        
        export_dir = Path.home() / ".rag_chatbot" / "exports"
        export_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        
        timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
        
        if format == 'json':
            file_path = export_dir / f"{session.title}_{timestamp}.json"
            with open(file_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                json.dump(session.to_dict(), f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
        
        elif format == 'txt':
            file_path = export_dir / f"{session.title}_{timestamp}.txt"
            with open(file_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                f.write(f"# {session.title}\n")
                f.write(f"Olu≈üturulma: {session.created_at}\n\n")
                
                for msg in session.messages:
                    role = "üë§ Kullanƒ±cƒ±" if msg['role'] == 'user' else "ü§ñ Asistan"
                    f.write(f"{role}:\n{msg['content']}\n\n")
        
        elif format == 'markdown':
            file_path = export_dir / f"{session.title}_{timestamp}.md"
            with open(file_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                f.write(f"# {session.title}\n\n")
                f.write(f"**Olu≈üturulma:** {session.created_at}\n\n")
                f.write("---\n\n")
                
                for msg in session.messages:
                    role = "üë§ **Kullanƒ±cƒ±**" if msg['role'] == 'user' else "ü§ñ **Asistan**"
                    f.write(f"### {role}\n\n")
                    f.write(f"{msg['content']}\n\n")
        
        return str(file_path)
```

### 2Ô∏è‚É£ `core/voice_manager.py` - Ses Giri≈üi/√áƒ±kƒ±≈üƒ±

```python name=core/voice_manager.py
import sounddevice as sd
import soundfile as sf
import numpy as np
from pathlib import Path
import tempfile
from openai import OpenAI
import pyttsx3
from PyQt6.QtCore import QThread, pyqtSignal
import queue
import threading

class VoiceRecorder(QThread):
    """Ses kaydƒ± thread'i"""
    
    recording_started = pyqtSignal()
    recording_stopped = pyqtSignal(str)  # Dosya yolu
    error_occurred = pyqtSignal(str)
    
    def __init__(self, sample_rate=16000):
        super().__init__()
        self.sample_rate = sample_rate
        self.is_recording = False
        self.audio_queue = queue.Queue()
    
    def run(self):
        """Kayƒ±t yap"""
        self.is_recording = True
        self.recording_started.emit()
        
        try:
            # Ses verilerini topla
            audio_data = []
            
            def callback(indata, frames, time, status):
                if status:
                    print(f"Recording status: {status}")
                if self.is_recording:
                    audio_data.append(indata.copy())
            
            # Kayƒ±t ba≈ülat
            with sd.InputStream(
                samplerate=self.sample_rate,
                channels=1,
                callback=callback
            ):
                while self.is_recording:
                    self.msleep(100)
            
            # Ge√ßici dosyaya kaydet
            if audio_data:
                recording = np.concatenate(audio_data, axis=0)
                
                temp_file = tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(
                    delete=False,
                    suffix='.wav'
                )
                temp_path = temp_file.name
                temp_file.close()
                
                sf.write(temp_path, recording, self.sample_rate)
                self.recording_stopped.emit(temp_path)
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.error_occurred.emit(f"Kayƒ±t hatasƒ±: {str(e)}")
    
    def stop_recording(self):
        """Kaydƒ± durdur"""
        self.is_recording = False

class VoiceManager:
    """Ses giri≈üi ve √ßƒ±kƒ±≈üƒ± y√∂netimi"""
    
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.client = OpenAI(api_key=config.get('api_key'))
        
        # TTS engine (offline)
        self.tts_engine = pyttsx3.init()
        self.tts_engine.setProperty('rate', 150)  # Konu≈üma hƒ±zƒ±
        self.tts_engine.setProperty('volume', 0.9)
        
        # T√ºrk√ße ses se√ß (varsa)
        voices = self.tts_engine.getProperty('voices')
        for voice in voices:
            if 'turkish' in voice.name.lower() or 'tr' in voice.languages:
                self.tts_engine.setProperty('voice', voice.id)
                break
        
        self.recorder: VoiceRecorder = None
    
    def start_recording(self) -> VoiceRecorder:
        """Ses kaydƒ±nƒ± ba≈ülat"""
        if self.recorder and self.recorder.isRunning():
            return self.recorder
        
        self.recorder = VoiceRecorder()
        self.recorder.start()
        return self.recorder
    
    def stop_recording(self):
        """Ses kaydƒ±nƒ± durdur"""
        if self.recorder:
            self.recorder.stop_recording()
    
    def transcribe_audio(self, audio_file_path: str) -> str:
        """Ses dosyasƒ±nƒ± metne √ßevir (Whisper API)"""
        try:
            with open(audio_file_path, 'rb') as audio_file:
                transcript = self.client.audio.transcriptions.create(
                    model="whisper-1",
                    file=audio_file,
                    language="tr"
                )
            return transcript.text
        
        except Exception as e:
            raise Exception(f"Transcription hatasƒ±: {str(e)}")
    
    def text_to_speech_openai(self, text: str, output_path: str = None):
        """Metni sese √ßevir (OpenAI TTS)"""
        if output_path is None:
            output_path = tempfile.mktemp(suffix='.mp3')
        
        try:
            response = self.client.audio.speech.create(
                model="tts-1",
                voice="alloy",  # alloy, echo, fable, onyx, nova, shimmer
                input=text
            )
            
            response.stream_to_file(output_path)
            return output_path
        
        except Exception as e:
            raise Exception(f"TTS hatasƒ±: {str(e)}")
    
    def text_to_speech_offline(self, text: str):
        """Metni sese √ßevir (Offline - pyttsx3)"""
        try:
            # Asenkron konu≈üma
            def speak():
                self.tts_engine.say(text)
                self.tts_engine.runAndWait()
            
            thread = threading.Thread(target=speak)
            thread.daemon = True
            thread.start()
        
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"TTS hatasƒ±: {e}")
    
    def play_audio(self, file_path: str):
        """Ses dosyasƒ±nƒ± √ßal"""
        try:
            data, sample_rate = sf.read(file_path)
            sd.play(data, sample_rate)
            sd.wait()
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Ses √ßalma hatasƒ±: {e}")
```

### 3Ô∏è‚É£ `core/vision_manager.py` - G√∂rsel Analizi (GPT-4 Vision)

```python name=core/vision_manager.py
from openai import OpenAI
import base64
from pathlib import Path
from PIL import Image
import io

class VisionManager:
    """G√∂rsel analizi y√∂netimi (GPT-4 Vision)"""
    
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.client = OpenAI(api_key=config.get('api_key'))
    
    def encode_image(self, image_path: str) -> str:
        """G√∂rseli base64'e √ßevir"""
        with open(image_path, 'rb') as image_file:
            return base64.b64encode(image_file.read()).decode('utf-8')
    
    def resize_image_if_needed(self, image_path: str, max_size: int = 2048) -> str:
        """G√∂rseli gerekirse k√º√ß√ºlt"""
        img = Image.open(image_path)
        
        if max(img.size) > max_size:
            # Oranƒ± koru ve k√º√ß√ºlt
            ratio = max_size / max(img.size)
            new_size = tuple(int(dim * ratio) for dim in img.size)
            img = img.resize(new_size, Image.Resampling.LANCZOS)
            
            # Ge√ßici dosyaya kaydet
            temp_path = Path(image_path).parent / f"resized_{Path(image_path).name}"
            img.save(temp_path, quality=85, optimize=True)
            return str(temp_path)
        
        return image_path
    
    def analyze_image(self, image_path: str, prompt: str = None, 
                     detail: str = "auto") -> str:
        """
        G√∂rseli analiz et
        
        Args:
            image_path: G√∂rsel dosya yolu
            prompt: Kullanƒ±cƒ± sorusu/talebi
            detail: 'low', 'high', 'auto' - Detay seviyesi
        """
        if prompt is None:
            prompt = "Bu g√∂rselde ne g√∂r√ºyorsun? Detaylƒ± a√ßƒ±kla."
        
        # G√∂rseli k√º√ß√ºlt (gerekirse)
        processed_image = self.resize_image_if_needed(image_path)
        
        # Base64'e √ßevir
        base64_image = self.encode_image(processed_image)
        
        try:
            response = self.client.chat.completions.create(
                model="gpt-4-vision-preview",
                messages=[
                    {
                        "role": "user",
                        "content": [
                            {
                                "type": "text",
                                "text": prompt
                            },
                            {
                                "type": "image_url",
                                "image_url": {
                                    "url": f"data:image/jpeg;base64,{base64_image}",
                                    "detail": detail
                                }
                            }
                        ]
                    }
                ],
                max_tokens=1000
            )
            
            return response.choices[0].message.content
        
        except Exception as e:
            raise Exception(f"Vision API hatasƒ±: {str(e)}")
    
    def analyze_multiple_images(self, image_paths: list, prompt: str = None) -> str:
        """Birden fazla g√∂rseli analiz et"""
        if prompt is None:
            prompt = "Bu g√∂rselleri kar≈üƒ±la≈ütƒ±r ve analiz et."
        
        content = [{"type": "text", "text": prompt}]
        
        for image_path in image_paths:
            processed_image = self.resize_image_if_needed(image_path)
            base64_image = self.encode_image(processed_image)
            
            content.append({
                "type": "image_url",
                "image_url": {
                    "url": f"data:image/jpeg;base64,{base64_image}",
                    "detail": "auto"
                }
            })
        
        try:
            response = self.client.chat.completions.create(
                model="gpt-4-vision-preview",
                messages=[{"role": "user", "content": content}],
                max_tokens=1500
            )
            
            return response.choices[0].message.content
        
        except Exception as e:
            raise Exception(f"Vision API hatasƒ±: {str(e)}")
```

### 4Ô∏è‚É£ `core/analytics.py` - Analitik & ƒ∞statistikler

```python name=core/analytics.py
import json
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Dict, List
import pandas as pd

class Analytics:
    """Kullanƒ±m analitiƒüi ve istatistikler"""
    
    # Token fiyatlarƒ± (USD per 1K tokens)
    TOKEN_PRICES = {
        'gpt-4-turbo-preview': {'input': 0.01, 'output': 0.03},
        'gpt-4': {'input': 0.03, 'output': 0.06},
        'gpt-3.5-turbo': {'input': 0.0005, 'output': 0.0015},
        'gpt-3.5-turbo-16k': {'input': 0.003, 'output': 0.004},
        'text-embedding-3-small': {'input': 0.00002, 'output': 0},
        'text-embedding-3-large': {'input': 0.00013, 'output': 0},
        'whisper-1': {'input': 0.006, 'output': 0},  # per minute
        'tts-1': {'input': 0.015, 'output': 0},  # per 1M characters
    }
    
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.analytics_dir = Path.home() / ".rag_chatbot" / "analytics"
        self.analytics_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        
        self.log_file = self.analytics_dir / "usage_log.jsonl"
        self.stats_file = self.analytics_dir / "statistics.json"
        
        self.stats = self.load_statistics()
    
    def load_statistics(self) -> Dict:
        """ƒ∞statistikleri y√ºkle"""
        if self.stats_file.exists():
            with open(self.stats_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                return json.load(f)
        
        return {
            'total_messages': 0,
            'total_tokens': 0,
            'total_cost': 0.0,
            'sessions_created': 0,
            'documents_added': 0,
            'voice_queries': 0,
            'image_queries': 0,
            'first_use': datetime.now().isoformat(),
            'last_use': datetime.now().isoformat(),
            'model_usage': {},
            'daily_stats': {}
        }
    
    def save_statistics(self):
        """ƒ∞statistikleri kaydet"""
        with open(self.stats_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(self.stats, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
    
    def log_usage(self, event_type: str, data: Dict):
        """Kullanƒ±m kaydƒ± ekle"""
        log_entry = {
            'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(),
            'type': event_type,
            'data': data
        }
        
        with open(self.log_file, 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            f.write(json.dumps(log_entry, ensure_ascii=False) + '\n')
    
    def record_message(self, model: str, input_tokens: int, output_tokens: int):
        """Mesaj kaydƒ±"""
        total_tokens = input_tokens + output_tokens
        
        # Maliyet hesapla
        prices = self.TOKEN_PRICES.get(model, {'input': 0, 'output': 0})
        cost = (input_tokens / 1000 * prices['input']) + \
               (output_tokens / 1000 * prices['output'])
        
        # ƒ∞statistikleri g√ºncelle
        self.stats['total_messages'] += 1
        self.stats['total_tokens'] += total_tokens
        self.stats['total_cost'] += cost
        self.stats['last_use'] = datetime.now().isoformat()
        
        # Model kullanƒ±mƒ±
        if model not in self.stats['model_usage']:
            self.stats['model_usage'][model] = {
                'count': 0,
                'tokens': 0,
                'cost': 0.0
            }
        
        self.stats['model_usage'][model]['count'] += 1
        self.stats['model_usage'][model]['tokens'] += total_tokens
        self.stats['model_usage'][model]['cost'] += cost
        
        # G√ºnl√ºk istatistik
        today = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
        if today not in self.stats['daily_stats']:
            self.stats['daily_stats'][today] = {
                'messages': 0,
                'tokens': 0,
                'cost': 0.0
            }
        
        self.stats['daily_stats'][today]['messages'] += 1
        self.stats['daily_stats'][today]['tokens'] += total_tokens
        self.stats['daily_stats'][today]['cost'] += cost
        
        # Log
        self.log_usage('message', {
            'model': model,
            'input_tokens': input_tokens,
            'output_tokens': output_tokens,
            'cost': cost
        })
        
        self.save_statistics()
    
    def record_document_upload(self, file_name: str, file_size: int, chunks: int):
        """Belge y√ºkleme kaydƒ±"""
        self.stats['documents_added'] += 1
        
        self.log_usage('document_upload', {
            'file_name': file_name,
            'file_size': file_size,
            'chunks': chunks
        })
        
        self.save_statistics()
    
    def record_voice_query(self, duration_seconds: float):
        """Ses sorgusu kaydƒ±"""
        self.stats['voice_queries'] += 1
        
        # Whisper maliyeti (dakika ba≈üƒ±na)
        cost = (duration_seconds / 60) * 0.006
        self.stats['total_cost'] += cost
        
        self.log_usage('voice_query', {
            'duration': duration_seconds,
            'cost': cost
        })
        
        self.save_statistics()
    
    def record_image_query(self, image_count: int, detail_level: str):
        """G√∂rsel sorgusu kaydƒ±"""
        self.stats['image_queries'] += 1
        
        # Vision API maliyeti (yakla≈üƒ±k)
        base_cost = 0.01 if detail_level == 'low' else 0.03
        cost = base_cost * image_count
        self.stats['total_cost'] += cost
        
        self.log_usage('image_query', {
            'image_count': image_count,
            'detail_level': detail_level,
            'cost': cost
        })
        
        self.save_statistics()
    
    def get_daily_usage(self, days: int = 30) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """Son N g√ºn√ºn kullanƒ±m verisi"""
        daily_data = []
        
        for date_str, data in self.stats['daily_stats'].items():
            daily_data.append({
                'date': date_str,
                'messages': data['messages'],
                'tokens': data['tokens'],
                'cost': data['cost']
            })
        
        df = pd.DataFrame(daily_data)
        if not df.empty:
            df['date'] = pd.to_datetime(df['date'])
            df = df.sort_values('date').tail(days)
        
        return df
    
    def get_model_breakdown(self) -> Dict:
        """Model bazƒ±nda kullanƒ±m daƒüƒ±lƒ±mƒ±"""
        return self.stats.get('model_usage', {})
    
    def get_summary(self) -> Dict:
        """√ñzet istatistikler"""
        return {
            'total_messages': self.stats['total_messages'],
            'total_tokens': self.stats['total_tokens'],
            'total_cost': round(self.stats['total_cost'], 2),
            'sessions': self.stats['sessions_created'],
            'documents': self.stats['documents_added'],
            'voice_queries': self.stats['voice_queries'],
            'image_queries': self.stats['image_queries'],
            'avg_tokens_per_message': round(
                self.stats['total_tokens'] / max(self.stats['total_messages'], 1)
            ),
            'days_active': (
                datetime.now() - datetime.fromisoformat(self.stats['first_use'])
            ).days + 1
        }
```

### 5Ô∏è‚É£ `plugins/base_plugin.py` - Plugin Sistemi

```python name=plugins/base_plugin.py
from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
from typing import Dict, Any, List
from PyQt6.QtCore import QObject, pyqtSignal

class BasePlugin(QObject, ABC):
    """Temel plugin sƒ±nƒ±fƒ±"""
    
    # Sinyaller
    execution_started = pyqtSignal()
    execution_finished = pyqtSignal(dict)
    execution_error = pyqtSignal(str)
    progress_updated = pyqtSignal(int, str)
    
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self._enabled = True
    
    @property
    @abstractmethod
    def name(self) -> str:
        """Plugin adƒ±"""
        pass
    
    @property
    @abstractmethod
    def description(self) -> str:
        """Plugin a√ßƒ±klamasƒ±"""
        pass
    
    @property
    @abstractmethod
    def version(self) -> str:
        """Plugin versiyonu"""
        pass
    
    @property
    @abstractmethod
    def author(self) -> str:
        """Plugin geli≈ütiricisi"""
        pass
    
    @property
    def enabled(self) -> bool:
        """Plugin aktif mi?"""
        return self._enabled
    
    @enabled.setter
    def enabled(self, value: bool):
        """Plugin durumunu deƒüi≈ütir"""
        self._enabled = value
    
    @abstractmethod
    def get_config_schema(self) -> Dict:
        """
        Plugin konfig√ºrasyon ≈üemasƒ±
        
        Returns:
            {
                'api_key': {'type': 'string', 'required': True, 'label': 'API Key'},
                'max_results': {'type': 'int', 'default': 5, 'label': 'Max Results'}
            }
        """
        pass
    
    @abstractmethod
    def execute(self, **kwargs) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Plugin'i √ßalƒ±≈ütƒ±r
        
        Returns:
            {
                'success': True/False,
                'result': 'Sonu√ß verisi',
                'error': 'Hata mesajƒ± (varsa)'
            }
        """
        pass
    
    def validate_config(self, config: Dict) -> bool:
        """Konfig√ºrasyonu doƒürula"""
        schema = self.get_config_schema()
        
        for key, rules in schema.items():
            if rules.get('required', False) and key not in config:
                raise ValueError(f"Gerekli parametre eksik: {key}")
        
        return True
    
    def get_metadata(self) -> Dict:
        """Plugin metadata'sƒ±"""
        return {
            'name': self.name,
            'description': self.description,
            'version': self.version,
            'author': self.author,
            'enabled': self.enabled
        }
```

### 6Ô∏è‚É£ `plugins/web_search.py` - Web Arama Plugin'i

```python name=plugins/web_search.py
from plugins.base_plugin import BasePlugin
import requests
from typing import Dict, Any, List
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup

class WebSearchPlugin(BasePlugin):
    """Web arama plugin'i (Bing API veya scraping)"""
    
    @property
    def name(self) -> str:
        return "Web Arama"
    
    @property
    def description(self) -> str:
        return "ƒ∞nternet'te arama yaparak g√ºncel bilgilere eri≈üir"
    
    @property
    def version(self) -> str:
        return "1.0.0"
    
    @property
    def author(self) -> str:
        return "RAG Chatbot Team"
    
    def get_config_schema(self) -> Dict:
        return {
            'api_key': {
                'type': 'string',
                'required': False,
                'label': 'Bing Search API Key',
                'description': 'Bo≈ü bƒ±rakƒ±lƒ±rsa basit scraping kullanƒ±lƒ±r'
            },
            'max_results': {
                'type': 'int',
                'default': 5,
                'label': 'Maksimum Sonu√ß Sayƒ±sƒ±'
            },
            'search_engine': {
                'type': 'choice',
                'choices': ['bing', 'duckduckgo', 'google'],
                'default': 'duckduckgo',
                'label': 'Arama Motoru'
            }
        }
    
    def execute(self, query: str, config: Dict = None, **kwargs) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Web aramasƒ± yap"""
        self.execution_started.emit()
        
        if config is None:
            config = {'max_results': 5, 'search_engine': 'duckduckgo'}
        
        try:
            api_key = config.get('api_key')
            search_engine = config.get('search_engine', 'duckduckgo')
            max_results = config.get('max_results', 5)
            
            if api_key and search_engine == 'bing':
                results = self._search_bing_api(query, api_key, max_results)
            elif search_engine == 'duckduckgo':
                results = self._search_duckduckgo(query, max_results)
            else:
                results = self._search_simple(query, max_results)
            
            formatted_results = self._format_results(results)
            
            result = {
                'success': True,
                'result': formatted_results,
                'raw_results': results
            }
            
            self.execution_finished.emit(result)
            return result
        
        except Exception as e:
            error = f"Web arama hatasƒ±: {str(e)}"
            self.execution_error.emit(error)
            return {
                'success': False,
                'error': error
            }
    
    def _search_bing_api(self, query: str, api_key: str, max_results: int) -> List[Dict]:
        """Bing Search API kullanarak ara"""
        endpoint = "https://api.bing.microsoft.com/v7.0/search"
        
        headers = {"Ocp-Apim-Subscription-Key": api_key}
        params = {
            "q": query,
            "count": max_results,
            "mkt": "tr-TR"
        }
        
        response = requests.get(endpoint, headers=headers, params=params)
        response.raise_for_status()
        
        data = response.json()
        results = []
        
        for item in data.get('webPages', {}).get('value', []):
            results.append({
                'title': item.get('name'),
                'url': item.get('url'),
                'snippet': item.get('snippet')
            })
        
        return results
    
    def _search_duckduckgo(self, query: str, max_results: int) -> List[Dict]:
        """DuckDuckGo instant answers API"""
        try:
            from duckduckgo_search import DDGS
            
            results = []
            with DDGS() as ddgs:
                for r in ddgs.text(query, max_results=max_results):
                    results.append({
                        'title': r.get('title'),
                        'url': r.get('href'),
                        'snippet': r.get('body')
                    })
            
            return results
        
        except ImportError:
            # Fallback: basit scraping
            return self._search_simple(query, max_results)
    
    def _search_simple(self, query: str, max_results: int) -> List[Dict]:
        """Basit HTML scraping (fallback)"""
        # DuckDuckGo HTML scraping (API gerektirmez)
        url = f"https://html.duckduckgo.com/html/"
        data = {"q": query}
        
        headers = {
            'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36'
        }
        
        response = requests.post(url, data=data, headers=headers, timeout=10)
        soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser')
        
        results = []
        for result in soup.find_all('div', class_='result')[:max_results]:
            title_elem = result.find('a', class_='result__a')
            snippet_elem = result.find('a', class_='result__snippet')
            
            if title_elem:
                results.append({
                    'title': title_elem.get_text(strip=True),
                    'url': title_elem.get('href', ''),
                    'snippet': snippet_elem.get_text(strip=True) if snippet_elem else ''
                })
        
        return results
    
    def _format_results(self, results: List[Dict]) -> str:
        """Sonu√ßlarƒ± formatla"""
        if not results:
            return "Sonu√ß bulunamadƒ±."
        
        formatted = "üåê Web Arama Sonu√ßlarƒ±:\n\n"
        
        for i, result in enumerate(results, 1):
            formatted += f"{i}. **{result['title']}**\n"
            formatted += f"   {result['snippet']}\n"
            formatted += f"   üîó {result['url']}\n\n"
        
        return formatted
```


## üíé Level 2 Kod ƒ∞mplementasyonu (Devam)

### 7Ô∏è‚É£ `plugins/code_executor.py` - Kod √áalƒ±≈ütƒ±rma Plugin'i

```python name=plugins/code_executor.py
from plugins.base_plugin import BasePlugin
import subprocess
import tempfile
import os
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict, Any
import sys
import io
import contextlib

class CodeExecutorPlugin(BasePlugin):
    """G√ºvenli kod √ßalƒ±≈ütƒ±rma plugin'i"""
    
    # Desteklenen diller
    SUPPORTED_LANGUAGES = {
        'python': {
            'extension': '.py',
            'command': [sys.executable],
            'timeout': 30
        },
        'javascript': {
            'extension': '.js',
            'command': ['node'],
            'timeout': 30
        },
        'bash': {
            'extension': '.sh',
            'command': ['bash'],
            'timeout': 30
        }
    }
    
    @property
    def name(self) -> str:
        return "Kod √áalƒ±≈ütƒ±rƒ±cƒ±"
    
    @property
    def description(self) -> str:
        return "Python, JavaScript ve Bash kodlarƒ±nƒ± g√ºvenli ortamda √ßalƒ±≈ütƒ±rƒ±r"
    
    @property
    def version(self) -> str:
        return "1.0.0"
    
    @property
    def author(self) -> str:
        return "RAG Chatbot Team"
    
    def get_config_schema(self) -> Dict:
        return {
            'timeout': {
                'type': 'int',
                'default': 30,
                'label': 'Timeout (saniye)',
                'description': 'Kod √ßalƒ±≈ütƒ±rma i√ßin maksimum s√ºre'
            },
            'max_output_length': {
                'type': 'int',
                'default': 10000,
                'label': 'Maksimum √áƒ±ktƒ± Uzunluƒüu'
            },
            'allowed_languages': {
                'type': 'multiselect',
                'choices': ['python', 'javascript', 'bash'],
                'default': ['python'],
                'label': 'ƒ∞zin Verilen Diller'
            }
        }
    
    def execute(self, code: str, language: str = 'python', 
                config: Dict = None, **kwargs) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Kod √ßalƒ±≈ütƒ±r"""
        self.execution_started.emit()
        
        if config is None:
            config = {
                'timeout': 30,
                'max_output_length': 10000,
                'allowed_languages': ['python']
            }
        
        try:
            # Dil kontrol√º
            if language not in config.get('allowed_languages', ['python']):
                raise ValueError(f"Bu dil izin verilmiyor: {language}")
            
            if language not in self.SUPPORTED_LANGUAGES:
                raise ValueError(f"Desteklenmeyen dil: {language}")
            
            # Python i√ßin √∂zel inline execution
            if language == 'python':
                result = self._execute_python_inline(code, config)
            else:
                result = self._execute_in_subprocess(code, language, config)
            
            response = {
                'success': True,
                'result': result,
                'language': language
            }
            
            self.execution_finished.emit(response)
            return response
        
        except Exception as e:
            error = f"Kod √ßalƒ±≈ütƒ±rma hatasƒ±: {str(e)}"
            self.execution_error.emit(error)
            return {
                'success': False,
                'error': error
            }
    
    def _execute_python_inline(self, code: str, config: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Python kodunu inline √ßalƒ±≈ütƒ±r (daha g√ºvenli)"""
        # Stdout ve stderr'i yakala
        stdout_capture = io.StringIO()
        stderr_capture = io.StringIO()
        
        try:
            # G√ºvenli globals/locals
            safe_globals = {
                '__builtins__': __builtins__,
                'print': print,
            }
            safe_locals = {}
            
            with contextlib.redirect_stdout(stdout_capture), \
                 contextlib.redirect_stderr(stderr_capture):
                
                exec(code, safe_globals, safe_locals)
            
            stdout = stdout_capture.getvalue()
            stderr = stderr_capture.getvalue()
            
            # √áƒ±ktƒ± uzunluƒüu kontrol√º
            max_length = config.get('max_output_length', 10000)
            if len(stdout) > max_length:
                stdout = stdout[:max_length] + "\n... (√ßƒ±ktƒ± kesildi)"
            
            return {
                'stdout': stdout,
                'stderr': stderr,
                'return_value': safe_locals.get('__return__', None),
                'variables': {k: str(v) for k, v in safe_locals.items() 
                            if not k.startswith('_')}
            }
        
        except Exception as e:
            return {
                'stdout': stdout_capture.getvalue(),
                'stderr': str(e),
                'error': True
            }
    
    def _execute_in_subprocess(self, code: str, language: str, 
                               config: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Kodu subprocess'te √ßalƒ±≈ütƒ±r"""
        lang_config = self.SUPPORTED_LANGUAGES[language]
        
        # Ge√ßici dosya olu≈ütur
        with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(
            mode='w',
            suffix=lang_config['extension'],
            delete=False,
            encoding='utf-8'
        ) as f:
            f.write(code)
            temp_file = f.name
        
        try:
            # Komutu √ßalƒ±≈ütƒ±r
            timeout = config.get('timeout', lang_config['timeout'])
            
            process = subprocess.run(
                lang_config['command'] + [temp_file],
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=timeout
            )
            
            # √áƒ±ktƒ± uzunluƒüu kontrol√º
            max_length = config.get('max_output_length', 10000)
            stdout = process.stdout
            stderr = process.stderr
            
            if len(stdout) > max_length:
                stdout = stdout[:max_length] + "\n... (√ßƒ±ktƒ± kesildi)"
            if len(stderr) > max_length:
                stderr = stderr[:max_length] + "\n... (√ßƒ±ktƒ± kesildi)"
            
            return {
                'stdout': stdout,
                'stderr': stderr,
                'return_code': process.returncode,
                'error': process.returncode != 0
            }
        
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            return {
                'stdout': '',
                'stderr': f'Timeout ({timeout}s a≈üƒ±ldƒ±)',
                'error': True
            }
        
        finally:
            # Ge√ßici dosyayƒ± sil
            try:
                os.unlink(temp_file)
            except:
                pass
```

### 8Ô∏è‚É£ `utils/token_counter.py` - Token & Maliyet Takibi

```python name=utils/token_counter.py
import tiktoken
from typing import Dict, List

class TokenCounter:
    """Token sayƒ±mƒ± ve maliyet hesaplama"""
    
    # Model encodingleri
    ENCODINGS = {
        'gpt-4': 'cl100k_base',
        'gpt-4-turbo-preview': 'cl100k_base',
        'gpt-3.5-turbo': 'cl100k_base',
        'gpt-3.5-turbo-16k': 'cl100k_base',
    }
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.encoders = {}
    
    def get_encoder(self, model: str):
        """Model i√ßin encoder al"""
        if model not in self.encoders:
            encoding_name = self.ENCODINGS.get(model, 'cl100k_base')
            self.encoders[model] = tiktoken.get_encoding(encoding_name)
        
        return self.encoders[model]
    
    def count_tokens(self, text: str, model: str = 'gpt-4-turbo-preview') -> int:
        """Metindeki token sayƒ±sƒ±nƒ± hesapla"""
        encoder = self.get_encoder(model)
        return len(encoder.encode(text))
    
    def count_message_tokens(self, messages: List[Dict], 
                            model: str = 'gpt-4-turbo-preview') -> int:
        """
        ChatGPT mesaj formatƒ±ndaki toplam token sayƒ±sƒ±
        
        Her mesaj ≈üu formatta: {'role': 'user', 'content': '...'}
        """
        encoder = self.get_encoder(model)
        
        # Model spesifik token overhead'leri
        tokens_per_message = 3  # Her mesaj i√ßin
        tokens_per_name = 1     # ƒ∞sim varsa
        
        num_tokens = 0
        for message in messages:
            num_tokens += tokens_per_message
            
            for key, value in message.items():
                num_tokens += len(encoder.encode(str(value)))
                
                if key == "name":
                    num_tokens += tokens_per_name
        
        num_tokens += 3  # Her reply i√ßin priming
        return num_tokens
    
    def estimate_cost(self, input_tokens: int, output_tokens: int, 
                     model: str = 'gpt-4-turbo-preview') -> float:
        """Maliyet tahmini (USD)"""
        from core.analytics import Analytics
        
        prices = Analytics.TOKEN_PRICES.get(model, {'input': 0, 'output': 0})
        
        input_cost = (input_tokens / 1000) * prices['input']
        output_cost = (output_tokens / 1000) * prices['output']
        
        return input_cost + output_cost
    
    def check_context_limit(self, messages: List[Dict], 
                           model: str = 'gpt-4-turbo-preview') -> Dict:
        """
        Context limit kontrol√º
        
        Returns:
            {
                'within_limit': bool,
                'current_tokens': int,
                'max_tokens': int,
                'remaining': int
            }
        """
        # Model limitleri
        limits = {
            'gpt-4-turbo-preview': 128000,
            'gpt-4': 8192,
            'gpt-3.5-turbo': 4096,
            'gpt-3.5-turbo-16k': 16384,
        }
        
        max_tokens = limits.get(model, 4096)
        current_tokens = self.count_message_tokens(messages, model)
        
        return {
            'within_limit': current_tokens < max_tokens,
            'current_tokens': current_tokens,
            'max_tokens': max_tokens,
            'remaining': max_tokens - current_tokens
        }
```

### 9Ô∏è‚É£ `utils/export_manager.py` - Export/Import Y√∂netimi

```python name=utils/export_manager.py
import json
import zipfile
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Dict, List
import shutil

class ExportManager:
    """Chat, ayarlar ve belgeleri dƒ±≈üa/i√ße aktarma"""
    
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.export_dir = Path.home() / ".rag_chatbot" / "exports"
        self.export_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    
    def export_full_backup(self, include_documents: bool = True,
                          include_chroma: bool = False) -> str:
        """
        Tam yedekleme (ZIP)
        
        ƒ∞√ßerik:
        - T√ºm chat sessions
        - Ayarlar
        - Belgeler (opsiyonel)
        - ChromaDB (opsiyonel)
        - Analytics
        """
        timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
        backup_name = f"rag_chatbot_backup_{timestamp}.zip"
        backup_path = self.export_dir / backup_name
        
        base_dir = Path.home() / ".rag_chatbot"
        
        with zipfile.ZipFile(backup_path, 'w', zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as zipf:
            # Config
            config_file = base_dir / "config.json"
            if config_file.exists():
                zipf.write(config_file, "config.json")
            
            # Sessions
            sessions_dir = base_dir / "sessions"
            if sessions_dir.exists():
                for file in sessions_dir.glob("*.json"):
                    zipf.write(file, f"sessions/{file.name}")
            
            # Analytics
            analytics_dir = base_dir / "analytics"
            if analytics_dir.exists():
                for file in analytics_dir.glob("*"):
                    if file.is_file():
                        zipf.write(file, f"analytics/{file.name}")
            
            # Documents
            if include_documents:
                docs_dir = base_dir / "documents"
                if docs_dir.exists():
                    for file in docs_dir.glob("*"):
                        if file.is_file():
                            zipf.write(file, f"documents/{file.name}")
            
            # ChromaDB
            if include_chroma:
                chroma_dir = base_dir / "chroma_db"
                if chroma_dir.exists():
                    for file in chroma_dir.rglob("*"):
                        if file.is_file():
                            rel_path = file.relative_to(chroma_dir)
                            zipf.write(file, f"chroma_db/{rel_path}")
            
            # Metadata
            metadata = {
                'export_date': datetime.now().isoformat(),
                'version': '2.0',
                'includes_documents': include_documents,
                'includes_chroma': include_chroma
            }
            zipf.writestr("metadata.json", json.dumps(metadata, indent=2))
        
        return str(backup_path)
    
    def import_full_backup(self, backup_path: str, 
                          merge: bool = False) -> Dict:
        """
        Tam yedeklemeyi i√ße aktar
        
        Args:
            backup_path: ZIP dosya yolu
            merge: True ise mevcut verilerle birle≈ütir, False ise √ºzerine yaz
        """
        base_dir = Path.home() / ".rag_chatbot"
        
        if not merge:
            # Onay gerekebilir - t√ºm veriler silinecek
            response = {
                'warning': 'Mevcut t√ºm veriler silinecek!',
                'requires_confirmation': True
            }
            return response
        
        imported = {
            'sessions': 0,
            'documents': 0,
            'config': False,
            'analytics': False
        }
        
        with zipfile.ZipFile(backup_path, 'r') as zipf:
            # Metadata kontrol
            try:
                metadata_content = zipf.read("metadata.json")
                metadata = json.loads(metadata_content)
            except:
                metadata = {}
            
            # Config
            try:
                zipf.extract("config.json", base_dir.parent)
                imported['config'] = True
            except:
                pass
            
            # Sessions
            for file in zipf.namelist():
                if file.startswith("sessions/"):
                    zipf.extract(file, base_dir.parent)
                    imported['sessions'] += 1
            
            # Documents
            for file in zipf.namelist():
                if file.startswith("documents/"):
                    zipf.extract(file, base_dir.parent)
                    imported['documents'] += 1
            
            # Analytics
            for file in zipf.namelist():
                if file.startswith("analytics/"):
                    zipf.extract(file, base_dir.parent)
                    imported['analytics'] = True
            
            # ChromaDB
            for file in zipf.namelist():
                if file.startswith("chroma_db/"):
                    zipf.extract(file, base_dir.parent)
        
        return {
            'success': True,
            'imported': imported,
            'metadata': metadata
        }
    
    def export_settings(self) -> str:
        """Sadece ayarlarƒ± dƒ±≈üa aktar (JSON)"""
        timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
        settings_file = self.export_dir / f"settings_{timestamp}.json"
        
        config_file = Path.home() / ".rag_chatbot" / "config.json"
        if config_file.exists():
            shutil.copy2(config_file, settings_file)
            return str(settings_file)
        
        return None
    
    def import_settings(self, settings_path: str):
        """Ayarlarƒ± i√ße aktar"""
        config_file = Path.home() / ".rag_chatbot" / "config.json"
        shutil.copy2(settings_path, config_file)
```

### üîü `ui/session_panel.py` - Session Y√∂netim Paneli

```python name=ui/session_panel.py
from PyQt6.QtWidgets import (QWidget, QVBoxLayout, QHBoxLayout, 
                             QListWidget, QListWidgetItem, QLineEdit,
                             QMenu, QInputDialog)
from PyQt6.QtCore import Qt, pyqtSignal
from PyQt6.QtGui import QIcon, QAction
from qfluentwidgets import (PushButton, LineEdit, FluentIcon, SearchLineEdit,
                           BodyLabel, StrongBodyLabel, MessageBox, 
                           RoundMenu, Action, MenuAnimationType)
from datetime import datetime

class SessionListItem(QWidget):
    """Session liste √∂ƒüesi"""
    
    clicked = pyqtSignal(str)  # session_id
    
    def __init__(self, session, parent=None):
        super().__init__(parent)
        self.session = session
        self.setup_ui()
    
    def setup_ui(self):
        layout = QVBoxLayout(self)
        layout.setContentsMargins(12, 8, 12, 8)
        
        # Ba≈ülƒ±k
        title = StrongBodyLabel(self.session.title)
        title.setStyleSheet("font-size: 13px;")
        
        # Zaman ve mesaj sayƒ±sƒ±
        time_str = self._format_time(self.session.updated_at)
        msg_count = len(self.session.messages)
        info = BodyLabel(f"{time_str} ‚Ä¢ {msg_count} mesaj")
        info.setStyleSheet("color: #888; font-size: 11px;")
        
        layout.addWidget(title)
        layout.addWidget(info)
        
        self.setStyleSheet("""
            SessionListItem {
                background-color: #2B2B2B;
                border-radius: 8px;
            }
            SessionListItem:hover {
                background-color: #353535;
            }
        """)
    
    def _format_time(self, iso_time: str) -> str:
        """Zamanƒ± kullanƒ±cƒ± dostu formata √ßevir"""
        try:
            dt = datetime.fromisoformat(iso_time)
            now = datetime.now()
            diff = now - dt
            
            if diff.days == 0:
                if diff.seconds < 3600:
                    minutes = diff.seconds // 60
                    return f"{minutes} dakika √∂nce"
                else:
                    hours = diff.seconds // 3600
                    return f"{hours} saat √∂nce"
            elif diff.days == 1:
                return "D√ºn"
            elif diff.days < 7:
                return f"{diff.days} g√ºn √∂nce"
            else:
                return dt.strftime("%d.%m.%Y")
        except:
            return ""
    
    def mousePressEvent(self, event):
        """Tƒ±klama eventi"""
        self.clicked.emit(self.session.id)
        super().mousePressEvent(event)

class SessionPanel(QWidget):
    """Session y√∂netim paneli"""
    
    session_selected = pyqtSignal(str)  # session_id
    session_deleted = pyqtSignal(str)
    session_renamed = pyqtSignal(str, str)  # id, new_title
    new_session_requested = pyqtSignal()
    
    def __init__(self, session_manager, parent=None):
        super().__init__(parent)
        self.session_manager = session_manager
        self.setup_ui()
        self.load_sessions()
    
    def setup_ui(self):
        layout = QVBoxLayout(self)
        layout.setContentsMargins(16, 16, 16, 16)
        layout.setSpacing(12)
        
        # Ba≈ülƒ±k ve yeni session butonu
        header = QHBoxLayout()
        
        title = StrongBodyLabel("Konu≈ümalar")
        title.setStyleSheet("font-size: 16px;")
        
        self.new_btn = PushButton(FluentIcon.ADD, "Yeni")
        self.new_btn.clicked.connect(self.new_session_requested.emit)
        
        header.addWidget(title)
        header.addStretch()
        header.addWidget(self.new_btn)
        
        layout.addLayout(header)
        
        # Arama
        self.search_box = SearchLineEdit()
        self.search_box.setPlaceholderText("Konu≈ümalarda ara...")
        self.search_box.textChanged.connect(self.filter_sessions)
        layout.addWidget(self.search_box)
        
        # Session listesi
        self.session_list = QListWidget()
        self.session_list.setSpacing(8)
        self.session_list.setStyleSheet("""
            QListWidget {
                background-color: #1E1E1E;
                border: 1px solid #3D3D3D;
                border-radius: 8px;
                padding: 8px;
            }
            QListWidget::item {
                background-color: transparent;
                border: none;
                padding: 0;
                margin: 0;
            }
            QListWidget::item:selected {
                background-color: transparent;
            }
        """)
        
        self.session_list.setContextMenuPolicy(Qt.ContextMenuPolicy.CustomContextMenu)
        self.session_list.customContextMenuRequested.connect(self.show_context_menu)
        
        layout.addWidget(self.session_list, 1)
    
    def load_sessions(self):
        """Session'larƒ± y√ºkle"""
        self.session_list.clear()
        
        sessions = self.session_manager.get_all_sessions()
        
        for session in sessions:
            item = QListWidgetItem(self.session_list)
            widget = SessionListItem(session)
            widget.clicked.connect(self.on_session_clicked)
            
            item.setSizeHint(widget.sizeHint())
            self.session_list.addItem(item)
            self.session_list.setItemWidget(item, widget)
    
    def filter_sessions(self, query: str):
        """Session'larƒ± filtrele"""
        if not query:
            self.load_sessions()
            return
        
        self.session_list.clear()
        
        sessions = self.session_manager.search_sessions(query)
        
        for session in sessions:
            item = QListWidgetItem(self.session_list)
            widget = SessionListItem(session)
            widget.clicked.connect(self.on_session_clicked)
            
            item.setSizeHint(widget.sizeHint())
            self.session_list.addItem(item)
            self.session_list.setItemWidget(item, widget)
    
    def on_session_clicked(self, session_id: str):
        """Session tƒ±klandƒ±"""
        self.session_selected.emit(session_id)
    
    def show_context_menu(self, position):
        """Saƒü tƒ±k men√ºs√º"""
        item = self.session_list.itemAt(position)
        if not item:
            return
        
        widget = self.session_list.itemWidget(item)
        if not widget:
            return
        
        session_id = widget.session.id
        
        menu = RoundMenu(parent=self)
        
        rename_action = Action(FluentIcon.EDIT, "Yeniden Adlandƒ±r")
        rename_action.triggered.connect(lambda: self.rename_session(session_id))
        
        delete_action = Action(FluentIcon.DELETE, "Sil")
        delete_action.triggered.connect(lambda: self.delete_session(session_id))
        
        export_action = Action(FluentIcon.DOWNLOAD, "Dƒ±≈üa Aktar")
        export_action.triggered.connect(lambda: self.export_session(session_id))
        
        menu.addAction(rename_action)
        menu.addAction(export_action)
        menu.addSeparator()
        menu.addAction(delete_action)
        
        menu.exec(self.session_list.mapToGlobal(position))
    
    def rename_session(self, session_id: str):
        """Session'ƒ± yeniden adlandƒ±r"""
        session = self.session_manager.get_session(session_id)
        if not session:
            return
        
        new_title, ok = QInputDialog.getText(
            self,
            "Yeniden Adlandƒ±r",
            "Yeni ba≈ülƒ±k:",
            text=session.title
        )
        
        if ok and new_title:
            self.session_manager.rename_session(session_id, new_title)
            self.session_renamed.emit(session_id, new_title)
            self.load_sessions()
    
    def delete_session(self, session_id: str):
        """Session'ƒ± sil"""
        result = MessageBox(
            "Onayla",
            "Bu konu≈ümayƒ± silmek istediƒüinize emin misiniz?",
            self
        ).exec()
        
        if result:
            self.session_manager.delete_session(session_id)
            self.session_deleted.emit(session_id)
            self.load_sessions()
    
    def export_session(self, session_id: str):
        """Session'ƒ± dƒ±≈üa aktar"""
        from qfluentwidgets import InfoBar, InfoBarPosition
        
        try:
            export_path = self.session_manager.export_session(session_id, format='markdown')
            
            InfoBar.success(
                title="Ba≈üarƒ±lƒ±",
                content=f"Konu≈üma dƒ±≈üa aktarƒ±ldƒ±: {export_path}",
                parent=self,
                position=InfoBarPosition.TOP,
                duration=3000
            )
        except Exception as e:
            MessageBox("Hata", f"Dƒ±≈üa aktarma hatasƒ±: {str(e)}", self).exec()
```

### 1Ô∏è‚É£1Ô∏è‚É£ `ui/prompt_library.py` - Hazƒ±r Prompt K√ºt√ºphanesi

```python name=ui/prompt_library.py
from PyQt6.QtWidgets import (QWidget, QVBoxLayout, QHBoxLayout, 
                             QListWidget, QListWidgetItem, QTextEdit)
from PyQt6.QtCore import Qt, pyqtSignal
from qfluentwidgets import (PushButton, FluentIcon, BodyLabel, 
                           StrongBodyLabel, SearchLineEdit, ScrollArea,
                           CardWidget, IconWidget)
import json
from pathlib import Path

class PromptCard(CardWidget):
    """Prompt kartƒ±"""
    
    use_clicked = pyqtSignal(str)  # prompt text
    
    def __init__(self, prompt_data: dict, parent=None):
        super().__init__(parent)
        self.prompt_data = prompt_data
        self.setup_ui()
    
    def setup_ui(self):
        layout = QVBoxLayout(self)
        layout.setContentsMargins(16, 16, 16, 16)
        layout.setSpacing(8)
        
        # Ba≈ülƒ±k ve kategori
        header = QHBoxLayout()
        
        # ƒ∞kon (kategori bazlƒ±)
        icon_map = {
            'Yazma': FluentIcon.EDIT,
            'Analiz': FluentIcon.SEARCH,
            'Kod': FluentIcon.CODE,
            'Eƒüitim': FluentIcon.EDUCATION,
            'ƒ∞≈ü': FluentIcon.BUSINESS,
            'Yaratƒ±cƒ±': FluentIcon.PALETTE
        }
        
        icon = IconWidget(icon_map.get(self.prompt_data.get('category'), FluentIcon.CHAT))
        icon.setFixedSize(24, 24)
        
        title = StrongBodyLabel(self.prompt_data['title'])
        title.setStyleSheet("font-size: 14px;")
        
        header.addWidget(icon)
        header.addWidget(title, 1)
        
        layout.addLayout(header)
        
        # A√ßƒ±klama
        description = BodyLabel(self.prompt_data.get('description', ''))
        description.setWordWrap(True)
        description.setStyleSheet("color: #888; font-size: 12px;")
        layout.addWidget(description)
        
        # Kullan butonu
        use_btn = PushButton(FluentIcon.SEND, "Kullan")
        use_btn.clicked.connect(lambda: self.use_clicked.emit(self.prompt_data['prompt']))
        layout.addWidget(use_btn, alignment=Qt.AlignmentFlag.AlignRight)
        
        self.setFixedHeight(150)

class PromptLibrary(QWidget):
    """Hazƒ±r prompt k√ºt√ºphanesi"""
    
    prompt_selected = pyqtSignal(str)
    
    # Hazƒ±r promptlar
    DEFAULT_PROMPTS = [

        },
        {
            'title': 'Problem √á√∂zme',
            'category': 'Analiz',
            'description': 'Probleme adƒ±m adƒ±m √ß√∂z√ºm bulur',
            'prompt': '≈ûu problemi adƒ±m adƒ±m √ß√∂z:\n\nProblem: [PROBLEM]\n\n1. Problemi analiz et\n2. √á√∂z√ºm alternatifleri sun\n3. En iyi √ß√∂z√ºm√º detaylandƒ±r\n4. Olasƒ± riskleri belirt'
        }

    def __init__(self, parent=None):
        super().__init__(parent)
        self.prompts = self.load_prompts()
        self.setup_ui()
    
    def load_prompts(self):
        """Promptlarƒ± y√ºkle"""
        prompts_file = Path.home() / ".rag_chatbot" / "prompts.json"
        
        if prompts_file.exists():
            with open(prompts_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                return json.load(f)
        
        # Default promptlarƒ± kaydet
        self.save_prompts(self.DEFAULT_PROMPTS)
        return self.DEFAULT_PROMPTS
    
    def save_prompts(self, prompts):
        """Promptlarƒ± kaydet"""
        prompts_file = Path.home() / ".rag_chatbot" / "prompts.json"
        with open(prompts_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(prompts, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
    
    def setup_ui(self):
        layout = QVBoxLayout(self)
        layout.setContentsMargins(20, 20, 20, 20)
        layout.setSpacing(16)
        
        # Ba≈ülƒ±k
        header = QHBoxLayout()
        title = StrongBodyLabel("üìù Prompt K√ºt√ºphanesi")
        title.setStyleSheet("font-size: 16px;")
        header.addWidget(title)
        header.addStretch()
        layout.addLayout(header)
        
        # Arama
        self.search_box = SearchLineEdit()
        self.search_box.setPlaceholderText("Promptlarda ara...")
        self.search_box.textChanged.connect(self.filter_prompts)
        layout.addWidget(self.search_box)
        
        # Kategori filtreleme
        category_layout = QHBoxLayout()
        category_label = BodyLabel("Kategori:")
        self.category_buttons = {}
        
        categories = ['T√ºm√º', 'Yazma', 'Analiz', 'Kod', 'Eƒüitim', 'ƒ∞≈ü', 'Yaratƒ±cƒ±']
        for cat in categories:
            btn = PushButton(cat)
            btn.clicked.connect(lambda checked, c=cat: self.filter_by_category(c))
            category_layout.addWidget(btn)
            self.category_buttons[cat] = btn
        
        category_layout.addStretch()
        layout.addLayout(category_layout)
        
        # Prompt kartlarƒ±
        scroll = ScrollArea()
        scroll.setWidgetResizable(True)
        
        scroll_widget = QWidget()
        self.prompts_layout = QVBoxLayout(scroll_widget)
        self.prompts_layout.setSpacing(12)
        
        self.display_prompts(self.prompts)
        
        self.prompts_layout.addStretch()
        scroll.setWidget(scroll_widget)
        layout.addWidget(scroll, 1)
    
    def display_prompts(self, prompts):
        """Promptlarƒ± g√∂ster"""
        # Mevcut kartlarƒ± temizle
        while self.prompts_layout.count() > 1:
            item = self.prompts_layout.takeAt(0)
            if item.widget():
                item.widget().deleteLater()
        
        # Yeni kartlar ekle
        for prompt in prompts:
            card = PromptCard(prompt)
            card.use_clicked.connect(self.prompt_selected.emit)
            self.prompts_layout.insertWidget(self.prompts_layout.count() - 1, card)
    
    def filter_prompts(self, query: str):
        """Promptlarƒ± filtrele"""
        if not query:
            self.display_prompts(self.prompts)
            return
        
        query_lower = query.lower()
        filtered = [
            p for p in self.prompts
            if query_lower in p['title'].lower() or 
               query_lower in p.get('description', '').lower() or
               query_lower in p.get('category', '').lower()
        ]
        
        self.display_prompts(filtered)
    
    def filter_by_category(self, category: str):
        """Kategoriye g√∂re filtrele"""
        if category == 'T√ºm√º':
            self.display_prompts(self.prompts)
        else:
            filtered = [p for p in self.prompts if p.get('category') == category]
            self.display_prompts(filtered)
```

### 1Ô∏è‚É£2Ô∏è‚É£ `ui/markdown_renderer.py` - Markdown Rendering

```python name=ui/markdown_renderer.py
from PyQt6.QtWidgets import QTextBrowser
from PyQt6.QtCore import Qt
from PyQt6.QtGui import QFont, QTextDocument, QSyntaxHighlighter, QTextCharFormat, QColor
import markdown2
import re
from pygments import highlight
from pygments.lexers import get_lexer_by_name, guess_lexer
from pygments.formatters import HtmlFormatter

class MarkdownRenderer(QTextBrowser):
    """Markdown i√ßerik renderer'ƒ±"""
    
    def __init__(self, parent=None):
        super().__init__(parent)
        self.setOpenExternalLinks(True)
        self.setReadOnly(True)
        
        # CSS stil
        self.setStyleSheet("""
            QTextBrowser {
                background-color: #2B2B2B;
                color: #E1E1E1;
                border: none;
                padding: 16px;
                font-family: 'Segoe UI', Arial, sans-serif;
                font-size: 13px;
                line-height: 1.6;
            }
        """)
    
    def set_markdown(self, markdown_text: str):
        """Markdown metnini render et"""
        # Markdown'ƒ± HTML'e √ßevir
        html = self._convert_markdown_to_html(markdown_text)
        
        # HTML'i g√∂ster
        self.setHtml(html)
    
    def _convert_markdown_to_html(self, markdown_text: str) -> str:
        """Markdown'ƒ± HTML'e √ßevir"""
        # Markdown2 ile √ßevir
        extras = [
            'fenced-code-blocks',
            'tables',
            'break-on-newline',
            'code-friendly',
            'cuddled-lists',
            'header-ids'
        ]
        
        html_content = markdown2.markdown(markdown_text, extras=extras)
        
        # Syntax highlighting ekle
        html_content = self._add_syntax_highlighting(html_content)
        
        # Tam HTML sayfasƒ± olu≈ütur
        full_html = f"""
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
        <head>
            <meta charset="UTF-8">
            <style>
                {self._get_css_styles()}
            </style>
        </head>
        <body>
            {html_content}
        </body>
        </html>
        """
        
        return full_html
    
    def _add_syntax_highlighting(self, html: str) -> str:
        """Kod bloklarƒ±na syntax highlighting ekle"""
        # <code class="language-xxx"> pattern'ini bul
        pattern = r'<code class="([^"]+)">(.*?)</code>'
        
        def replace_code(match):
            language = match.group(1).replace('language-', '')
            code = match.group(2)
            
            # HTML entity'leri √ß√∂z
            import html as html_module
            code = html_module.unescape(code)
            
            try:
                lexer = get_lexer_by_name(language, stripall=True)
            except:
                try:
                    lexer = guess_lexer(code)
                except:
                    return match.group(0)  # Highlighting yapƒ±lamadƒ±
            
            formatter = HtmlFormatter(
                style='monokai',
                noclasses=True,
                cssclass='highlight'
            )
            
            highlighted = highlight(code, lexer, formatter)
            return highlighted
        
        return re.sub(pattern, replace_code, html, flags=re.DOTALL)
    
    def _get_css_styles(self) -> str:
        """CSS stilleri"""
        return """
            body {
                background-color: #2B2B2B;
                color: #E1E1E1;
                font-family: 'Segoe UI', Arial, sans-serif;
                font-size: 13px;
                line-height: 1.6;
                padding: 0;
                margin: 0;
            }
            
            h1, h2, h3, h4, h5, h6 {
                color: #FFFFFF;
                margin-top: 24px;
                margin-bottom: 12px;
                font-weight: 600;
            }
            
            h1 { font-size: 24px; border-bottom: 2px solid #005A9E; padding-bottom: 8px; }
            h2 { font-size: 20px; }
            h3 { font-size: 18px; }
            
            p {
                margin: 12px 0;
            }
            
            code {
                background-color: #1E1E1E;
                color: #CE9178;
                padding: 2px 6px;
                border-radius: 4px;
                font-family: 'Consolas', 'Monaco', monospace;
                font-size: 12px;
            }
            
            pre {
                background-color: #1E1E1E;
                padding: 16px;
                border-radius: 8px;
                overflow-x: auto;
                border-left: 3px solid #005A9E;
            }
            
            pre code {
                background-color: transparent;
                padding: 0;
            }
            
            blockquote {
                border-left: 4px solid #005A9E;
                padding-left: 16px;
                margin-left: 0;
                color: #AAA;
                font-style: italic;
            }
            
            a {
                color: #4A9EFF;
                text-decoration: none;
            }
            
            a:hover {
                text-decoration: underline;
            }
            
            table {
                border-collapse: collapse;
                width: 100%;
                margin: 16px 0;
            }
            
            th, td {
                border: 1px solid #3D3D3D;
                padding: 8px 12px;
                text-align: left;
            }
            
            th {
                background-color: #1E1E1E;
                font-weight: 600;
            }
            
            tr:nth-child(even) {
                background-color: #252525;
            }
            
            ul, ol {
                padding-left: 24px;
                margin: 12px 0;
            }
            
            li {
                margin: 6px 0;
            }
            
            hr {
                border: none;
                border-top: 1px solid #3D3D3D;
                margin: 24px 0;
            }
            
            .highlight {
                margin: 0;
            }
        """
```
