### 1Ô∏è‚É£3Ô∏è‚É£ `ui/analytics_dashboard.py` - Analitik Dashboard

```python name=ui/analytics_dashboard.py
from PyQt6.QtWidgets import (QWidget, QVBoxLayout, QHBoxLayout, QGridLayout,
                             QLabel, QFrame)
from PyQt6.QtCore import Qt
from qfluentwidgets import (CardWidget, BodyLabel, StrongBodyLabel, 
                           IconWidget, FluentIcon, ProgressBar)
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
from matplotlib.backends.backend_qt5agg import FigureCanvasQTAgg as FigureCanvas
from matplotlib.figure import Figure
import pandas as pd

class StatCard(CardWidget):
    """ƒ∞statistik kartƒ±"""
    
    def __init__(self, title: str, value: str, icon: FluentIcon, 
                 color: str = "#005A9E", parent=None):
        super().__init__(parent)
        self.setup_ui(title, value, icon, color)
    
    def setup_ui(self, title, value, icon, color):
        layout = QVBoxLayout(self)
        layout.setContentsMargins(20, 16, 20, 16)
        layout.setSpacing(8)
        
        # √úst kƒ±sƒ±m: ƒ∞kon ve ba≈ülƒ±k
        header = QHBoxLayout()
        
        icon_widget = IconWidget(icon)
        icon_widget.setFixedSize(32, 32)
        
        title_label = BodyLabel(title)
        title_label.setStyleSheet("color: #888; font-size: 12px;")
        
        header.addWidget(icon_widget)
        header.addWidget(title_label, 1)
        
        layout.addLayout(header)
        
        # Deƒüer
        value_label = StrongBodyLabel(value)
        value_label.setStyleSheet(f"color: {color}; font-size: 28px; font-weight: bold;")
        layout.addWidget(value_label)
        
        self.setFixedHeight(120)

class ChartWidget(QWidget):
    """Grafik widget'ƒ±"""
    
    def __init__(self, parent=None):
        super().__init__(parent)
        self.figure = Figure(figsize=(8, 4), facecolor='#2B2B2B')
        self.canvas = FigureCanvas(self.figure)
        
        layout = QVBoxLayout(self)
        layout.setContentsMargins(0, 0, 0, 0)
        layout.addWidget(self.canvas)
        
        # Matplotlib dark theme
        plt.style.use('dark_background')
    
    def plot_daily_usage(self, df: pd.DataFrame):
        """G√ºnl√ºk kullanƒ±m grafiƒüi"""
        self.figure.clear()
        ax = self.figure.add_subplot(111)
        
        if df.empty:
            ax.text(0.5, 0.5, 'Hen√ºz veri yok', 
                   ha='center', va='center', fontsize=14, color='#888')
            self.canvas.draw()
            return
        
        # Grafik √ßiz
        ax.plot(df['date'], df['messages'], 
               marker='o', linewidth=2, markersize=6,
               color='#4A9EFF', label='Mesajlar')
        
        ax.fill_between(df['date'], df['messages'], alpha=0.3, color='#4A9EFF')
        
        ax.set_xlabel('Tarih', fontsize=10, color='#E1E1E1')
        ax.set_ylabel('Mesaj Sayƒ±sƒ±', fontsize=10, color='#E1E1E1')
        ax.set_title('Son 30 G√ºnl√ºk Kullanƒ±m', fontsize=12, 
                    color='#FFFFFF', pad=20)
        
        ax.grid(True, alpha=0.2, linestyle='--')
        ax.legend(loc='upper left', frameon=False)
        
        # X ekseni etiketlerini d√∂nd√ºr
        plt.setp(ax.xaxis.get_majorticklabels(), rotation=45, ha='right')
        
        # Kenarlƒ±klarƒ± ayarla
        ax.spines['top'].set_visible(False)
        ax.spines['right'].set_visible(False)
        ax.spines['left'].set_color('#3D3D3D')
        ax.spines['bottom'].set_color('#3D3D3D')
        
        self.figure.tight_layout()
        self.canvas.draw()
    
    def plot_model_usage(self, model_data: dict):
        """Model kullanƒ±m daƒüƒ±lƒ±mƒ± (pasta grafiƒüi)"""
        self.figure.clear()
        ax = self.figure.add_subplot(111)
        
        if not model_data:
            ax.text(0.5, 0.5, 'Hen√ºz veri yok', 
                   ha='center', va='center', fontsize=14, color='#888')
            self.canvas.draw()
            return
        
        # Veriyi hazƒ±rla
        labels = []
        sizes = []
        colors = ['#4A9EFF', '#FF6B6B', '#4ECDC4', '#FFD93D', '#A8E6CF']
        
        for i, (model, data) in enumerate(model_data.items()):
            labels.append(model)
            sizes.append(data['count'])
        
        # Pasta grafiƒüi
        wedges, texts, autotexts = ax.pie(
            sizes, 
            labels=labels,
            colors=colors[:len(labels)],
            autopct='%1.1f%%',
            startangle=90,
            textprops={'color': '#E1E1E1', 'fontsize': 10}
        )
        
        # Y√ºzde metinlerini beyaz yap
        for autotext in autotexts:
            autotext.set_color('white')
            autotext.set_fontweight('bold')
        
        ax.set_title('Model Kullanƒ±m Daƒüƒ±lƒ±mƒ±', fontsize=12, 
                    color='#FFFFFF', pad=20)
        
        self.figure.tight_layout()
        self.canvas.draw()
    
    def plot_token_cost(self, df: pd.DataFrame):
        """Token ve maliyet grafiƒüi (√ßift eksen)"""
        self.figure.clear()
        ax1 = self.figure.add_subplot(111)
        
        if df.empty:
            ax1.text(0.5, 0.5, 'Hen√ºz veri yok', 
                    ha='center', va='center', fontsize=14, color='#888')
            self.canvas.draw()
            return
        
        # ƒ∞lk eksen: Token
        color1 = '#4A9EFF'
        ax1.set_xlabel('Tarih', fontsize=10, color='#E1E1E1')
        ax1.set_ylabel('Token Sayƒ±sƒ±', fontsize=10, color=color1)
        line1 = ax1.plot(df['date'], df['tokens'], 
                        color=color1, marker='o', label='Token')
        ax1.tick_params(axis='y', labelcolor=color1)
        ax1.fill_between(df['date'], df['tokens'], alpha=0.2, color=color1)
        
        # ƒ∞kinci eksen: Maliyet
        ax2 = ax1.twinx()
        color2 = '#FF6B6B'
        ax2.set_ylabel('Maliyet ($)', fontsize=10, color=color2)
        line2 = ax2.plot(df['date'], df['cost'], 
                        color=color2, marker='s', label='Maliyet')
        ax2.tick_params(axis='y', labelcolor=color2)
        
        # Ba≈ülƒ±k
        ax1.set_title('Token ve Maliyet Analizi', fontsize=12, 
                     color='#FFFFFF', pad=20)
        
        # Grid
        ax1.grid(True, alpha=0.2, linestyle='--')
        
        # Legend
        lines = line1 + line2
        labels = [l.get_label() for l in lines]
        ax1.legend(lines, labels, loc='upper left', frameon=False)
        
        # X ekseni etiketleri
        plt.setp(ax1.xaxis.get_majorticklabels(), rotation=45, ha='right')
        
        # Kenarlƒ±klar
        ax1.spines['top'].set_visible(False)
        ax1.spines['left'].set_color(color1)
        ax1.spines['bottom'].set_color('#3D3D3D')
        ax2.spines['top'].set_visible(False)
        ax2.spines['right'].set_color(color2)
        
        self.figure.tight_layout()
        self.canvas.draw()

class AnalyticsDashboard(QWidget):
    """Analitik dashboard"""
    
    def __init__(self, analytics, parent=None):
        super().__init__(parent)
        self.analytics = analytics
        self.setup_ui()
        self.refresh_data()
    
    def setup_ui(self):
        layout = QVBoxLayout(self)
        layout.setContentsMargins(20, 20, 20, 20)
        layout.setSpacing(20)
        
        # Ba≈ülƒ±k
        title = StrongBodyLabel("üìä Analitik Dashboard")
        title.setStyleSheet("font-size: 18px;")
        layout.addWidget(title)
        
        # √ñzet kartlarƒ±
        cards_layout = QGridLayout()
        cards_layout.setSpacing(16)
        
        self.message_card = StatCard(
            "Toplam Mesaj", "0", 
            FluentIcon.CHAT, "#4A9EFF"
        )
        
        self.token_card = StatCard(
            "Toplam Token", "0", 
            FluentIcon.CERTIFICATE, "#4ECDC4"
        )
        
        self.cost_card = StatCard(
            "Toplam Maliyet", "$0.00", 
            FluentIcon.MONEY, "#FFD93D"
        )
        
        self.session_card = StatCard(
            "Konu≈ümalar", "0", 
            FluentIcon.HISTORY, "#FF6B6B"
        )
        
        cards_layout.addWidget(self.message_card, 0, 0)
        cards_layout.addWidget(self.token_card, 0, 1)
        cards_layout.addWidget(self.cost_card, 0, 2)
        cards_layout.addWidget(self.session_card, 0, 3)
        
        layout.addLayout(cards_layout)
        
        # Grafikler
        charts_layout = QGridLayout()
        charts_layout.setSpacing(16)
        
        # G√ºnl√ºk kullanƒ±m grafiƒüi
        daily_frame = self._create_chart_frame("G√ºnl√ºk Kullanƒ±m Trendi")
        self.daily_chart = ChartWidget()
        daily_frame.layout().addWidget(self.daily_chart)
        charts_layout.addWidget(daily_frame, 0, 0, 1, 2)
        
        # Model daƒüƒ±lƒ±mƒ±
        model_frame = self._create_chart_frame("Model Kullanƒ±m Daƒüƒ±lƒ±mƒ±")
        self.model_chart = ChartWidget()
        model_frame.layout().addWidget(self.model_chart)
        charts_layout.addWidget(model_frame, 1, 0)
        
        # Token & Maliyet
        token_frame = self._create_chart_frame("Token ve Maliyet Analizi")
        self.token_chart = ChartWidget()
        token_frame.layout().addWidget(self.token_chart)
        charts_layout.addWidget(token_frame, 1, 1)
        
        layout.addLayout(charts_layout, 1)
    
    def _create_chart_frame(self, title: str) -> QFrame:
        """Grafik frame'i olu≈ütur"""
        frame = QFrame()
        frame.setStyleSheet("""
            QFrame {
                background-color: #2B2B2B;
                border-radius: 12px;
                border: 1px solid #3D3D3D;
            }
        """)
        
        layout = QVBoxLayout(frame)
        layout.setContentsMargins(16, 16, 16, 16)
        layout.setSpacing(12)
        
        title_label = StrongBodyLabel(title)
        title_label.setStyleSheet("font-size: 14px;")
        layout.addWidget(title_label)
        
        return frame
    
    def refresh_data(self):
        """Verileri yenile"""
        # √ñzet istatistikleri al
        summary = self.analytics.get_summary()
        
        # Kartlarƒ± g√ºncelle
        self.message_card.findChild(StrongBodyLabel).setText(
            str(summary['total_messages'])
        )
        
        self.token_card.findChild(StrongBodyLabel).setText(
            f"{summary['total_tokens']:,}"
        )
        
        self.cost_card.findChild(StrongBodyLabel).setText(
            f"${summary['total_cost']:.2f}"
        )
        
        self.session_card.findChild(StrongBodyLabel).setText(
            str(summary['sessions'])
        )
        
        # Grafikleri g√ºncelle
        daily_df = self.analytics.get_daily_usage(30)
        self.daily_chart.plot_daily_usage(daily_df)
        
        model_data = self.analytics.get_model_breakdown()
        self.model_chart.plot_model_usage(model_data)
        
        if not daily_df.empty:
            self.token_chart.plot_token_cost(daily_df)

class ProgressCard(CardWidget):
    """ƒ∞lerleme g√∂sterge kartƒ±"""
    
    def __init__(self, title: str, current: int, target: int, parent=None):
        super().__init__(parent)
        self.setup_ui(title, current, target)
    
    def setup_ui(self, title, current, target):
        layout = QVBoxLayout(self)
        layout.setContentsMargins(20, 16, 20, 16)
        layout.setSpacing(8)
        
        # Ba≈ülƒ±k
        title_label = StrongBodyLabel(title)
        title_label.setStyleSheet("font-size: 13px;")
        layout.addWidget(title_label)
        
        # ƒ∞lerleme √ßubuƒüu
        progress = ProgressBar()
        progress.setRange(0, target)
        progress.setValue(current)
        layout.addWidget(progress)
        
        # Metin
        text = BodyLabel(f"{current} / {target} ({int(current/target*100)}%)")
        text.setStyleSheet("color: #888; font-size: 11px;")
        layout.addWidget(text)
```

### 1Ô∏è‚É£4Ô∏è‚É£ `ui/main_window.py` - G√ºncellenmi≈ü Ana Pencere (v2)

```python name=ui/main_window_v2.py
from PyQt6.QtWidgets import QWidget, QHBoxLayout, QVBoxLayout, QSplitter
from PyQt6.QtCore import Qt, QTimer
from qfluentwidgets import (FluentWindow, NavigationItemPosition, FluentIcon,
                           setTheme, Theme, setThemeColor, SplitFluentWindow,
                           MessageBox)
from ui.chat_widget import ChatWidget
from ui.settings_dialog import SettingsDialog
from ui.document_manager import DocumentManager
from ui.session_panel import SessionPanel
from ui.prompt_library import PromptLibrary
from ui.analytics_dashboard import AnalyticsDashboard
from ui.markdown_renderer import MarkdownRenderer

class MainWindowV2(SplitFluentWindow):
    """Level 2 - Geli≈ütirilmi≈ü ana pencere"""
    
    def __init__(self, config, chat_manager, rag_engine, 
                 session_manager, analytics, voice_manager, vision_manager):
        super().__init__()
        
        self.config = config
        self.chat_manager = chat_manager
        self.rag_engine = rag_engine
        self.session_manager = session_manager
        self.analytics = analytics
        self.voice_manager = voice_manager
        self.vision_manager = vision_manager
        
        self.setWindowTitle("RAG Chatbot v2.0 Pro")
        self.resize(1400, 900)
        
        # Tema
        setTheme(Theme.DARK)
        setThemeColor("#005A9E")
        
        self.setup_ui()
        self.setup_connections()
        
        # Auto-save timer
        self.auto_save_timer = QTimer()
        self.auto_save_timer.timeout.connect(self.auto_save)
        self.auto_save_timer.start(30000)  # 30 saniyede bir kaydet
    
    def setup_ui(self):
        """Aray√ºz√º kur"""
        
        # Ana chat alanƒ± (ortada)
        chat_container = QWidget()
        chat_layout = QVBoxLayout(chat_container)
        chat_layout.setContentsMargins(0, 0, 0, 0)
        
        # Session paneli + Chat widget (split)
        main_splitter = QSplitter(Qt.Orientation.Horizontal)
        
        # Sol: Session paneli
        self.session_panel = SessionPanel(self.session_manager)
        self.session_panel.setMaximumWidth(350)
        main_splitter.addWidget(self.session_panel)
        
        # Orta: Chat widget
        self.chat_widget = ChatWidget(self.chat_manager)
        main_splitter.addWidget(self.chat_widget)
        
        # Split oranlarƒ±
        main_splitter.setStretchFactor(0, 1)
        main_splitter.setStretchFactor(1, 3)
        
        chat_layout.addWidget(main_splitter)
        
        # Ana sekme: Chat
        self.addSubInterface(
            chat_container,
            FluentIcon.CHAT,
            "Chat",
            NavigationItemPosition.TOP
        )
        
        # Belgeler
        self.doc_manager = DocumentManager(self.rag_engine)
        self.addSubInterface(
            self.doc_manager,
            FluentIcon.DOCUMENT,
            "Belgeler",
            NavigationItemPosition.TOP
        )
        
        # Prompt K√ºt√ºphanesi
        self.prompt_library = PromptLibrary()
        self.addSubInterface(
            self.prompt_library,
            FluentIcon.BOOK_SHELF,
            "Promptlar",
            NavigationItemPosition.TOP
        )
        
        # Analitik
        self.analytics_dashboard = AnalyticsDashboard(self.analytics)
        self.addSubInterface(
            self.analytics_dashboard,
            FluentIcon.CHART,
            "Analitik",
            NavigationItemPosition.TOP
        )
        
        # --- Alt navigasyon ---
        
        # Ses giri≈üi butonu
        self.navigationInterface.addItem(
            routeKey="voice",
            icon=FluentIcon.MICROPHONE,
            text="Ses Giri≈üi",
            onClick=self.toggle_voice_input,
            position=NavigationItemPosition.BOTTOM
        )
        
        # G√∂rsel analizi butonu
        self.navigationInterface.addItem(
            routeKey="vision",
            icon=FluentIcon.PHOTO,
            text="G√∂rsel",
            onClick=self.upload_image,
            position=NavigationItemPosition.BOTTOM
        )
        
        # Export/Import
        self.navigationInterface.addItem(
            routeKey="export",
            icon=FluentIcon.DOWNLOAD,
            text="Dƒ±≈üa Aktar",
            onClick=self.show_export_menu,
            position=NavigationItemPosition.BOTTOM
        )
        
        # Ayarlar
        self.navigationInterface.addItem(
            routeKey="settings",
            icon=FluentIcon.SETTING,
            text="Ayarlar",
            onClick=self.show_settings,
            position=NavigationItemPosition.BOTTOM
        )
        
        # Hakkƒ±nda
        self.navigationInterface.addItem(
            routeKey="about",
            icon=FluentIcon.INFO,
            text="Hakkƒ±nda",
            onClick=self.show_about,
            position=NavigationItemPosition.BOTTOM
        )
    
    def setup_connections(self):
        """Sinyalleri baƒüla"""
        # Session y√∂netimi
        self.session_panel.session_selected.connect(self.load_session)
        self.session_panel.new_session_requested.connect(self.create_new_session)
        
        # Prompt k√ºt√ºphanesi
        self.prompt_library.prompt_selected.connect(self.use_prompt)
        
        # Belge g√ºncellemeleri
        self.doc_manager.documents_updated.connect(self.on_documents_updated)
    
    def load_session(self, session_id: str):
        """Session y√ºkle"""
        self.session_manager.set_current_session(session_id)
        session = self.session_manager.get_session(session_id)
        
        if session:
            # Chat'i temizle
            self.chat_widget.clear_chat()
            
            # Mesajlarƒ± y√ºkle
            for msg in session.messages:
                is_user = msg['role'] == 'user'
                self.chat_widget.add_message(msg['content'], is_user)
            
            # Chat manager'ƒ±n ge√ßmi≈üini g√ºncelle
            self.chat_manager.conversation_history = session.messages.copy()
    
    def create_new_session(self):
        """Yeni session olu≈ütur"""
        session = self.session_manager.create_new_session()
        self.chat_widget.clear_chat()
        self.chat_manager.clear_history()
        self.session_panel.load_sessions()
        self.analytics.stats['sessions_created'] += 1
        self.analytics.save_statistics()
    
    def use_prompt(self, prompt_text: str):
        """Hazƒ±r prompt'u kullan"""
        # Chat input'una yaz
        self.chat_widget.input_field.setPlainText(prompt_text)
        self.chat_widget.input_field.setFocus()
        
        # Chat sekmesine ge√ß
        self.switchTo(self.chat_widget.parent())
    
    def toggle_voice_input(self):
        """Ses giri≈üini ba≈ülat/durdur"""
        from qfluentwidgets import InfoBar, InfoBarPosition
        
        if not self.voice_manager.recorder or not self.voice_manager.recorder.isRunning():
            # Kaydƒ± ba≈ülat
            recorder = self.voice_manager.start_recording()
            recorder.recording_stopped.connect(self.on_voice_recorded)
            
            InfoBar.info(
                title="Kayƒ±t Ba≈üladƒ±",
                content="Konu≈ümaya ba≈ülayabilirsiniz...",
                parent=self,
                position=InfoBarPosition.TOP,
                duration=2000
            )
        else:
            # Kaydƒ± durdur
            self.voice_manager.stop_recording()
    
    def on_voice_recorded(self, audio_path: str):
        """Ses kaydƒ± tamamlandƒ±ƒüƒ±nda"""
        from qfluentwidgets import InfoBar, InfoBarPosition
        
        try:
            # Transcribe et
            InfoBar.info(
                title="ƒ∞≈üleniyor",
                content="Ses metne d√∂n√º≈üt√ºr√ºl√ºyor...",
                parent=self,
                position=InfoBarPosition.TOP,
                duration=2000
            )
            
            text = self.voice_manager.transcribe_audio(audio_path)
            
            # Chat input'una yaz
            self.chat_widget.input_field.setPlainText(text)
            
            # Analytics kaydet
            import os
            from pydub import AudioSegment
            audio = AudioSegment.from_file(audio_path)
            duration = len(audio) / 1000.0
            self.analytics.record_voice_query(duration)
            
            InfoBar.success(
                title="Ba≈üarƒ±lƒ±",
                content="Ses metne d√∂n√º≈üt√ºr√ºld√º!",
                parent=self,
                position=InfoBarPosition.TOP,
                duration=2000
            )
            
        except Exception as e:
            MessageBox("Hata", f"Ses i≈üleme hatasƒ±: {str(e)}", self).exec()
    
    def upload_image(self):
        """G√∂rsel y√ºkle ve analiz et"""
        from PyQt6.QtWidgets import QFileDialog
        from qfluentwidgets import InfoBar, InfoBarPosition
        
        files, _ = QFileDialog.getOpenFileNames(
            self,
            "G√∂rsel Se√ß",
            "",
            "G√∂rseller (*.png *.jpg *.jpeg *.bmp *.gif)"
        )
        
        if not files:
            return
        
        try:
            if len(files) == 1:
                # Tek g√∂rsel
                prompt = "Bu g√∂rseli detaylƒ± analiz et."
                result = self.vision_manager.analyze_image(files[0], prompt)
            else:
                # √áoklu g√∂rsel
                prompt = "Bu g√∂rselleri kar≈üƒ±la≈ütƒ±r ve analiz et."
                result = self.vision_manager.analyze_multiple_images(files, prompt)
            
            # Sonucu chat'e ekle
            self.chat_widget.add_message(prompt, is_user=True)
            self.chat_widget.add_message(result, is_user=False)
            
            # Analytics
            self.analytics.record_image_query(len(files), 'auto')
            
            InfoBar.success(
                title="Analiz Tamamlandƒ±",
                content=f"{len(files)} g√∂rsel analiz edildi",
                parent=self,
                position=InfoBarPosition.TOP,
                duration=2000
            )
            
        except Exception as e:
            MessageBox("Hata", f"G√∂rsel analizi hatasƒ±: {str(e)}", self).exec()
    
    def show_export_menu(self):
        """Export/Import men√ºs√º"""
        from qfluentwidgets import RoundMenu, Action, MenuAnimationType
        from PyQt6.QtWidgets import QFileDialog
        from utils.export_manager import ExportManager
        
        menu = RoundMenu(parent=self)
        
        # Export se√ßenekleri
        export_full = Action(FluentIcon.SAVE, "Tam Yedekleme")
        export_full.triggered.connect(lambda: self.export_backup(True, True))
        
        export_sessions = Action(FluentIcon.HISTORY, "Sadece Konu≈ümalar")
        export_sessions.triggered.connect(lambda: self.export_backup(False, False))
        
        export_settings = Action(FluentIcon.SETTING, "Sadece Ayarlar")
        export_settings.triggered.connect(self.export_settings_only)
        
        menu.addAction(export_full)
        menu.addAction(export_sessions)
        menu.addAction(export_settings)
        menu.addSeparator()
        
        # Import
        import_action = Action(FluentIcon.UPLOAD, "ƒ∞√ße Aktar")
        import_action.triggered.connect(self.import_backup)
        menu.addAction(import_action)
        
        # Men√ºy√º g√∂ster
        cursor = self.cursor()
        menu.exec(cursor.pos())
    
    def export_backup(self, include_docs: bool, include_chroma: bool):
        """Yedekleme yap"""
        from qfluentwidgets import InfoBar, InfoBarPosition
        from utils.export_manager import ExportManager
        
        try:
            manager = ExportManager(self.config)
            backup_path = manager.export_full_backup(include_docs, include_chroma)
            
            InfoBar.success(
                title="Yedekleme Tamamlandƒ±",
                content=f"Yedek: {backup_path}",
                parent=self,
                position=InfoBarPosition.TOP,
                duration=3000
            )
        except Exception as e:
            MessageBox("Hata", f"Yedekleme hatasƒ±: {str(e)}", self).exec()
    
    def export_settings_only(self):
        """Sadece ayarlarƒ± dƒ±≈üa aktar"""
        from qfluentwidgets import InfoBar, InfoBarPosition
        from utils.export_manager import ExportManager
        
        try:
            manager = ExportManager(self.config)
            settings_path = manager.export_settings()
            
            if settings_path:
                InfoBar.success(
                    title="Ayarlar Dƒ±≈üa Aktarƒ±ldƒ±",
                    content=f"Dosya: {settings_path}",
                    parent=self,
                    position=InfoBarPosition.TOP,
                    duration=3000
                )
        except Exception as e:
            MessageBox("Hata", f"Export hatasƒ±: {str(e)}", self).exec()
    
    def import_backup(self):
        """Yedekleme i√ße aktar"""
        from PyQt6.QtWidgets import QFileDialog
        from utils.export_manager import ExportManager
        from qfluentwidgets import InfoBar, InfoBarPosition
        
        file_path, _ = QFileDialog.getOpenFileName(
            self,
            "Yedek Dosyasƒ± Se√ß",
            "",
            "ZIP Dosyalarƒ± (*.zip);;JSON Dosyalarƒ± (*.json)"
        )
        
        if not file_path:
            return
        
        try:
            manager = ExportManager(self.config)
            result = manager.import_full_backup(file_path, merge=False)
            
            if result.get('requires_confirmation'):
                # Onay iste
                confirm = MessageBox(
                    "Dikkat",
                    result['warning'] + "\n\nDevam etmek istiyor musunuz?",
                    self
                ).exec()
                
                if confirm:
                    result = manager.import_full_backup(file_path, merge=False)
            
            if result.get('success'):
                InfoBar.success(
                    title="ƒ∞√ße Aktarma Tamamlandƒ±",
                    content=f"ƒ∞√ße aktarƒ±ldƒ±: {result['imported']}",
                    parent=self,
                    position=InfoBarPosition.TOP,
                    duration=3000
                )
                
                # Yeniden y√ºkle
                self.session_panel.load_sessions()
                self.doc_manager.load_documents()
        
        except Exception as e:
            MessageBox("Hata", f"ƒ∞√ße aktarma hatasƒ±: {str(e)}", self).exec()
    
    def show_settings(self):
        """Ayarlar dialog'u"""
        dialog = SettingsDialog(self.config, self)
        dialog.settings_changed.connect(self.on_settings_changed)
        dialog.exec()
    
    def on_settings_changed(self, updates):
        """Ayarlar deƒüi≈ütiƒüinde"""
        from qfluentwidgets import InfoBar, InfoBarPosition
        
        # Yeniden ba≈ülat
        self.chat_manager.initialize()
        self.rag_engine.initialize()
        
        InfoBar.success(
            title="Ba≈üarƒ±lƒ±",
            content="Ayarlar g√ºncellendi!",
            parent=self,
            position=InfoBarPosition.TOP,
            duration=2000
        )
    
    def on_documents_updated(self):
        """Belgeler g√ºncellendiƒüinde"""
        # Analytics'i g√ºncelle
        count = self.rag_engine.get_document_count()
        self.analytics.stats['documents_added'] = count
        self.analytics.save_statistics()
    
    def auto_save(self):
        """Otomatik kayƒ±t"""
        # Aktif session'ƒ± kaydet
        if self.session_manager.current_session:
            current = self.session_manager.current_session
            current.messages = self.chat_manager.conversation_history.copy()
            self.session_manager.save_session(current)
    
    def show_about(self):
        """Hakkƒ±nda"""
        MessageBox(
            "RAG Chatbot v2.0 Pro",
            "üöÄ **Profesyonel RAG Chatbot Uygulamasƒ±**\n\n"
            "**Yeni √ñzellikler:**\n"
            "‚úÖ √áoklu konu≈üma oturumlarƒ±\n"
            "‚úÖ Ses giri≈üi/√ßƒ±kƒ±≈üƒ± (Whisper + TTS)\n"
            "‚úÖ G√∂rsel analizi (GPT-4 Vision)\n"
            "‚úÖ Hazƒ±r prompt k√ºt√ºphanesi\n"
            "‚úÖ Geli≈ümi≈ü analitik dashboard\n"
            "‚úÖ Export/Import sistemi\n"
            "‚úÖ Plugin desteƒüi\n"
            "‚úÖ Token & maliyet takibi\n"
            "‚úÖ Markdown rendering\n"
            "‚úÖ Kod √ßalƒ±≈ütƒ±rma\n\n"
            "¬© 2024 RAG Chatbot Team",
            self
        ).exec()
    
    def closeEvent(self, event):
        """Pencere kapatƒ±lƒ±rken"""
        # Son kayƒ±t
        self.auto_save()
        event.accept()
```

### 1Ô∏è‚É£5Ô∏è‚É£ `main.py` - G√ºncellenmi≈ü Ana Dosya (v2)

```python name=main_v2.py
import sys
from PyQt6.QtWidgets import QApplication
from PyQt6.QtCore import Qt
from core.config import Config
from core.rag_engine import RAGEngine
from core.chat_manager import ChatManager
from core.session_manager import SessionManager
from core.analytics import Analytics
from core.voice_manager import VoiceManager
from core.vision_manager import VisionManager
from ui.main_window_v2 import MainWindowV2

def main():
    """Ana fonksiyon"""
    
    # High DPI desteƒüi
    QApplication.setHighDpiScaleFactorRoundingPolicy(
        Qt.HighDpiScaleFactorRoundingPolicy.PassThrough
    )
    QApplication.setAttribute(Qt.ApplicationAttribute.AA_EnableHighDpiScaling)
    QApplication.setAttribute(Qt.ApplicationAttribute.AA_UseHighDpiPixmaps)
    
    app = QApplication(sys.argv)
    app.setApplicationName("RAG Chatbot v2.0 Pro")
    app.setOrganizationName("RAG Chatbot Team")
    
    # Splash screen (opsiyonel)
    from qfluentwidgets import SplashScreen
    from PyQt6.QtGui import QPixmap, QIcon
    
    # Konfig√ºrasyon
    config = Config()
    
    # Core mod√ºller
    rag_engine = RAGEngine(config)
    chat_manager = ChatManager(config, rag_engine)
    session_manager = SessionManager(config)
    analytics = Analytics(config)
    voice_manager = VoiceManager(config)
    vision_manager = VisionManager(config)
    
    # Ana pencere
    window = MainWindowV2(
        config=config,
        chat_manager=chat_manager,
        rag_engine=rag_engine,
        session_manager=session_manager,
        analytics=analytics,
        voice_manager=voice_manager,
        vision_manager=vision_manager
    )
    
    window.show()
    
    sys.exit(app.exec())

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```
